  8. 08
    多尺度 GNN 学习晶体热电输运#
    Learning Thermoelectric Transport from Crystal Structures via Multiscale Graph Neural Network#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 材料 / 器件📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 Yuxuan Zeng, Wei Cao, Yijing Zuo, Fang Lyu, Wenhao Xie, Tan Peng, Yue Hou, Ling Miao, Ziyu Wang, Jing Shi🔥 AI 1

    💡 亮点：从晶体结构直接预测热电输运。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题如何仅从无机晶体结构与条件信息中，快速、准确预测热电电子输运系数 S、σ/τ、κe/τ，弥补传统实验/DFT筛选成本高、化学式模型看不见晶体拓扑、通用晶体GNN不适配热电输运的问题。
    创新方法提出 TECSA-GNN：把晶体画成四尺度多图，同时编码全局化学统计 U、原子节点 V、键 E、键角 Θ；用周期 k-NN 建图、RBF 展开键长/键角，并通过“键角 Θ → 键 E → 原子 V”的层级消息传递和线图角度聚合，让局部畸变、键角耦合、全局组成、掺杂类型/浓度、温度与带隙共同参与热电输运预测。
    工作流程输入晶体结构、化学式、温度、n/p 掺杂类型、掺杂浓度和带隙 Eg；先用周期 k-NN 连接每个原子近邻并提取键长、键角；再将原子、键、角特征投影到统一隐空间，在线图中用键角更新键，在原子图中用注意力聚合更新原子；随后对节点和边做均值池化，并与全局化学统计描述符拼接；最后由回归头输出 S、log(σ/τ)、log(κe/τ)，再用于 Materials Project 高通量筛选、DFT 验证和能带/PDOS/ELF 机制解释。
    关键结果TECSA-GNN 在热电基准数据上达到 SOTA，在 600/900 K、n/p 型、n=10¹⁹ cm⁻³ 条件下普遍取得最低 MAE；例如 600 K p 型 Seebeck 系数 MAE 为 54.333 μV/K，明显优于 CraLiGNN 的 79.79 μV/K；900 K n 型 log(σ/τ) MAE 为 0.261，优于 CraLiGNN 的 0.429；t-SNE 显示模型嵌入能区分晶系和 n/p 型；冻结图卷积层、只微调回归头约 50 epochs 即可降低 FH、HH、RS、ZB 特殊结构离群误差。
    应用价值可作为热电材料发现的快速预筛选引擎，把庞大的 Materials Project 晶体库压缩为少量高潜力候选，并与 DFT 形成“AI筛选—量子验证—机制解释”闭环；识别 NaTlSe₂、Te₃As₂、LiMgSb 等候选，其中 Te₃As₂ 属高电导高 PF 型，NaTlSe₂ 属高 S、低 σ、低 κe 型，LiMgSb 显示 Sb/Mg-Sb 子晶格主导输运，为低成本发现和解释新型热电半导体提供工具。

    第一部分：核心概览

    提出 TECSA-GNN，以全局化学统计、原子、键、键角四尺度图表示直接学习无机晶体的热电电子输运系数 S、σ/τ、κe/τ。模型在热电基准数据上显著优于 CrabNet、CGCNN、ALIGNN、CraLiGNN 等，尤其在 600/900 K、n/p 型条件下取得最低 MAE。结合 Materials Project 高通量筛选与 DFT 验证，识别 NaTlSe₂、Te₃As₂、LiMgSb 等候选材料，并通过 t-SNE、敏感性分析、能带与 PDOS 解释输运来源，体现了面向热电材料发现的任务特异性 GNN 设计价值。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Learning Thermoelectric Transport from Crystal Structures via Multiscale Graph Neural Network》（None，）

    背景

    热电材料通过 Seebeck effect 实现热-电转换，性能由 S、σ、κ 共同决定。传统实验和 ab initio 筛选成本高、周期长；既有机器学习方法常依赖化学式或经验描述符，难以充分表达晶体拓扑、键角、局域畸变等结构因素。

    方法

    构建 TECSA-GNN，将晶体表示为包含 global descriptors U、atomic features V、bond features E、angular features Θ 的多尺度图。采用周期性 k-NN，k = 8 建图，使用 RBF 展开键长与键角，通过 Θ → E → V 的层级消息传递、注意力聚合、线图角度更新和均值池化完成输运系数预测。

    结果

    模型在 Seebeck coefficient、log(σ/τ)、log(κe/τ) 三个任务上达到 SOTA。以 n = 10¹⁹ cm⁻³、600/900 K 为基准，TECSA-GNN 的 MAE 显著低于 CrabNet、CGCNN、GeoCGNN、ALIGNN、CraLiGNN，例如 600 K p 型 S 的 MAE 为 54.333 μV/K，优于 CraLiGNN 的 79.79 μV/K。

    讨论

    t-SNE 表明模型嵌入可区分晶系、相近晶系邻近分布，并呈现 n/p 型近似镜像对称。特殊结构 FH、HH、RS、ZB 上冻结图卷积层、仅微调回归头约 50 epochs 即可降低离群误差，说明预训练结构表示具有可迁移性。

    局限

    模型依赖数据集中提供的 band gap Eg；完全未知材料通常没有 Eg，需要用预训练模型预测 Êg 替代。σ/τ 与 κe/τ 受弛豫时间 τ 近似影响，误差高于 S。复杂架构不适合所有任务，在 Eg、Ef 预测上不如 ALIGNN。

    结论

    多尺度、任务特异性 GNN 能有效学习热电电子输运规律，并可与 DFT 结合进行高通量筛选。Te₃As₂ 的高 PF 主要来自高电导，NaTlSe₂ 呈现高 S、低 σ、低 κe 特征，LiMgSb 的输运由 Sb/Mg-Sb 子晶格主导。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析

    Abstract

    Multiscale graph learning targets thermoelectric transport

    核心贡献是面向无机热电晶体电子输运系数估计的 GNN，而不是通用晶体性质预测模型。摘要明确指出 GNN 适合晶体表示学习：*"Graph neural networks (GNNs) are designed to extract latent patterns from graph-structured data, making them particularly well suited for crystal representation learning."* 任务对象限定为 electronic transport coefficients，即热电材料中与载流子输运相关的 S、σ/τ、κe/τ。

    Global-atomic-bond-angular representation forms the architectural core

    模型的独特性来自四尺度编码：*"The model encodes crystal structures and physicochemical properties in a multiscale manner, encompassing global, atomic, bond, and angular levels."* 这意味着模型不只看化学组成，也不只看原子邻接，而是同时纳入晶体全局统计性质、原子位点、化学键、键角几何。

    Benchmark performance and extrapolation are central claims

    摘要给出的性能定位是 state-of-the-art 与外推能力：*"It achieves state-of-the-art performance on benchmark datasets with remarkable extrapolative capability."* 外推能力并非只靠随机测试集验证，还包括后文对特殊结构 Full-Heusler、Half-Heusler、rocksalt、zinc blende 的遮蔽、微调与测试。

    DFT coupling enables candidate discovery and mechanistic interpretation

    模型不仅用于预测，还与 ab initio calculations 结合筛选材料：*"By combining the proposed GNN with ab initio calculations, we successfully identify compounds exhibiting outstanding electronic transport properties"*。后续 DFT 验证集中于 NaTlSe₂、Te₃As₂、LiMgSb，并使用能带、PDOS、ELF 追踪输运行为来源。

    ---

    I Introduction

    Thermoelectric performance is governed by coupled electronic and thermal transport

    热电材料通过温差驱动载流子运动产生电势差：*"TE materials convert temperature gradients into electrical potential differences by driving carrier transport via the Seebeck effect."* 性能指标由 Seebeck coefficient S、电导率 σ、热导率 κ 共同决定，并由无量纲优值表示为 zT = S²σT/κ；电子输运能力还可单独用 PF = S²σ 衡量。

    Thermal conductivity contains electronic and phononic components

    热导率分解为 κ = κe + κph，并且两者受不同散射机制控制：*"The thermal transport in TE materials involves the combined contributions of both electronic and phononic carriers, i.e., κ = κe + κph."* 这解释了为什么仅预测电子输运仍不能完整判断 zT，但对高通量预筛选具有直接价值。

    Traditional discovery routes are limited by cost and combinatorial complexity

    热电输运机制复杂，元素和结构组合近乎无限，传统试错实验与 ab initio 计算面临高成本和长周期：*"traditional trial-and-error experimentation and ab initio computations... face significant challenges like high costs and long development cycles."* 因而需要更高效的计算模型识别候选材料。

    Formula-only models miss crystal topology

    既有 ML 方法常依赖化学式或经验描述符：*"Existing approaches either rely solely on chemical formulas or employ empirical descriptors."* 化学式特征容易构建，但无法表达拓扑差异；典型例子是 diamond 与 graphite 同为 “C” 却性质截然不同：*"diamond is an insulator, while graphite is a good conductor."*

    Structural representation is indispensable for thermoelectric tuning

    晶格畸变是调控热电输运的重要手段：*"Since lattice distortion serves as an important strategy in tuning TE transport, structural representations are therefore indispensable."* 这将模型设计从“成分学习”推向“结构感知学习”。

    Generic crystal GNNs are not automatically optimal for thermoelectric transport

    CGCNN 之后的晶体 GNN 在 formation energy、band gap、bulk modulus 等任务上可达 ab initio 级准确性，但热电输运预测表现不稳定：*"they often underperform in TE transport prediction, sometimes even lagging behind formula-based models."* 这被归结为 No Free Lunch theorem，即没有一种模型在所有任务上最优。

    Task-specific physics-guided design is required

    热电输运学习不能简单套用标准 GNN：*"learning TE transport also requires incorporating physics-guided design, rather than simply applying standard baseline models."* 该逻辑支撑了 TECSA-GNN 加入 global descriptors、bond angles、local structural distortions 的必要性。

    Global descriptors complement structural graph features

    方法核心是将结构图特征与化学统计特征耦合：*"Beyond the commonly adopted atomic, bond, and angular features, we further incorporate global crystal-level descriptors to capture overarching physicochemical characteristics of the structure."* 这种设计试图同时利用公式级统计规律与晶体拓扑信息。

    ---

    II Results

    II.1 Crystal graph representation and network architecture design

    Crystal graph is extended from nodes and edges to angles and global descriptors

    基础图定义为 G = (V, E)：*"An undirected graph 𝒢 consists of node vectors V and edge vectors E."* 但热电输运对键角和局部畸变敏感，因此引入角度尺度 Θ：*"complex properties, including TE transport, are sensitive to structural variations such as bond angles and local geometric distortions."*

    Formula-derived global descriptors provide interpretable physicochemical statistics

    全局晶体级描述符 U 来自化学式及其统计特征：*"global physicochemical properties of the crystal and their statistics (denoted as U) can achieve reliable accuracy and possess interpretable physical meaning."* 这些描述符本身缺少结构表达，因此需要与 (V, E, Θ) 耦合。

    TECSA-GNN uses a four-level crystal representation

    晶体被表示为多图：𝒢 = U, Vi, Eij, Θjik。原文定义为：*"The model represents a crystal as a multigraph, 𝒢 = U, Vi, Eij, Θjik."* 其中 Vi 是原子特征，Eij 是键特征，Θjik 是以原子 i 为中心的键角特征，U 是全局晶体级描述符。

    Periodic k-nearest-neighbor construction balances accuracy and efficiency

    建图采用周期性 k-NN，每个原胞原子与最近邻连接：*"we adopt a periodic k-nearest neighbors (k-NN) scheme."* 实际设定为 k = 8：*"In practice, we set k = 8; smaller values may lead to information loss, whereas larger values significantly increase computational cost."* 多轮卷积允许远距离信息传播，因此 k = 8 不等于限制感受野。

    Distance and angle features are expanded by radial basis functions

    键长与键角使用 RBF 展开：*"Bond lengths and bond angles are expanded using radial basis functions (RBF)."* 这样连续几何量可转化为神经网络更易处理的高维平滑特征。

    Heterogeneous features are projected into a shared latent space

    原子、键、角特征通过独立 MLP 对齐维度：*"we first align their dimensionalities by projecting atomic, bond, and angular features into a shared latent space using independent MLPs."* 每个 MLP 包含线性变换、layer normalization 和 ReLU activation，公式中给出 Ṽi、Ẽij、Θ̃jik 的投影过程。

    Pooling combines learned structural embeddings with global descriptors

    图级表示通过节点与边均值池化得到 V̄、Ē，再与全局描述符 U 拼接：*"the pooled embeddings are concatenated with the global descriptor U."* 最终图向量 h𝒢 输入回归网络输出单一输运系数 ŷ ∈ ℝ¹。

    Hierarchical message passing follows angular-to-bond-to-atom information flow

    消息传递顺序为 Θ → E → V：*"Hierarchical message passing proceeds in the order Θ → E → V."* 这体现了几何角度先更新键，再由键影响原子嵌入的物理层级：角度影响局部配位与键耦合，键再影响原子环境。

    Node updates use attention-weighted neighbor aggregation

    边消息由中心原子、邻居原子和边嵌入拼接得到：*"the edge message is constructed as mi←j."* 注意力系数定义为 αij = wᵀmi←j，节点更新使用 softmax 归一化权重聚合邻居信息：*"Node embeddings are updated via normalized attention aggregation."*

    Angular coupling is modeled on the line graph

    相邻键 (i,j) 与 (i,k) 共享中心原子 i，构成角三元组：*"To model angular coupling, message passing is performed on the line graph."* 角消息 rjik 由两条边和角特征拼接后生成，键嵌入通过线图聚合更新：*"Bond embeddings are updated via line-graph aggregation."*

    Graph extraction relies on pymatgen

    局部键和角关系由 pymatgen 工具包提取：*"Bonding and angular relations are extracted using the pymatgen toolkit."* 这保证了周期晶体结构解析与邻接关系构建的标准化。

    ---

    II.2 Quantitative evaluation, unsupervised learning and fine-tuning

    Regression targets are S, σ/τ, and κe/τ

    TECSA-GNN 被定义为从晶体图到热电输运量的可学习映射：*"TECSA-GNN may be regarded as a learnable function whose task is to map a crystal graph 𝒢 onto a quantitative descriptor of TE transport."* 目标集合为 𝒴 = S, σ/τ, κe/τ，覆盖 Seebeck 系数、电导率除弛豫时间、电子热导率除弛豫时间。

    Training minimizes mean squared error

    回归损失采用 MSE：*"we adopt the mean squared error (MSE)."* 公式为 L = 1/NB Σ(yi − ŷi)²，其中 NB 是 mini-batch 样本数并作为超参数。

    Doping information and band gap enter the global feature vector

    掺杂类型与浓度拼接进全局特征 U：*"the doping type and concentration of the material are concatenated with the global feature vector U."* Eg 也直接加入 U：*"the band gap Eg... is directly provided by the dataset and likewise incorporated into U."*

    Unseen-material prediction requires surrogate band gaps

    完全未知材料通常没有 Eg：*"for entirely unseen materials, Eg is typically unavailable."* 实用方案是调用 SOTA 预训练模型从晶体结构预测 Êg：*"with the estimated value Êg serving as a surrogate."* 该点是高通量应用中的关键依赖。

    Log transformation addresses skewed σ/τ and κe/τ distributions

    模型预测 log(σ/τ) 和 log(κe/τ) 而非原始值：*"we model log(σ/τ) and log(κe/τ) instead of σ/τ and κe/τ themselves to alleviate skewness arising from their wide-ranging distribution."* 这属于数值稳定和分布归一化处理。

    10-fold cross-validation prevents material-level leakage

    评估采用 10-fold cross-validation：*"We employed 10-fold cross-validation to evaluate the predictive performance of the model."* 为防止数据泄漏，同一材料在不同掺杂条件下的所有条目被分配到同一子集：*"all entries corresponding to the same material under different doping conditions were consistently assigned to the same subset."*

    S is easier to predict than σ/τ and κe/τ

    预测误差中 S 最小：*"the prediction error for S is the smallest among the three targets."* log(σ/τ) 与 log(κe/τ) 误差相近，主要受弛豫时间 τ 近似影响：*"largely reflecting the approximation inherent in τ."*

    Generalization is strong for S and mildly underfit for transport-rate quantities

    训练与测试损失在 S 上接近：*"LTrain and LTest for S are closely aligned, indicative of robust generalisation."* 对 log(σ/τ) 与 log(κe/τ) 存在轻微欠拟合：*"Slight underfitting is observed for log(σ/τ) and log(κe/τ)."*

    Unified architecture handles all three transport targets

    TECSA-GNN 的优势在于无需为不同目标修改结构：*"The principal advantage of TECSA-GNN lies in its unified architecture, which accommodates the simultaneous learning of S, σ/τ, κe/τ without necessitating task-specific adjustments."*

    Benchmark shows SOTA performance for thermoelectric properties

    在 n = 10¹⁹ cm⁻³，600 K 与 900 K，n/p 型分别评估。表中 TECSA-GNN 全部热电输运任务均为最低 MAE。例如：

    • 600 K n 型 S：TECSA-GNN 60.686 μV/K，CraLiGNN 74.645，ALIGNN 84.267。
    • 600 K p 型 S：TECSA-GNN 54.333 μV/K，CraLiGNN 79.79。
    • 900 K n 型 log(σ/τ)：TECSA-GNN 0.261，CraLiGNN 0.429。
    • 900 K p 型 log(κe/τ)：TECSA-GNN 0.319，CraLiGNN 0.449。

    对应原文定位为：*"TECSA-GNN achieves SOTA performance in predicting TE properties."*

    CrabNet is composition-only, whereas other baselines are structure-aware GNNs

    基准模型中仅 CrabNet 纯化学组成建模：*"only CrabNet characterises materials purely in terms of their chemical compositions, whereas all others are GNNs that exploit structural descriptors."* TECSA-GNN 优势来自结构编码与物理化学统计特征结合：*"attributable to its comprehensive encoding of crystal structures together with the incorporation of physicochemical statistical features."*

    No Free Lunch remains valid for TECSA-GNN

    TECSA-GNN 不适合所有材料性质预测：*"It is worth emphasising that the No Free Lunch theorem applies equally to TECSA-GNN."* 在 Eg 和 Ef 预测中表现不突出：TECSA-GNN 的 Eg MAE = 0.397 eV，低于 ALIGNN 的 0.224 eV；Ef MAE = 0.054 eV/atom，低于 ALIGNN 的 0.022 eV/atom。

    Overparameterization can hurt simple tasks

    复杂架构在相对简单任务中可能过拟合噪声：*"for relatively simple tasks, an excessive number of parameters risks capturing spurious noise within the data, thereby impairing generalisation."* 这说明热电输运任务需要复杂多尺度结构，但 Eg/Ef 可能由较简单结构描述符即可学习。

    Occam’s razor explains why more features are not always better

    能量相关任务中，结构描述符可能足够：*"for energy prediction tasks, structural descriptors alone may suffice."* 复杂度选择需匹配物理任务：*"The choice of architectural complexity should therefore be made with due consideration of the physical context."*

    t-SNE embeddings encode crystal-system structure

    用预训练 S 模型输出前最后一层 MLP 激活作为样本表示：*"we extract the activations from the final fully connected MLP layer preceding the output node."* t-SNE 显示三点：同晶系形成连续相邻簇，相似晶系邻近，n/p 型近似对称。原文概括为：*"samples of the same system form continuous and adjoining clusters"*，以及 *"structurally similar systems... appear in close proximity."*

    Embedding symmetry reflects doping-type separation

    t-SNE 水平轴可能编码掺杂类型：*"the horizontal axis encodes the qualitative separation of doping type, with n-type materials on the left and p-type on the right."* 上方区域少数样本出现与标称掺杂相反的 S 值，可能与双极传导有关：*"may be associated with bipolar conduction phenomena."*

    Fine-tuning tests extrapolation to masked special structures

    特殊结构集合包含 133 个样本，覆盖 Full-Heusler (FH)、Half-Heusler (HH)、rocksalt (RS)、zinc blende (ZB)：*"a total of 133 special structures... were considered."* 这些样本与预训练不同，被均分为训练和测试子集：*"these samples were evenly divided into training and testing subsets."*

    Frozen feature extractors and fine-tuned regression head improve efficiency

    微调时冻结维度对齐 MLP 与所有 GConv 层，仅更新末端回归头：*"the MLPs used for dimensional alignment and all GConv layers were kept frozen, and only the terminal regression head was fine-tuned."* 约 50 epochs 即取得明显提升：*"requiring only ∼50 epochs in our case to achieve substantial accuracy gains."*

    Fine-tuning mainly reduces outlier errors

    微调优势包括降低特殊结构预测离群误差和避免从头训练成本：*"it selectively improves predictions for these special structures, most notably by reducing outlier errors."* 跨不同样本量数据集比较时，MAE 比 R² 更可靠：*"Across datasets of unequal size, MAE is a more dependable metric."*

    ---

    II.3 Discovering potential thermoelectric materials

    Materials Project screening uses pretrained TECSA-GNN

    预训练 TECSA-GNN 用于未标注材料筛选：*"Leveraging the pretrained TECSA-GNN model, we screened unlabeled data to identify promising candidates with potentially high PF values."* 数据源为 Materials Project，其提供晶体结构和 DFT 计算带隙：*"The Materials Project provides a vast repository of crystal structures along with DFT-computed band gaps."*

    Candidate filtering imposes semiconducting and computational simplicity constraints

    筛选条件为：

    • 0 < Eg < 1.5 eV
    • nonmagnetic
    • free of transition metals
    • nₛᵢₜₑₛ < 20

    原文列为：*"0 < Eg < 1.5 [eV], nonmagnetic, free of transition metals, and fewer than 20 atomic sites in the unit cell."* 第一条保证半导体范围，后三条主要简化 DFT 验证计算。

    Three candidates are validated by DFT at 300 K

    去除训练集中已有材料后，对三种候选进行 DFT 验证：*"we conducted DFT validations on three promising candidates at 300 K: [mp-1209957] NaTlSe2, [mp-9897] Te3As2 and [mp-1207082] LiMgSb."*

    NaTlSe₂ extends prior formula-only identification to structure-level evaluation

    NaTlSe₂ 曾由公式模型报告，但分析只限化学式：*"NaTlSe2 was previously reported by Ref. [6], albeit with analysis limited to its chemical formula."* TECSA-GNN 提供晶体结构级评价：*"our GNN-based approach enables structural evaluation at the crystal level."*

    PF thresholds define qualitatively high room-temperature electronic performance

    300 K 下，高 PF 参考阈值包括：

    • p 型 SnSe：6.8 × 10⁻⁴ W/m/K²
    • n 型 Sc₀.₀₁₅Mg₃.₁₈₅Sb₁.₅Bi₀.₄₇Te₀.₀₃：8 × 10⁻⁴ W/m/K²

    原文表述为：*"a PF exceeding 6.8 × 10−4 [W/m/K2]... or 8 × 10−4 [W/m/K2]... can be considered qualitatively high at 300 K."*

    Electronic thermal conductivity remains below 1 W/m/K across considered doping range

    候选材料 κe 在考虑掺杂范围内低于 1 W/m/K：*"the κe of the candidates remains below 1 [W/m/K] across the considered doping range."* 但这不代表总热导低，因为 κph 通常主导：*"κph is typically the dominant contribution to heat transport."*

    TECSA-GNN agrees well with DFT, especially for S

    模型与 DFT 整体一致，尤其 S：*"TECSA-GNN shows good agreement with DFT calculations, particularly in the estimation of S."* σ/τ 与 κe/τ 稍差，原因仍是 τ 近似：*"the dataset’s approximation of the relaxation time τ inevitably introduces some uncertainty."*

    High-throughput value outweighs imperfect ab initio-level accuracy

    尽管存在误差，预训练 AI 相比 ab initio 更适合大规模筛选：*"the efficiency of a pretrained AI model compared with ab initio calculations makes it highly practical for high-throughput screening of new materials."* 价值在于快速覆盖庞大未知成分-结构空间：*"rapid identification of promising candidates across vast, unexplored regions of compositional and structural space."*

    ---

    II.4 Tracing thermoelectric behaviour from DFT insights

    DFT validation alone is insufficient to declare valuable materials

    候选材料不能仅凭 DFT 输运验证直接定义为“有价值”：*"it is still premature to classify them directly as 'valuable materials' solely on the basis of the DFT validation results."* 更高保真理论计算仍然必要：*"more rigorous evidence can be obtained through higher-fidelity theoretical calculations."*

    Band structures and ELF are used to trace performance origins

    对候选材料计算 band structures 与 electron localization functions (ELF)：*"we performed DFT calculations of their band structures and electron localization functions (ELF) to trace the origin of their TE performance."* 该步骤将机器学习筛选结果转化为物理可解释机制。

    Te₃As₂ is a narrow-gap, high-conductivity PF candidate

    Te₃As₂ 的 CBM 与 VBM 均接近费米能级：*"both the conduction band minimum (CBM) and the valence band maximum (VBM) are located near EFermi, indicating a small Eg and a narrow-gap character."* 费米能级附近色散明显，说明有效质量小：*"The pronounced band dispersion around EFermi further implies a small m*."*

    Mott formula links Seebeck coefficient to conductivity-energy gradient

    Seebeck 系数由 Mott 公式描述：*"S is closely related to the energy-dependent gradients of the density of states and scattering strength."* 公式为 S = π²kB²T/(3e) · d ln σ(E)/dE |E=EFermi。当 N(E) 与 v(E) 变化平缓时，d ln σ(E)/dE 小，导致 S 较低。

    Te₃As₂ high PF originates from high σ rather than high S

    Te₃As₂ 的高 PF 来源是异常高电导：*"the excellent PF of Te3As2 arises from its exceptionally high σ, consistent with its narrow-gap nature."* 同时其 κe/τ 明显大于 LiMgSb 和 NaTlSe₂：*"Te3As2 exhibits a markedly larger κe/τ than LiMgSb and NaTlSe2."*

    LiMgSb and NaTlSe₂ share p-type-favorable valence-band features

    LiMgSb 与 NaTlSe₂ 的 VBM 靠近费米能级：*"The VBM lies close to EFermi, indicating hole-dominated conduction under intrinsic or lightly acceptor-doped conditions."* 这与 p 型热电材料通常更易取得高 PF 的趋势一致：*"p-type TE materials usually achieve higher PF values."*

    Alkali cations act as electrostatic charge balancers

    LiMgSb 中 Li、NaTlSe₂ 中 Na 在带边附近 PDOS 近零：*"the projected density of states (PDOS) of Li in LiMgSb and Na in NaTlSe2 is nearly zero."* 因而主要作为电荷平衡离子：*"these ions mainly act as electrostatic charge balancers rather than active contributors to transport."*

    Na layers tune Tl-Se framework and hybridization

    Na 层稳定 Tl-Se 骨架并调控 Tl-Se 键几何：*"The Na layers stabilize the Tl-Se framework and influence the geometry of Tl-Se bonds."* 这进一步影响 d-p hybridization 与 VBM 位置：*"thereby tuning the d-p hybridization strength and the position of the VBM."*

    NaTlSe₂ is high-S, low-σ, low-κe

    NaTlSe₂ 价带较平，带来大有效质量和低迁移率：*"The valence bands of NaTlSe2 are relatively flat, leading to large carrier effective masses and low mobility, and hence low σ."* 但 DOS 在费米能级附近陡变，提升 S：*"the steep variation of the DOS near EFermi yields a large d ln σ(E)/dE and thus a high S."* 整体表现为：*"NaTlSe2 represents a system characterized by high S, low σ, and low κe."*

    LiMgSb transport is sublattice-selective

    Li 在价带和导带附近贡献可忽略：*"Li ion acting mainly as an electrostatic stabilizer."* 价带由 Sb-d orbitals 主导，导带由 Mg-d character 主导：*"The valence bands are dominated by Sb-d orbitals, while the conduction bands are primarily Mg-d in character."* 因而空穴输运由 Sb 子晶格控制，电子输运主要发生在 Mg-Sb 框架：*"hole transport is governed by the Sb sublattice and electron transport occurs mainly within the Mg-Sb framework."*

    LiMgSb dispersive valence bands favor high mobility and high σ

    LiMgSb 的强色散价带意味着小有效质量：*"The strongly dispersive valence bands in LiMgSb indicate small m*."* 根据 μ ∝ 1/m*，小有效质量导致高迁移率与高电导：*"lead to high carrier mobility and thus high σ."*

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持

    1. 术语解析

    #### Extrapolative capability

    学术含义不是普通测试集准确率，而是对训练集中未充分覆盖结构类型或分布外材料的泛化能力。语境中对应特殊结构遮蔽实验：FH、HH、RS、ZB 在预训练中被 mask，随后只微调回归头测试。*"remarkable extrapolative capability"* 强调模型学到的是可迁移结构表示，而非只记忆训练分布。

    #### Physicochemical statistical descriptors

    指由化学组成推导的全局统计特征，例如元素属性的均值、方差、最大值、最小值等。与局部结构图不同，这类特征表达的是材料整体化学倾向。语境中 U 是全局输入，*"global physicochemical properties of the crystal and their statistics"* 既提供可解释性，也弥补结构图难以直接捕捉的组成规律。

    #### Line graph aggregation

    普通图中节点是原子、边是键；线图中“键”变成节点，两个共享原子的键之间通过键角相连。因此键角信息可通过线图消息传递影响键嵌入。语境中用于实现 Θ → E：*"To model angular coupling, message passing is performed on the line graph."*

    #### Bipolar conduction

    热电半导体中电子和空穴同时参与输运，可能导致 Seebeck 系数符号或大小偏离简单 n/p 型预期。t-SNE 中部分样本的 S 与标称掺杂类型相反，被解释为可能存在双极传导：*"may be associated with bipolar conduction phenomena."*

    #### No Free Lunch theorem

    在机器学习中表示不存在对所有任务都最优的模型。语境中 TECSA-GNN 在热电输运上优异，但在 Eg、Ef 上不如 ALIGNN，说明复杂多尺度架构必须服务于具体物理任务，而非盲目增加特征与参数。

    ---

    2. 疑难查证

    #### 为什么热电输运比 Eg 或 Ef 更需要多尺度结构？

    Eg 和 Ef 多数情况下主要由局部键合、元素种类、晶体对称性决定，结构图的原子-键-角信息往往足够。热电输运则更复杂，因为 S、σ、κe 同时依赖：

    • 能带曲率，即有效质量 m*
    • 费米能级附近 DOS 梯度
    • 载流子速度 v(E)
    • 弛豫时间 τ(E)
    • 掺杂类型与浓度
    • 温度
    • 局部畸变、键角、轨道杂化
    • 全局化学组成规律

    因此 TECSA-GNN 同时引入 U、V、E、Θ。如果只用结构图，可能缺少组成统计规律；如果只用化学式，则丢失拓扑与局部几何。

    #### 为什么 S 的预测误差小于 σ/τ 和 κe/τ？

    S 对弛豫时间的绝对值不如 σ 和 κe 敏感。在常弛豫时间近似下，σ/τ 与 κe/τ 的真实值仍隐含复杂散射机制，数据标签本身存在近似误差。S 更接近能带形状和 DOS 梯度决定的量，因此模型更容易从结构和组成中学习。

    #### 为什么高 PF 不一定意味着高 zT？

    PF = S²σ 只衡量电子输运中的发电能力，不包含总热导 κ = κe + κph。即使 PF 高，如果晶格热导 κph 很高，zT = S²σT/κ 仍可能不高。因此 Te₃As₂、NaTlSe₂、LiMgSb 只能被视为电子输运潜力候选，还需要更高保真声子热导、缺陷散射、稳定性等验证。

    #### 为什么 NaTlSe₂ 的高 S 与低 σ 可以同时出现？

    平坦价带使 DOS 在费米能级附近快速变化，增强 d ln σ(E)/dE，从而提高 S。但平坦能带也意味着大有效质量 m*，降低迁移率 μ，进而降低 σ。这就是热电材料中的经典权衡：高 Seebeck 往往伴随低电导。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联

    1. 创新性判断

    #### Task-specific GNN for thermoelectric transport rather than generic crystal prediction

    过去 2–5 年晶体 GNN 的主流进展集中在 formation energy、band gap、elastic properties、adsorption、phonon-related properties 等任务；热电电子输运因依赖温度、掺杂、弛豫时间、能带细节，常被公式模型或经验特征模型处理。TECSA-GNN 的新颖性在于将 GNN 架构直接面向 S、σ/τ、κe/τ 三个热电输运目标优化，而不是把 CGCNN/ALIGNN 等通用模型直接套用。

    #### Four-scale representation solves formula-only and structure-only limitations

    前人公式模型如 CrabNet 可快速学习组成规律，但忽略晶体拓扑；结构 GNN 可学习原子连接，但未必编码热电所需的全局物理化学统计。TECSA-GNN 将 global U + atomic V + bond E + angular Θ 融合，解决了两类信息割裂问题。

    #### Angular line-graph message passing captures local distortion effects

    热电性能对局域畸变、键角变化、轨道杂化很敏感。TECSA-GNN 通过 line graph aggregation 将键角信息显式传递到键嵌入，再影响原子嵌入，形成 Θ → E → V 的层级机制。相比只用原子-键邻接的 CGCNN，这更适合描述复杂输运物理。

    #### Doping and temperature-aware transport learning improves practical relevance

    模型输入显式包含掺杂类型、掺杂浓度、温度条件、Eg，目标也按 n/p 型与不同温度评估。相比只预测材料静态性质，热电输运模型更接近实验与器件设计场景，因为热电性能本质上是条件依赖的。

    #### Material-level leakage control improves benchmark credibility

    同一材料不同掺杂条件必须进入同一 fold，避免模型在训练集中见过同一晶体结构后在测试集中“预测”不同掺杂条目。该设置比普通随机划分更严格，更接近真实未知材料预测。

    #### Fine-tuning protocol demonstrates transferable structural embeddings

    对 133 个特殊结构进行遮蔽，再冻结特征提取层、只微调回归头，证明预训练模型可迁移到特定结构家族。该策略解决了热电材料中某些结构族样本少、从头训练成本高的问题。

    #### Screening-to-DFT-to-mechanism pipeline closes the loop

    创新不止于预测精度，还形成闭环：

    • TECSA-GNN 从 Materials Project 筛选候选；
    • DFT 验证 PF、κe/τ；
    • 能带、PDOS、ELF 解释输运来源；
    • 区分 Te₃As₂ 高 σ 型、NaTlSe₂ 高 S 低 σ 型、LiMgSb 子晶格输运型机制。

    这种流程将黑箱高通量筛选推进到物理解释层面。

    #### Solved gap relative to recent works

    解决的核心前人问题包括：

    • 化学式模型无法区分同组成异构体；
    • 通用晶体 GNN 在 TE 输运上可能落后于公式模型；
    • 热电输运需要同时表达局部几何、全局组成、掺杂与温度；
    • σ/τ、κe/τ 分布跨度大，需要 log 建模；
    • 特殊结构族数据少，需要可微调的迁移方案；
    • 高通量预测缺少 DFT 机制追踪。
    阅读原文 ↗
    原文链接页内定位
  9. 09
    迈向工程材料神经网络#
    Towards Engineering Material Neural Networks#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 材料 / 器件📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 Charles de Kergariou, Hortense le Ferrand, Ali Momeni, Romain Fluery, Kunal Masania, Adam W Perriman, Fabrizio Scarpa🔥 AI 0

    💡 亮点：把智能计算功能嵌入材料结构。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题如何把神经网络式学习机制真正嵌入承载工程材料中，使材料结构不再只是由外部电子系统控制的被动自适应体，而是由可独立调节的材料节点、物理权重和反馈机制共同完成输入感知、信息传递、目标输出和在役学习；核心瓶颈是让刚度、热导率、电导率、几何形变等材料参数像神经网络权重一样可写入、可保持、可逆更新，并同时维持结构承载稳定性。
    创新方法提出 Engineering Material Neural Networks（EMNNs）概念框架：把承载架构材料设计成互连材料节点网络，每个节点拥有可训练物理参数，材料本体同时承担力学承载、物理信号传播、权重存储和反馈更新功能。Aha 点在于将传统“外部计算机控制材料”转变为“材料自身作为神经网络”，并用三条规则界定 EMNN：可单独适应的互连材料节点、按用户需求改变的输出、面向能效/精度/去数字化/收敛速度的优化设计；同时建立从 in-silico 到 full physical feedback control 的训练路线图。
    工作流程输入端接收环境或操作者给出的物理变量，如温度、载荷、湿度、磁场或位移；这些输入被编码为材料网络内部的热、力、电、磁或形貌变化；物理量在由可调节点组成的材料网格中传播，节点权重由刚度、热导率、电导率、几何状态等物理参数表示；前向推理产生可测输出，如目标温度、位移、副翼角度或机器人皮肤粗糙度；反馈阶段比较实际输出与目标输出，形成误差信号或局部差异；误差信息通过物理机制传回节点，例如热电 Seebeck 电压、压电变形、局部力学耦合、随机反馈投影或对比状态；节点材料参数被更新，完成下一轮物理学习。
    关键结果论文形成了 EMNN 的概念判据、前向推理与反馈训练框架，以及一条从传统电子控制到全物理材料学习的技术路线图。它指出现有机械神经网络、可调刚度梁、屈曲梁网络、局部学习弹簧系统和自适应超材料多数只实现了前向功能或数字辅助训练，尚未达到真正材料内生学习；理想 EMNN 需要永久且可逆的自适应材料，因为这类材料可像可擦写存储器一样反复改变并保持物理权重。复合材料、架构材料、生物材料和工程活材料被识别为最有潜力的载体。
    应用价值该研究为智能工程材料提供了从“被控制材料”走向“会学习材料”的设计蓝图，可用于低能耗、自主适应和抗极端环境的结构系统。潜在应用包括无需大量数字计算即可调节翼面姿态的飞机副翼、能根据湿度和物体状态改变粗糙度的软机器人手、极端金星环境中的自主探索结构、可自优化的超材料和工程活材料。长期价值在于降低 GPU 和外部电子控制依赖，让承载结构本身具备感知、计算、记忆和适应能力。

    第一部分：核心概览

    提出Engineering Material Neural Networks（EMNNs）：一类具有承载能力、互连可调材料节点与物理可训练参数的神经网络式工程材料结构。核心贡献在于把物理神经网络从光学、声学、电磁计算扩展到结构工程材料，强调材料本体同时承担力学功能、信息传递、参数更新与环境适应。该框架明确了 EMNN 的三条设计规则、前向推理与反馈训练流程，并系统比较了从 in-silico 到全物理反馈控制的训练路径，定位为智能材料、超材料、机械神经网络与工程活材料之间的概念桥梁。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Towards Engineering Material Neural Networks》（None，）

    背景

    传统自适应材料多依赖预设结构设计与电子计算控制；现有物理神经网络主要集中在光学、声学、电磁系统，缺乏真正嵌入承载工程材料中的学习机制。EMNN 被定义为物理神经网络的一个子类，目标是在材料结构内部实现智能、适应与学习。

    方法

    构建 EMNN 的概念框架：要求结构由可独立调节的互连材料节点组成，输出可按用户需求适应，并优化能效、精度、去数字化依赖与收敛速度。训练机制被分为前向推理与反馈更新，并比较 in-silico training、physics-aware training、DFA、ELM、RC、zeroth-order gradient、equilibrium propagation、local learning、Hamiltonian echo backpropagation 与 full physical feedback control。

    结果

    形成一套从传统控制到全物理材料神经网络的技术路线图。复合材料、微结构材料、生物材料、工程活材料等被识别为潜在载体；可逆永久自适应材料被视为最理想的 EMNN 候选材料。

    讨论

    EMNN 的关键挑战在于把可训练权重、局部反馈、能量自主性与承载结构稳定性同时嵌入材料。机械神经网络、可调刚度梁、屈曲梁网络、局部学习弹簧系统等已有研究提供了原型，但尚未达到全材料内生学习。

    局限

    现有系统大多依赖 MATLAB、电子传感器、外部执行器或人工调参；许多结构只有前向功能，没有真正的反馈学习。非线性材料虽增强表达能力，却会增加物理反馈、梯度计算与权重更新难度。

    结论

    EMNN 是智能工程材料的重要未来方向。短期可通过 physics-aware training、局部学习、DFA、ELM/RC 等中间路线推进；长期目标是实现每个材料节点均可通过物理机制独立、可逆、可控更新的全物理反馈控制材料神经网络。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析

    Abstract

    Core concept of EMNNs

    EMNNs 被定义为一种把神经网络式形态与可训练物理参数嵌入承载工程材料中的结构体系，其核心不是把电子计算器放入材料，而是让材料结构本身承担信息变换与学习功能。摘要明确指出：*"We discuss here the potential to design load-bearing engineering materials with trainable physical parameters and neural network-inspired morphologies, embedding intelligence directly into their structure a concept we define as Engineering Material Neural Networks (EMNNs) as a subcategory of Physical Neural Networks."*

    Problem with existing adaptive material systems

    当前多数自适应材料系统依赖预定义自适应设计和服役中的电子计算，材料自身并未完成学习或推理。关键限制在于结构行为的动态修改仍由外部电子系统主导，而不是由材料节点间的物理交互完成。摘要直接给出问题边界：*"Currently, the majority of adaptive material systems rely on predefined adaptive designs combined with in-service, electronics-based computing to dynamically modify the structural behaviour."*

    Function approximation as the enabling principle

    互连可调节点结构具有近似连续函数的潜力，因此可超越传统超材料和计算材料的固定响应范式。这里的理论基础是节点网络—函数近似关系：*"structural configurations with interconnected adaptable nodes are able to approximate continuous functions, providing new possibilities and opportunities than classical metamaterials and computational materials."*

    Material families with EMNN potential

    可用于 EMNN 的材料候选包括复合材料、架构材料、生物材料、工程活材料。这些材料被看作实现可训练节点、可逆参数变化、能量耦合与结构功能一体化的基础平台。摘要列出：*"Key material candidates for realising EMNNs include composites, architected, biological and engineering living materials."*

    ---

    1 Introduction

    AI motivates new physical computing paradigms

    AI 已成为医疗、软件开发、设计等领域的关键工具，但其计算硬件，尤其是 GPU，存在高成本和不可持续能耗问题，因此推动了新型物理计算系统的发展。引言开头指出：*"Over the past decades, AI has emerged as an indispensable tool across diverse fields including healthcare, software development and design."* 随后强调新方向：*"New physical computing systems, however, are being developed to limit the use of expensive and non-sustainable graphic processing units (GPU)."*

    Physical neural-like computation has historical depth

    物理计算并非新概念，可追溯至古希腊，并经由 Charles Babbage 的机械计算思想广泛传播。该历史脉络说明 EMNN 不是凭空出现，而是物理计算、材料科学与神经网络结构思想的交汇。原文写道：*"Physical computing can be traced back to ancient Greece and was largely popularised by Charles Babbage."*

    Optical and electronic neural-like structures still depend on external energy

    自 1964 年 optical correlator 以来，光学与电子系统已经可以模拟神经网络行为，但它们通常仍依赖外部电力，并执行类似传统处理器的计算功能。关键表述为：*"Since the optical correlator in 1964, structures mimicking neural network behaviour capable of computation have been developed in optics and electronics."* 但限制在于：*"These structures still rely on the use of external electric power and serve the same computational functions as conventional processing units."*

    Material-embodied computation improves energy efficiency

    材料神经网络式结构的优势在于神经连接并不由 GPU 数字处理，而是由材料刚度等物理属性直接实现。计算能效提升来自连接权重的物理嵌入。原文给出关键机制：*"The intrinsic materials-based approach to design these neural network-like structures enhances the computational energy efficiency, as neuronal connections are not processed by a GPU but they are physically embodied through the material’s stiffness."*

    Fixed structural parameters limit current material computation

    现有材料计算结构的关键缺陷是刚度、密度、几何、电导率等参数通常在制造阶段固定，服役中不能为目标输出或误差校正而自适应更新。原文精确列举：*"However, structural parameters (e.g. stiffness, density, geometry, conductivity) for the material-based computation are fixed during production and cannot be adapted in service to achieve the desired output or correct errors."*

    Buckled beams demonstrate mechanical neural computation but remain computer substitutes

    屈曲梁状态已被用于构建稳健神经网络，可识别数字并执行计算；但这些结构大多仍被当作非数字计算机替代品，而非真正具备材料内生学习的工程结构。证据包括：*"Buckled states of beams have been used to create a robust neural network capable of recognising numbers and performing computing."* 同时指出限制：*"these adaptive structures are mostly used as a non-digital substitute of computers."*

    Electromagnetic physical neural networks still use electronics for control layers

    电磁波物理神经网络利用波物理作为数学运算基底，但调制、读出、记忆或控制通常仍由电子系统承担。因此，它们虽是物理神经网络，却不完全等同于材料自治智能。原文说明：*"In electromagnetic wave-based physical neural networks, wave physics provides the computational substrate for mathematical operations, while electronics typically handle modulation, readout, memory or control functions."*

    Neuromorphic metamaterials face adaptation limits at non-electronic junctions

    类脑超材料概念已经提出，但单元之间的非电子物理连接使计算过程难以在服役中调整。Sylvestre 等系统中，刚度节点连接的计算能力由生产时定义的输入载荷决定，不能服役自适应。原文指出：*"the non electronic physical junctions between unit cells (nodes) make it difficult to adapt the computations occurring within the metamaterial."* 具体例子为：*"the stiffness node junction’s computing power is determined by input loads defined during production and cannot be adapted in service."*

    Adaptable junctions are central to increasing metamaterial intelligence

    若能制造可适应节点连接，超材料的适应性和计算能力将显著提升。这是 EMNN 区别于传统超材料的重要切入点。原文明确判断：*"Hence, creating adaptable junctions would represent a way to increase the adaptability and computing power of metamaterials."*

    EMNN converts physical variables into outputs through material architecture

    EMNN 被定义为一种类脑结构，通过图 1 所示架构把物理变量转化为可测输出，并利用材料内在属性实现这种转换。核心定义为：*"The EMNN concept describes a neuromorphic structure that converts physical variables into measurable outputs by approximating a physical function through the architecture presented in Fig. 1."* 其机制为：*"An EMNN leverages the intrinsic properties of a material to achieve this transformation."*

    Inputs and outputs may share or differ in physical nature

    EMNN 不限于同类变量映射，例如温度到温度，也可以实现跨物理域的转导，例如力到电、湿度到形貌、温度到电压。原文强调：*"The system’s inputs and outputs can be of the same nature or dissimilar, as in the case of transduction functions."*

    EMNNs are load-bearing physical neural networks with trainable material parameters

    EMNN 是物理神经网络的子类，特征是承载架构材料结构与可训练物理参数结合。原文定义非常关键：*"EMNNs represent a subcategory of physical neural networks, consisting of load-bearing architected material structures with trainable physical parameters."*

    Three objectives: sustainability, autonomy and optimisation

    EMNN 的发展目标被归纳为可持续性、自主性、优化性。这三者分别对应低能耗训练、减少人工调参、在不可预测环境中自适应优化。原文写道：*"The development of EMNNs will target three main objectives: sustainability, autonomy and optimisation."* 进一步说明：*"designed to minimise the energy required for behavioural training and to reduce the time operators spend tuning physical parameters, enabling the structure to autonomously adapt and optimise its performance in unpredictable contexts."*

    Venus exploration illustrates EMNN application relevance

    NASA 计划使用 automata 进行金星表面探索；EMNN 可能提供金星极端环境所需的低能耗自主性与自适应优化能力。原文给出应用背景：*"NASA plans to use automata for Venus surface exploration."* 潜在价值为：*"EMNNs could offer energy-efficient autonomy and adaptive optimization required for navigating the unpredictable and harsh Venusian environment."*

    Three rules define EMNN eligibility

    EMNN 必须满足三条规则：其一，结构由可单独适应的互连材料节点构成；其二，系统输出可按用户需求改变；其三，设计应优化能效、精度、去数字化计算依赖与收敛速度。原文完整列出：*"Rule #1 : The structure must feature an assembly of individual interconnected material nodes individually adaptable."*；*"Rule #2 : The output of the system must be adaptable according to the demand of the user."*；*"Rule #3 : The design of the EMNN should optimise energy efficiency, output accuracy, independence from traditional digital computations and speed of convergence."*

    Learning, adaptation, feedback control and autonomous actuation are carefully distinguished

    术语边界被严格划分：autonomous actuation 指系统获取并处理运行输入；feedback control 指更新物理神经网络权重；learning 指为特定任务优化可训练参数；adaptation 指材料或结构尺度响应因触发而改变。关键定义包括：*"Feedback control refers to the update of the weight of the physical neural network."*；*"Learning here is used to designate the optimisation of trainable parameters for a specific task."*；*"Adaptation, at both the material and structural scales, refers to the change in behaviour or response following an adaptation trigger."*

    ---

    1.1 Structure

    Interconnected node networks provide the mathematical basis

    互连节点网络能够近似连续函数，这是 EMNN 能把输入物理变量映射为目标输出的理论基础。原文直接给出基础命题：*"Networks of interconnected nodes can approximate continuous functions."* 因此，环境适应和目标输出可通过动态近似所需行为实现：*"a networked structure of interconnected nodes can dynamically approximate the necessary behaviour."*

    ANN-to-EMNN translation makes all parameters physical

    图 2a 的 ANN 中，系数 λᵢⱼ 用于从输入温度 Tᵢ₋ₖ 获得输出温度 Tₒ；图 2b 的 EMNN 版本中，所有参数都必须成为物理参数，以满足规则 #1。原文说明：*"Fig. 2 b shows its equivalent EMNN version, in which all parameters become physical to respect the Rule #1 previously defined."* 在示例中：*"the coefficients λij represent the thermal conductivity, while To and Ti−k are the output and input temperatures."*

    Forward pass encodes and evolves physical information

    EMNN 的前向过程包括两步：第一，把操作者或环境输入编码为结构内的物理变化；第二，构建节点网格的物理模型，使其在边界条件和可训练参数下通过耦合材料动力学生成输出。原文定义 FW1：*"Encode the information of the input provided by the operator or the environment through physical changes within the EMNN."* 定义 FW2：*"Propose a physical model for the node grid that evolves through coupled material dynamics under boundary conditions and trainable parameters to generate outputs."*

    Output is expressed as a physical function of trainable material parameters

    前向推理输出由函数 (Tₒ₌f(łambdaᵢⱼ;Tᵢ₎) 表示，其中 (f) 是由神经网络近似的函数，(łambdaᵢⱼ) 是物理权重，例如热导率。原文写道：*"From the forward pass, the measurable variable output of the EMNN can be calculated using Eq. 1, with f being the function approximated via the neural network: To=f(λij;Ti)."*

    Feedback pass requires physical loss, gradient transfer and weight update

    反馈过程包括比较输出与目标、计算权重梯度、把梯度信息传递到节点、用梯度更新材料权重。核心难点在于损失和梯度值如何物理获得。原文定义 FB1：*"Compare the obtained output against the target."* 并指出难点：*"One of the core difficulties in creating EMNN lies in the physical obtention of these values."* 权重更新形式为 (łambda łeftarrow łambda-μnablałₐₘbdₐL)，原文写道：*"An example of gradient calculation is given in Eq. 4."*

    Metamaterials already have forward pass but lack cognitive training

    传统超材料通常具备固定功能或前向响应，但缺少训练相位与可学习反馈机制。原文定义超材料：*"A metamaterial is a 3D structure with a response or function due to the collective effect of meta-atom elements that is not possible to achieve conventionally with any individual constituent material."* 其优势为：*"Metamaterials can generate functionalities beyond the properties of the classical bulk or continuum materials."* 但关键缺陷是：*"Classical metamaterials lack cognitive training functions."*

    Training and adaptation could transform metamaterials into EMNNs

    若在超材料中加入训练阶段和自适应机制，结构不仅能响应变化条件，还能发现传统建模未预见的优化行为模式。原文判断：*"By incorporating a training phase and adaptation, a metamaterial could respond to changing conditions and discover optimised behavioural patterns even those unforeseen by conventional modelling."*

    ---

    2 Training Strategies: Autonomous Physical Adaptability

    Real-time EMNN functionality depends on forward inference

    EMNN 的主要目标是把物理变量转换为目标输出；实时自适应功能依赖前向推理过程。前向效率取决于转换性质、尺度、复杂度以及各节点转换性能。原文指出：*"the main objective of a EMNN is to transform a physical variable into the required output."* 并补充：*"The real-time, adaptive functionality of EMNNs depends solely on the forward inference pass."*

    Training physical parameters is central to EMNN identity

    EMNN 区别于普通材料结构的关键，在于能根据环境和操作者需求调节前向推理输出所依赖的材料属性。因此，训练策略不是辅助模块，而是 EMNN 的核心。原文明确：*"EMNNs differentiate themselves from standard material structures by their ability to adapt to their environment and operator requirements."* 随后指出：*"Training strategies for the material properties controlling the output of the inference pass are therefore central to their functioning."*

    Autonomous physical adaptability measures independence from digital computation

    Autonomous physical adaptability 表征神经网络式结构在不依赖传统计算输入时，以物理方式近似目标连续函数的能力。原文定义为：*"The degree of autonomous physical adaptability reflects how effectively the neural network-inspired structure physically approximates the desired continuous function without input from traditional computation."*

    In-silico training is the lowest physical adaptability level

    in-silico training 中，所有计算都在 GPU 或传统计算平台完成，之后再物理实现结构，因此材料本体并不学习。原文判断：*"The lowest degree of autonomous physical adaptability is In-silico training, where all computations are performed on GPUs before physical implementation."* Li 等采用 adjoint-based gradient descent backpropagation 训练刚度机械神经网络控制输出位移，但结构自身不学习：*"the physical structure itself does not learn; its behaviour remains fully dependent on the pre-designed and manufactured properties of the mechanical metamaterial."*

    Creased-sheet and polymer-crease systems indicate partial physical adaptability

    折痕片材物理神经网络、动态振荡系统、拓扑机械神经网络等可以通过计算设计实现分类功能；聚合物局部折痕结构中，折叠软化折痕并改变折叠行为，体现不可逆实验学习。原文描述：*"Similar purely theoretical and computational models have been developed to design physical neural networks made of folded creased sheets, dynamic oscillating and topological mechanical neural networks."* 聚合物例子为：*"the polymer folding softens the crease and therefore supports the adaptation of the folding behaviour."*

    Ultimate EMNN target is reversible full physical function approximation

    EMNN 的最终目标是完全独立于外部计算，以物理且可逆方式近似目标连续函数。原文给出长期目标：*"The ultimate goal of Engineering Material Neural Networks is to physically and reversibly approximate the desired continuous function, entirely independent of external computation."*

    Optical neural networks inspire EMNN training architectures

    现有开放文献中多数物理神经网络基于光或声，因为二者能在空气中传播信息；这些系统不完全是 EMNN，但可为材料神经网络的训练回路提供启发。原文指出：*"most of the Physical Neural Networks developed in open literature are based on physical mechanisms associated to light or sound, which can transmit information through air."* 同时强调：*"optical neural networks, more advanced in development, offer valuable inspiration for EMNNs."*

    Adjoint-based backpropagation bridges digital and physics-based learning

    Adjoint-based backpropagation 介于梯度反向传播和物理训练方法之间：结构执行前向过程，反向只求解伴随方程以更新代码权重。原文写道：*"Adjoint-based backpropagation serves as a technique bridging gradient-based backpropagation ... and physics-based methods."* 机制为：*"the structure simulates the forward pass, but only solves an adjoint equation backward to update the weight of the code."*

    Direct Feedback Alignment may reduce backpropagation constraints

    DFA 通过注入随机反馈矩阵直接调整各权重，而不是逐层传播更新，因此可能降低 EMNN 对传统反向传播的依赖，更便于物理实现。原文说明：*"individual weights are adjusted directly using injected random feedback matrices ... rather than propagating weight updates layer by layer."* 其价值为：*"This method has the potential of limiting the backpropagation constrains from the EMNN, hence, facilitating their physical implementation."*

    ELM and reservoir computing offer partial-training intermediate routes

    ELM 与 RC 不要求所有权重更新，通常只训练读出层或少数层，因而适合作为全物理反馈控制前的中间路径。原文指出：*"training EMNNs has the potential of being conducted by applying Extreme Learning Machine (ELM) and Reservoir Computing (RC) concepts, where not all weights are updated."* 限制为：*"These methods are limited in adaptability, and will serve as an intermediary step toward effective learning throughout all layers via full physical feedback control training."*

    Zeroth-order gradient estimates updates through perturbations

    zeroth-order gradient 方法通过轻微扰动可训练参数并测量损失或输出变化估计更新方向，不同于完全无梯度搜索。原文定义：*"trainable parameters are slightly perturbed and the resulting change in loss or output is measured to estimate an update direction."* 并区分：*"This differs from fully gradient-free search methods, which optimize without explicitly estimating gradients."*

    Equilibrium propagation uses contrast between system states

    Equilibrium propagation 是能量基础的局部对比学习方法，通过比较系统两种配置得到权重更新，通常需要两个并行实例来生成比较点，从而避免外部记忆。原文解释：*"Equilibrium propagation is a way of obtaining updates on the weights of the network by, for example, comparing the system in two different configurations."* 进一步说明：*"This typically requires two parallel instances of the system to simultaneously generate comparison points, eliminating the need for external memory."*

    Physical local learning reduces global feedback requirements

    物理局部学习只使用局部可得信息更新神经元，避免全尺度反馈控制，降低设备和空间需求。原文表述：*"physical local learning updating neurons using only locally available information."* 优势为：*"This eliminates the need for full scale feedback control, reducing both equipment and physical space requirements for the material neural network structure."*

    Hamiltonian echo backpropagation exploits time-reversal dynamics

    Hamiltonian Echo Backpropagation 通过理想化能量模型和反馈系统，把误差信号叠加到返回信号中更新结构，并利用 Hamiltonian 动力学的时间反演不变性。原文写道：*"Hamiltonian Echo Backpropagation uses a feedback system with an idealized energy model of the system to superimpose error onto the return signal, updating the structure."* 图示含义为：*"using the time reversal invariant dynamics of the Hamiltonian gradient update method."*

    Full Physical Feedback Control is the ultimate EMNN training target

    全物理反馈控制不是某一种已实现的具体算法，而是 EMNN 的终极目标：每个材料权重都由物理机制独立、可控更新，并完全摆脱传统计算系统。原文明确：*"Full Physical Feedback Control training for EMNN where each material is updated individually with physical mechanism."* 其性质为：*"This last step is not a training method of a specific nature, it is the ultimate training target for the creation of EMNNs."*

    Iterative physical learning demonstrates physics-aware stiffness adaptation

    Chen 等通过局部感知梁中桁架位置，并根据局部目标位置与测量位置差异调节刚度，实现 tip displacement 控制，是 physics-aware training 的例子。原文描述：*"an Iterative Physical learning strategy locally senses the position of the different trusses used as reinforcement in the beam and adjusts the stiffness of the beam on the difference between the local targeted position and the one measured."*

    Existing mechanical neural networks remain limited by manual or electronic updates

    Mei 等的弹簧—屈曲梁机械神经网络可通过双稳态节点控制输出位移，但训练在 MATLAB 中完成，梯度误差修正由人工实施。原文写道：*"Training calculations were performed in MATLAB using manually implemented gradient-based error correction."* 限制为：*"manually updating the network’s weights limits its physical adaptability."*

    Tunable stiffness beam networks provide in-service control but rely on electronics

    Lee 等提出由可调刚度电子梁组成的机械神经网络，通过刚度关系控制输入—输出位移；遗传算法与 partial pattern search 用于 in-silico 求最优刚度。原文指出：*"The structure consisted of an assembly of tunable stiffness electronic beams."* 局限为：*"While not a true Material Neural Network due to its hardware electronic components, the study provides valuable insights into in service stiffness control for such systems."*

    Manual educational and experimental networks show local training principles

    Schaffland 的教育机械神经网络中，杠杆位移既作为输入、输出又作为权重，训练由操作者手动完成；Du 等系统用节点角位置作为输入，组装节点形状作为输出，局部节点与近邻信息足以手动控制反作用刚度。原文写道：*"lever displacements serve as inputs, outputs and weights."* Du 等机制为：*"the angular position of a given node and its closest neighbour provide sufficient information to manually control the stiffness that counteracts the action of the motorised hinge."*

    Node distribution is a major design variable

    许多已有结构不是网格，而是线性排列或不规则连接；空间布局会直接影响物理神经网络性能，因此测试多种节点分布至关重要。原文指出：*"many of the architectures proposed in the previous studies are not organised around a grid like structure, but rather along a line arrangement, or sets of irregular connections."* 设计意义为：*"testing various node distributions is essential for developing physical neural networks, since spatial arrangement directly affects performance."*

    Hebbian adaptation offers strong potential for material neural networks

    Stern 等提供局部训练 MNN 的理论框架，其中一种策略借鉴 contrastive Hebbian adaptation：比较固定输入状态与固定输入+目标输出状态，再用两状态节点输出差异更新局部权重。原文说明：*"One proposed strategy draws inspiration from contrastive Hebbian adaptation ... comparing two distinct states of the system."* 权重更新机制为：*"The network weights (e.g. stiffness, conductivity) are then locally updated using the difference between nodes outputs in both states."*

    Material neural networks with fully embedded training do not yet exist

    到目前为止，真正把训练完全嵌入材料属性的材料神经网络尚不存在；不过相关实验与理论已提供清晰路线。原文结论非常关键：*"material neural networks with training fully embedded in their materials properties do not yet exist."* 同时给出积极判断：*"recent experimental and theoretical advances in related fields offer clear pathways for developing systems."*

    Engineering Material Motor Unit Neural Networks are a transitional class

    EMMUNNs 借鉴生物运动神经元：中央控制系统比较目标与实际输出，再优化节点参数。许多当代超材料若加入物理训练适应性，可能成为 EMMUNNs。原文类比为：*"Motor units are neurones actuating muscles in the body after being triggered by a centralised cortex system."* 潜在路径为：*"Many metamaterials proposed today have the potential of becoming Engineering Material Motor Unit Neural Networks (EMMUNNs) by implementing physical training adaptability."*

    ---

    3 Materials

    Material adaptability is the bottleneck after structural and training concepts

    前一节涉及的系统多为理论结构或仅具有有限材料物理适应性；本节转向可实际增强 EMNN 适应能力的材料方案。原文承接为：*"The previous section describes systems either theoretical or with limited material physical adaptability out of traditional silicon-based computing."* 目标为：*"This section proposes practical, material-based solutions to enhance the adaptability of EMNNs."*

    Energy and memory view is insufficient without node-state transitions

    Walther 的自适应材料视角强调能量与记忆功能，但 EMNN 需要更关注材料在不同永久状态之间如何转换并近似节点行为。原文指出：*"Walther proposes an energy and memory functional view to describe adaptable materials."* 但 EMNN 关键为：*"it is crucial to focus on how transitions between permanent states can approximate node behaviour."*

    Non-adaptive materials cannot form EMNNs

    非自适应材料在触发条件下属性不改变，因此无法承担可训练权重或节点更新功能。原文直接判断：*"Non adaptive materials in Fig. 5 a cannot be used for EMNN."* 图注对应定义为：*"Non adaptive material: the material properties do not change with the trigger."*

    Non-permanently adaptive materials may support EMMUNNs but not full EMNNs

    非永久自适应材料在触发时属性改变，但触发移除后回到初始状态；它们不具备材料内部永久记忆，适合 EMMUNN，而非完整 EMNN。原文写道：*"the non-permanently adaptive materials of Fig. 5 b do not intrinsically display permanent adaptability within the material, but can be used to generate EMMUNNs."* 图注定义为：*"the material properties change with the trigger, but when trigger is then removed ... returning the material to its initial state."*

    Permanently non-reversible adaptive materials enable limited EMNNs

    永久但不可逆自适应材料可用于具有限制的 EMNN，因为其属性改变只能朝某些方向发生，无法自由回调到任意权重。原文说明：*"Permanently non reversible adaptive materials of Fig. 5 c can provide platforms to design EMNNs with limited permanent adaptability, as only certain changes of properties are possible."* 图注描述为：*"the trigger induces permanent changes in the material, leading to restrictions to the achievable range of properties of the material itself."*

    Permanently reversible adaptive materials are ideal EMNN candidates

    永久且可逆的自适应材料最适合 EMNN，因为触发后属性保持新值，而另一触发可使属性回到初始值或其他目标值，等价于可反复写入和擦除的物理权重。原文判断：*"Permanently reversible adaptive materials ... are ideal candidates to for EMNNs, as they provide full flexibility in changing the weights of the nodes."* 图注说明：*"Properties of the material go back to the initial values if a different trigger is applied to the structure."*

    Nonlinear materials increase expressive power but complicate feedback

    线性或非线性材料均可用于 EMNN，但非线性材料会使反馈步骤更难，因为材料本身需要参与计算并把更新权重反馈到结构。原文指出：*"Such materials allow in theory to adapt the behaviour of the structure using linear or non linear materials."* 但限制为：*"the feedback steps presented in Fig. 2 will be harder to implement with non linear materials as the materials will be responsible for calculating and feed the updated weights back to the EMNN."*

    Broken-isomorphism EMNNs could avoid copying artificial neural network operations

    若采用非线性材料，EMNN 可能不再一一复现人工神经网络操作，而是由材料物理变换本身完成训练，形成 broken-isomorphism EMNN。原文定义：*"By adopting non linear material in EMNN, broken-isomorphism EMNN can be created if it does not reproduce operations of artificial neural networks."* 其机制为：*"the physical transformation of the material trains the system instead of having a set of operation mapped onto an artificial neural network."*

    ---

    3.1 Examples of theoretical Engineering Material Neural Networks

    Thermal EMNN illustrates physical weights as tunable conductivity

    热学示例中，结构使用可通过拉伸动态调节热导率的聚合物；(łambdaᵢⱼ) 表示热导率权重，输入与输出分别为温度。原文说明：*"we examine the thermal example in Fig. 2 b. Here, the structure uses a polymer whose thermal conductivity can be dynamically adjusted through tensioning."* Xu 等材料的关键能力为：*"a polymer whose thermal conductivity can be reversibly tuned by adjusting the applied deformation."*

    Feed-forward neural network structure is reached before true EMNN

    当热导率可服役调节时，结构满足规则 #1 和 #2，可被归为前馈神经网络结构；但真正 EMNN 还要求用户任务实现、可逆适应与脱离数字计算。原文判断：*"At this stage, the structure satisfies Rules #1 and #2 for MNNs and can be classified as a Feed Forward Neural Network Structure."* 进一步要求为：*"To qualify as a true engineering material neural network, the structure must fulfil user defined tasks and achieve adaptability and reversibility independently of digital computation."*

    Initial learning may still rely on traditional computing

    早期 EMNN 可采用电子传感器检测输入、输出温度和材料应变，再由电子系统动态拉伸材料，通过 surrogate model 预测并优化材料属性。原文写道：*"Initially, learning could be fully conducted using traditional computing."* 技术细节为：*"electronic sensors detect the input and output temperatures as well as the strain in each material, while an electronic system dynamically stretches each material."* 计算组件为：*"A surrogate model is then implemented to predict and optimise the properties of all stretched materials under the desired conditions."*

    DFA can add material intelligence through Seebeck-effect feedback

    DFA 可通过输出热结构与材料直接接触产生反馈；Seebeck 效应使温差生成电压，该电压再经固定随机投影反馈到材料权重。原文描述：*"Direct Feedback Alignment (DFA) can be employed to update the weights collectively."* 物理机制为：*"Via Seebeck effect, a voltage is generated proportional to the temperature difference."* 反馈路径为：*"this voltage is fed back into the structure’s materials via fixed random projections."*

    Piezoelectric actuation can couple voltage feedback to conductivity modulation

    DFA 反馈电压可放大后输入压电材料，压电变形进一步调节材料电导率；这说明 EMNN 可通过跨物理域耦合完成权重更新。原文细节为：*"The resulting electrical current can be amplified and then directed to a piezoelectric material, which deforms to further modulate the material’s electrical conductivity."*

    Training instrumentation must be miniaturised

    训练系统复杂，若体积或能量耦合过强，会干扰材料前向行为，因此必须小型化。原文指出：*"The training instrumentation is complex and must be miniaturised to minimise its impact on the material’s forward pass behaviour."*

    ELM can reduce interference by updating only final layers

    为减少权重更新机制对前向推理的干扰，可采用 ELM，只更新最终权重层。原文说明：*"To reduce interference from material update mechanisms, Extreme Learning Machine (ELM) can be employed, updating only the final weight layer."*

    Plane aileron example extends stiffness-based mechanical neural networks

    Plane Aileron 应用把 EMNN 用于飞机翼面控制，通过可控、可适应刚度梁自动调节副翼位置，扩展 Lee 等机械神经网络在叶片上的概念。原文说明：*"The application called Plane Aileron is an extension of a concept proposed by Lee et al., in which stiffness-based neural networks ... could be implemented on blades."* 图注概括为：*"integrate controllable and adaptable stiffness beams to automatically control the position of an aileron on a plane’s wing."*

    Grip robot hand example uses roughness control for wet grasping

    Grip Robot Hand 通过控制软皮肤表面皱褶模拟人类皮肤，以提高浸没或潮湿条件下抓取湿物体的能力。原文指出：*"describes the possibility to generate wrinkles on the surface of humanoid robots to mimic human skin, with the wrinkles improving the handling of wet objects in immersed conditions."* 图注概括为：*"an assembly of magnet to control the roughness of a soft skin to adapt the roughness of a robotic hand."*

    Traditional control stage has no embedded material intelligence

    第一阶段是传统控制，训练与实施完全依赖常规计算，材料本身没有智能，也不满足 EMNN 三条规则。原文定义：*"The first stage is the Traditional Control one, where both training and implementation rely entirely on conventional computing."* 限制为：*"This approach does not require embedded material intelligence and does not align with any of the three rules of the EMNN concept."*

    Aileron traditional control is external-engine dominated

    在传统副翼控制中，发动机或执行机构处理飞行员输入、滚转传感器数据和当前副翼位置，材料不参与计算。原文写道：*"the aileron’s orientation is determined by an engine, which processes the pilot’s input, roll sensor data, and the aileron’s current position."* 结论为：*"the material itself has no intelligence as all computations are external."*

    Robotic skin traditional control also lacks matter intelligence

    机器人皮肤皱褶传统方案中，计算机测量皮肤粗糙度和环境湿度，执行器根据传感器数据与操作者需求调节纹理，因此仍无材料内嵌智能。原文说明：*"a computer measures skin roughness and ambient humidity, while the engine adjusts the skin’s texture based on sensor data and operator requirements such as the object to be grasped."* 限制为：*"No embedded matter intelligence is also needed in this case."*

    Forward inference NN structure discretises control into material nodes

    第二阶段把控制系统离散化为前向推理神经网络结构，满足规则 #1 和 #2。副翼例子中，可变刚度材料把发动机输入转换为精确副翼位置控制；刚度属性被动态调节以实现目标输出。原文写道：*"The second step towards the creation of EMNN discusses the discretisation of the controlling system."* 副翼机制为：*"variable stiffness materials are assembled to convert the engine’s input into precise control of the aileron’s position."*

    Magnet-network robotic skin uses field coupling as distributed control

    机器人手皮肤中，嵌入金属颗粒的皮肤由离散磁体通过磁场互连控制；调节磁场强度可产生不同皮肤形貌，单个磁体取向变化即可影响整个磁网络。原文说明：*"the skin embedded with metallic particles is controlled using discrete magnets interconnected through their magnetic fields."* 进一步机制为：*"Controlling the orientation of a single magnet enables large scale skin configurations, as adjusting one magnet’s alignment influences the entire magnetic network."*

    Training maps environmental and task inputs to material control parameters

    副翼和机器人手都需要训练，把输入如湿度、待抓取物、飞行控制信号映射到目标输出如皮肤粗糙度或副翼位置，并对应控制参数如磁场强度或刚度。原文以机器人手为例写道：*"Training is needed to map inputs (e.g., humidity, object to grasp) to desired outputs (e.g., skin roughness) via control parameters (e.g., magnetic field intensity)."*

    Available text ends during autonomous forward inference discussion

    可用内容在句子 *"The autonomous forward inference pass NN configuration of Fig. 6 can represent the structure"* 后中断，因此后续关于 Fig. 6 后两阶段的完整描述、最终结论和材料候选展开无法从给定内容中可靠恢复。

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持

    1. 术语解析

    Physical Neural Network

    Physical Neural Network 指利用物理系统本身执行类似神经网络映射的结构，而不是在数字硬件中模拟神经网络。这里的重点是“权重、传播、非线性或耦合关系”由物理属性承担，例如刚度、热导率、电导率、几何形变、波传播相位等。EMNN 是其子类，但额外要求承载工程材料属性。

    Trainable physical parameters

    Trainable physical parameters 不是普通模型参数，而是可被物理改变并保持或调节的材料/结构属性，例如刚度、热导率、电导率、密度分布、节点几何、连接状态。微妙之处在于“trainable”不只是可设计，而是服役中可更新，且最好可逆、可重复、可局部寻址。

    Autonomous physical adaptability

    Autonomous physical adaptability 强调材料结构在没有传统计算持续介入时，自行通过物理机制调整行为的能力。它不同于普通 adaptive material：普通自适应材料可能只是被动响应刺激，而 EMNN 要能围绕目标任务更新节点权重，形成类似学习的行为。

    Forward inference pass

    Forward inference pass 借自神经网络术语，指输入通过网络产生输出的过程。在 EMNN 中，这不是矩阵乘法在 GPU 上运行，而是热、力、电、磁、声、流体等物理量在材料网络中传播、耦合和转换。

    Full Physical Feedback Control

    Full Physical Feedback Control 是 EMNN 的理想终点：误差检测、梯度或更新方向计算、更新信号传输、材料权重改变，全部通过物理机制完成。它不是现成算法，而是目标状态，要求每个节点权重都能被独立、可控、可逆地物理更新。

    ---

    2. 疑难查证

    为什么“超材料”还不是 EMNN？

    超材料通常已经具有节点化结构和非传统宏观功能，例如负泊松比、异常折射、带隙、可编程形变等。但大多数超材料的功能来自制造时确定的几何和材料参数。它们可以“响应”，但未必能“学习”。

    EMNN 要求更进一步：

    • 节点参数可在服役中改变；
    • 输出可按用户目标调整；
    • 变化过程尽量不依赖外部数字计算；
    • 结构本身承担承载功能。

    因此，传统超材料相当于“固定权重网络”，EMNN 则试图变成“可训练权重网络”。

    为什么反馈训练比前向推理难得多？

    前向推理只要求物理量从输入端传播到输出端。例如温度场经过热导率网络产生目标温度分布，或力经过刚度网络产生目标位移。

    反馈训练还要求知道：

    • 输出与目标差多少；
    • 哪些节点权重造成误差；
    • 每个节点应增加还是减少某个物理属性；
    • 更新后材料仍保持结构稳定；
    • 更新过程不能破坏前向功能。

    数字神经网络中，这些由反向传播和内存完成；EMNN 中则必须通过热电效应、压电效应、局部力学耦合、相变、可逆化学反应、形状记忆、磁耦合等机制完成，难度高得多。

    为什么可逆永久自适应材料最理想？

    EMNN 的权重类似神经网络参数，需要反复训练和修正。若材料变化不可永久保持，则没有记忆；若永久但不可逆，则只能训练有限次数或单方向漂移。理想材料应满足：

    • 触发后属性改变；
    • 触发移除后新属性仍保持；
    • 另一个触发可把属性调回；
    • 多次循环后性能不显著衰减；
    • 可局部控制而非全局同时变化。

    这相当于材料版的“可写入、可保存、可擦除、可重写权重”。

    什么是 broken-isomorphism EMNN？

    普通神经网络式材料设计往往试图把 ANN 的结构映射到材料中：节点对应神经元，连接对应权重，反向传播对应物理反馈。但材料世界不一定必须复制 ANN。

    Broken-isomorphism EMNN 指材料的物理过程不再严格对应 ANN 的数学操作。材料可能通过相变、屈曲、局部损伤修复、细胞生长、磁畴重排等复杂过程完成任务优化。此时不是“材料模拟神经网络”，而是“材料以自己的物理规律学习”。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联

    1. 创新性判断

    From physical neural networks to load-bearing material intelligence

    近 2–5 年内，物理神经网络研究主要集中在光学、声学、电磁、机械计算原型。许多系统擅长分类或信号处理，但不承担工程结构载荷。该框架的新颖性在于把神经网络式学习要求明确转移到承载工程材料中，使材料不只是计算媒介，而是同时承担结构功能和智能功能。

    From adaptive metamaterials to trainable metamaterials

    已有自适应超材料通常能改变刚度、形状、波传播或热响应，但多依赖预设逻辑或外部控制。EMNN 的关键创新在于提出超材料向“可训练节点网络”演化：不仅响应刺激，还要根据目标输出更新内部物理权重。

    Clear rules for distinguishing EMNN from adjacent concepts

    三条规则为领域提供了判据：互连且可单独适应的材料节点、用户需求驱动的可变输出、能效/精度/去数字化/收敛速度优化。这个判据能区分 EMNN、传统超材料、普通自适应材料、机械计算机、工程活材料和电子控制智能结构。

    Training taxonomy connects scattered communities

    in-silico、physics-aware、DFA、ELM、RC、zeroth-order gradient、equilibrium propagation、local learning、Hamiltonian echo backpropagation、full physical feedback control 被放在同一物理适应性尺度上。创新点不在单一算法，而在建立一条从数字辅助设计到全物理材料学习的路线图。

    Material reversibility becomes a neural-network design constraint

    传统材料科学常关注强度、韧性、导热、导电、阻尼、疲劳寿命等指标。EMNN 框架把可逆永久适应性提升为神经网络权重训练的核心材料指标。这使材料筛选逻辑发生变化：材料不仅要“性能好”，还要“可作为可重写物理权重”。

    Intermediate category EMMUNN resolves near-term feasibility

    完全自治 EMNN 尚未实现，直接追求 full physical feedback control 可能过于遥远。EMMUNN 概念提供了过渡路线：中央控制仍存在，但节点执行与材料响应更物理化。该思路可把现有可调超材料、软机器人皮肤、可变刚度结构逐步推向更高材料智能水平。

    Unsolved problem addressed

    前人未解决的核心问题是：如何让工程材料结构不仅具备预设自适应响应，还能在服役中通过材料节点的可训练物理参数实现目标导向学习，并减少对传统数字计算的依赖。EMNN 框架正面回应这一问题，提出结构规则、训练层级、材料适应性分类和理论应用场景。

    Current novelty is conceptual and integrative rather than experimental

    新颖性主要体现在概念统一、判据建立、训练路线图和材料筛选框架；并未展示一个完整实验 EMNN。最强贡献是提出可操作的研究议程：把现有机械神经网络、智能超材料、可调材料和工程活材料组织为通向全物理材料神经网络的连续谱。

    AFM-net 加速稀缺数据纳米计量#
    AFM-net: machine learning acceleration of atomic force microscopy nanometrology from scarce data and fast scans#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 材料 / 器件📖 npj Computational Materials👤 Eva Natinsky, Ryan M. Khan, Qianshu Wang, David Morris, Michael Cullinan, Rémi Dingreville🔥 AI 1

    💡 亮点：AFM-net 处理快扫与少样本纳米计量。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题原子力显微镜纳米计量在快速扫描时容易出现图像质量下降、重构不稳定的问题；同时高质量训练数据稀缺，使常规机器学习方法难以可靠学习 AFM 图像重构规律。核心问题是：如何在少量训练数据和高速扫描条件下，快速恢复可信的 AFM 纳米尺度形貌图像。
    创新方法提出 AFM-net，用机器学习网络专门面向 AFM 纳米计量图像重构，将“少数据可训练”和“快速扫描重构”作为核心设计目标。Aha 点在于：不是依赖大量慢速高质量扫描数据，而是让模型从有限样本中学习快速扫描图像到高质量纳米形貌的映射，从而加速 AFM 成像与计量。
    工作流程输入为快速扫描获得的 AFM 原始或低质量纳米图像，以及少量可用训练样本；AFM-net 学习快速扫描图像中的形貌特征、噪声模式和重构关系；经过模型推理后输出更接近高质量计量需求的 AFM 纳米形貌重构图，实现从稀疏训练数据到快速图像增强重建的流程。
    关键结果AFM-net 被用于加速 AFM 纳米计量图像重构，展示了在训练数据有限和快速扫描条件下进行机器学习重建的可行性。论文摘要未提供具体速度提升倍数、误差降低数值、分辨率改善幅度或与基线方法的定量对比。
    应用价值该研究有助于减少 AFM 纳米计量对慢速高质量扫描和大量标注训练数据的依赖，使纳米尺度表面形貌测量更快、更高效，适用于材料表征、纳米制造质量控制、半导体表面检测和高通量显微成像等场景。

    核心概览

    本文提出 AFM-net，用机器学习在训练数据稀缺和快速扫描条件下加速原子力显微镜（AFM）纳米计量图像重构，属于 AFM 成像/纳米计量与机器学习重建方向。

    方法要点

    • 使用名为 AFM-net 的机器学习网络进行 AFM 纳米计量图像重构。
    • 面向“稀缺训练数据”场景设计或验证模型能力。
    • 面向“快速扫描”条件下的 AFM 图像重构加速。
    • 具体网络结构、训练策略、损失函数、数据来源与实验设置：摘要未详述。

    关键结果

    • AFM-net 被用于加速 AFM 纳米计量图像重构。
    • 该方法针对训练数据有限与快速扫描带来的重构挑战。
    • 摘要未给出具体误差、分辨率提升、速度提升或定量对比结果。
    • 摘要未说明与哪些基线方法比较，也未详述实验样品或应用场景。

    创新性判断

    • 可能的新颖点在于：将机器学习重构方法专门适配 AFM 纳米计量中的“少数据训练”和“快速扫描”双重限制。
    • 相比常规 AFM 图像处理或深度学习重建工作，潜在贡献可能是降低对大量训练数据的依赖，并提升快速扫描下的重构效率。
    • 但由于摘要未详述模型结构、训练机制、数据规模和对比实验，其创新性强弱及相对已有工作的实质差异无法确定。
