  11. 11
    物理引导深度学习洪水预测#
    Advanced Flood Prediction with Physics-Guided Deep Learning: Combining UNet, FNO, and SAR/Optical Imagery#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 方法 / 工具📖 arXiv / cs.LG👤 Tewodros Syum Gebre, Jagrati Talreja, Leila Hashemi-Beni🔥 AI 0

    💡 亮点：影像网络与水动力约束联合制图。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题如何把卫星影像中的“水面痕迹”转化为应急决策需要的连续洪水状态图：不仅识别淹没范围，还同时估计水深、自由水面高程和流速，并在地面观测稀缺、云覆盖、SAR噪声、地形复杂的洪泛区保持水动力守恒一致性。
    创新方法提出物理引导的 UNet–FNO 多模态洪水预测框架：用 Sentinel-1 SAR 捕捉云下水体边界，Sentinel-2 光学影像补充光谱水体线索，DEM/HAND/坡度提供地形约束；UNet 负责精细淹没边界和局部纹理，FNO 在频域学习流域尺度上下游水力联系；MLP 输出水深、水面高程和二维流速，并用浅水方程的质量守恒与动量守恒残差作为训练约束，使预测结果像“被物理方程拉住的洪水场”，而不是单纯像素分类图。
    工作流程输入配准后的 SAR 后向散射、光学波段/云影掩膜、DEM 高程/坡度/HAND → 按传感器归一化并重叠切片 → UNet 提取道路、建筑、河岸、湿干边界等局部细节 → FNO 学习流域尺度低频水动力传播和上下游连通性 → 多分辨率残差连接与特征拼接融合局部-全局信息 → MLP head 逐像素输出洪水概率、水深、自由水面高程、流速 u/v → 根据 DEM 与预测水深构造水面高程，计算浅水方程质量/动量残差 → 联合优化洪水范围损失、水深/速度回归损失、物理残差损失与正则项 → 输出带有物理一致性的淹没范围图和连续水动力场。
    关键结果在三个空间独立、训练中未见过的洪泛区测试中，混合模型达到洪水范围 IoU=0.82±0.03、F1=0.90±0.02，优于 UNet-only 的 IoU=0.75/F1=0.85 和 FNO-only 的 IoU=0.77/F1=0.87；以 HEC-RAS 模拟为参考，水深 RMSE=0.21 m，低于 UNet-only 的 0.34 m 和 FNO-only 的 0.28 m，流速 RMSE=0.15 m/s；质量残差均方约 0.03、动量残差均方约 0.05，质量不平衡低于 2.1%；去除物理正则化后水深 RMSE 增加 18%，证明浅水方程约束不是装饰项，而是提升稳定性和泛化性的关键。
    应用价值该研究把传统“二值洪水掩膜”推进为“可用于调度和救援的连续水动力状态图”，可为灾中应急响应提供淹没边界、水深危险区、流速风险带和质量守恒可信度指标；在缺少实测水位和流速的地区，利用遥感观测与物理方程先验获得更可靠的洪水预测，适合洪泛区风险评估、道路封控、人员疏散、基础设施防护和跨区域快速制图。

    第一部分：核心概览 (Overview)

    该研究提出一种物理引导深度学习洪水预测框架，融合 Sentinel-1 SAR、Sentinel-2 光学影像、DEM 地形特征与深度平均浅水方程（SWE）残差约束，以同时预测洪水范围、水深、自由水面高程和流速。核心贡献在于将 UNet 的局部边界刻画能力与 FNO 的流域尺度算子建模能力结合，并用质量、动量残差提升物理一致性。模型在三个空间独立测试洪泛区取得 IoU=0.82±0.03、F1=0.90±0.02、水深 RMSE=0.21 m、流速 RMSE=0.15 m/s、质量不平衡低于 2.1%，优于 UNet-only 与 FNO-only 基线。该工作位于遥感洪水制图、物理信息机器学习与神经算子洪水模拟的交叉前沿，突出价值在于从二值淹没图推进到连续水动力状态估计。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Advanced Flood Prediction with Physics-Guided Deep Learning: Combining UNet, FNO, and SAR/Optical Imagery》（None，）

    背景

    洪水制图面临地面观测稀缺、地形异质性、传感器噪声、云覆盖、时序缺口以及数据驱动模型难以满足水动力一致性等问题。传统遥感方法多输出二值洪水范围，难以提供应急决策所需的水深、流速、自由水面高程。

    方法

    框架融合 Sentinel-1 SAR、Sentinel-2 光学影像、DEM 派生特征（elevation、slope、HAND）。模型结构由 UNet 提取局部空间细节，由 Fourier Neural Operator (FNO) 建模流域尺度长程水力相互作用，再通过 MLP head 输出连续水动力变量。训练目标包含洪水范围监督损失、水深/流速回归损失、浅水方程质量与动量残差损失、正则化项。

    结果

    混合模型在三个空间独立洪泛区测试集上取得 IoU=0.82±0.03、F1=0.90±0.02，优于 UNet-only：IoU=0.75、F1=0.85 与 FNO-only：IoU=0.77、F1=0.87。以 HEC-RAS 水动力模拟为参考，水深 RMSE=0.21 m，优于 UNet-only 的 0.34 m 与 FNO-only 的 0.28 m；流速 RMSE=0.15 m/s。

    讨论

    混合结构同时捕获局部淹没边界和大尺度水动力联系。物理正则化提升了泛化性与稳定性，尤其适用于观测稀缺区域。消融实验显示，去除物理正则化会使水深 RMSE 增加 18%。

    局限

    模型假设稳态流、静水压力、深度平均速度、不可压缩流，可能限制其对快速演进洪水事件的适用性。SAR 与光学数据在时空上难以严格对齐，且计算需求较高，影响大范围实时部署。

    结论

    将浅水方程约束嵌入 UNet–FNO 多模态遥感模型，可显著提升洪水范围制图与连续水动力变量估计的准确性、物理一致性和可解释性。未来关键方向包括放宽稳态假设、引入时间序列影像、降低计算开销。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析 (Section-by-Section Condensing)

    Abstract

    Accurate flood prediction requires both remote sensing scalability and hydrodynamic consistency

    洪水制图的核心困难来自地面观测有限、地形条件异质、数据驱动模型难以强制水动力一致性。摘要明确问题边界：*"Accurate and scalable flood mapping remains challenging due to limited ground observations, heterogeneous terrain conditions, and the difficulty of enforcing hydrodynamic consistency within data-driven models."* 该问题不是单纯的图像分割问题，而是遥感观测与水动力状态推断之间的逆问题。

    The framework fuses SAR, optical imagery, DEM terrain features, and shallow water equation constraints

    模型输入覆盖三类互补信息：Sentinel-1 SAR、Sentinel-2 optical imagery、DEM-derived terrain features，并以深度平均浅水方程（SWE）提供物理约束。摘要给出完整技术组合：*"integrates multi-modal remote sensing (Sentinel-1 SAR, Sentinel-2 optical imagery, and DEM-derived terrain features) with constraints from the depth-averaged shallow water equations (SWE)."* SAR 提供云下水体敏感性，光学影像提供光谱水体线索，DEM 提供地形约束。

    The hybrid architecture assigns local detail extraction to UNet and basin-scale hydraulic interaction modeling to FNO

    模型结构的关键设计是UNet + Fourier Neural Operator。UNet 负责高分辨率空间边界，FNO 负责长程水动力联系。摘要中的结构描述为：*"combines a UNet to capture fine-scale spatial details with a Fourier Neural Operator (FNO) to model basin-scale hydraulic interactions."* 这一组合针对洪水过程的多尺度性：局部建筑、道路、微地形影响淹没边界；上游-下游连通性影响整体水量分配。

    Physics-informed residual losses enforce mass and momentum consistency

    训练目标不只拟合标签，还引入质量守恒残差与动量守恒残差。摘要明确指出：*"physics-informed residual losses ensure mass and momentum consistency."* 这意味着输出水深与速度场必须在浅水方程意义下尽量自洽，而不仅是在像素层面接近参考图。

    Flood extent accuracy exceeds UNet-only and FNO-only baselines

    混合模型洪水范围预测达到 IoU=0.82、F1=0.90，并优于两个基线。摘要给出定量证据：*"the hybrid model achieves an Intersection over Union of 0.82 and an F1 score of 0.90 for flood extent prediction, outperforming UNet-only and FNO-only baselines."* 该指标显示模型在淹没区域交并比与精确率-召回率平衡上均有优势。

    Continuous hydraulic variables are estimated with low RMSE against hydrodynamic simulations

    水动力变量以模拟结果为参考，模型达到水深 RMSE=0.21 m、流速 RMSE=0.15 m/s。摘要给出的证据为：*"Using hydrodynamic simulations as reference data, the model achieves an RMSE of 0.21 m for water depth and 0.15 m/s for flow velocity."* 这表明模型目标已超出传统二值 flood mask，进入连续水动力场估计。

    Physics consistency remains quantitatively bounded

    物理一致性通过残差与质量不平衡衡量，其中质量不平衡低于 2.1%。摘要写明：*"Physics consistency is maintained, with low residuals and mass imbalance below 2.1%."* 该结果支持“物理可信预测”而非仅“视觉上相似预测”。

    Ablation confirms physics regularization is not ornamental but performance-critical

    消融实验显示，去除物理约束显著降低性能。摘要中的关键判断为：*"Ablation studies confirm that removing physics-based regularization significantly degrades performance, underscoring the value of physical constraints for stability and generalization."* 物理损失在该框架中承担正则化与解空间约束功能。

    ---

    I Introduction

    Flood hazard severity is increasing under climate change, urbanization, and intense rainfall

    研究动机来自洪水灾害风险的上升。引言直接指出：*"Floods are among the most damaging natural hazards worldwide. Their frequency and severity are rising due to climate change, rapid urbanization, and intense rainfall."* 这将问题定位于全球尺度高影响灾害监测，而非单一区域制图任务。

    Frequent SAR and multispectral optical observations enable rapid mapping but do not directly provide decision-ready variables

    卫星遥感提供高频观测，尤其是 SAR 与多光谱光学数据。引言说明：*"Recent advances in satellite remote sensing, especially frequent SAR and multispectral optical observations, offer new opportunities for rapid flood mapping."* 但传感器观测并不等价于应急决策所需水动力信息。

    The core mismatch is between sensor measurements and emergency-response variables

    遥感观测与决策变量之间存在语义鸿沟。原文表述为：*"The core issue is the gap between what satellites measure and what decision-makers need."* 具体而言，传感器获得的是digital numbers、backscatter、reflectance、coherence，而应急响应需要water depth、surface elevation、flow velocity。原文明确列出：*"Sensors capture raw observations (e.g., digital numbers) which are processed into backscatter, reflectance, and coherence, while emergency response depends on water depth, surface elevation, and flow velocity."*

    Hydraulic state estimation from imagery is difficult because of noise, clouds, temporal gaps, and nonlinear hydrodynamics

    从影像反演水深与速度存在多重困难。引言指出：*"Estimating these variables from imagery is difficult because of sensor noise, cloud cover, temporal gaps, and the nonlinear nature of hydrodynamic processes."* 其中 cloud cover 主要影响光学影像，speckle/noise 影响 SAR，nonlinear hydrodynamic processes 则使像素特征到水深/流速之间不存在简单映射。

    Data scarcity worsens the inverse problem

    在缺乏现场水位、流速、高分辨率水动力模型的区域，模型监督信号不足。原文强调：*"The problem is worse in data-scarce regions where field measurements and high-resolution hydraulic models are limited."* 这说明该框架特别面向少监督或弱监督洪水水动力推断。

    The proposed framework embeds shallow water equations into multi-modal deep learning

    方法核心是把多模态卫星数据与浅水方程结合。引言中给出定位：*"This work proposes a physics-guided deep learning framework that combines multi-modal satellite data with the shallow water equations."* 与传统分类不同，该框架把物理方程放入学习过程。

    The approach differs from classification-only or purely data-driven regression methods

    传统方法常依赖二值分类或纯回归，缺少物理约束。引言明确区分：*"Unlike conventional flood mapping methods that rely only on classification or purely data-driven regression, our approach embeds physical laws into the learning process."* 关键差异是输出不仅拟合标签，还满足水动力约束。

    UNet captures fine-scale spatial features and FNO captures basin-scale hydrodynamics

    混合模型的职责分配清晰：*"We integrate a U-Net (UNet) for fine-scale spatial features with a Fourier Neural Operator (FNO) for basin-scale hydrodynamics."* UNet 适合局部纹理、边界、建筑物附近淹没识别；FNO 适合频域全局算子学习和流域尺度相互作用建模。

    The model predicts continuous hydrodynamic state variables while maintaining physical consistency

    研究目标不是只输出洪水掩膜，而是预测连续状态变量。引言写明：*"This hybrid design predicts continuous hydrodynamic state variables while maintaining physical consistency."* 连续变量包括后文输出的water depth、surface elevation、depth-averaged velocity (u,v)。

    Two main contributions define the paper

    贡献包括：UNet–FNO 混合架构与SWE 残差物理引导训练。原文列出：*"Our main contributions include: (1) a hybrid UNet–FNO architecture that captures both local inundation patterns and large-scale flow dynamics; and (2) a physics-guided training approach leveraging shallow water equation residuals to ensure consistency with minimal supervision."* 其中“minimal supervision”说明物理残差用于减少对大规模真实水动力标签的依赖。

    The framework actively assimilates SAR-derived flood extent instead of relying only on simulation emulation

    与纯模拟代理模型不同，该框架利用真实遥感观测边界。引言强调：*"Unlike pure emulators that rely solely on simulation data, our framework actively assimilates SAR-derived flood extent."* 这点重要，因为纯 HEC-RAS 或合成模拟库可能无法反映灾时真实河道、堤防破坏、地物变化或过时地形数据。

    Physics loss constrains plausible states while SAR input anchors observed flood boundaries

    物理项与 SAR 观测项承担互补作用。原文给出机制：*"The physics loss acts as a regularization term, constraining the solution space to physically plausible states, while the SAR input forces the model to respect observed boundaries that static hydraulic models might miss due to outdated bathymetry."* 即物理损失防止不守恒的水深/速度场，SAR 输入纠正静态水动力模型可能遗漏的真实淹没边界。

    ---

    II Related Works

    Remote-sensing flood mapping has progressed from thresholding to learning-based methods

    洪水遥感制图经历了从阈值法到机器学习/深度学习的发展。相关工作开篇指出：*"Flood mapping using remote sensing has evolved from threshold-based classification to advanced learning-based approaches."* 这为 UNet、FNO、PINN 等方法的引入提供技术谱系。

    SAR is widely used because of all-weather capability but remains affected by speckle, roughness ambiguity, and geometric artifacts

    SAR 的优势是全天候、穿云能力。原文写道：*"SAR imagery has been widely adopted due to its all-weather capability."* 经典 SAR 洪水方法包括 Otsu thresholding、region-growing、Bayesian frameworks，尤其用于城市洪水提取：*"Classical methods such as Otsu thresholding, region-growing, and Bayesian frameworks have been extensively applied for flood delineation in urban areas."* 但 SAR 存在斑点噪声、表面粗糙度歧义、叠掩/阴影效应：*"SAR-based mapping faces challenges including speckle noise, surface roughness ambiguity, and layover/shadow effects."*

    The framework extends SAR flood mapping from binary masks to continuous hydrodynamic fields

    已有 SAR 机器学习和模糊逻辑方法提升了洪水检测，但多集中于范围提取。该研究的扩展点是：*"Our work extends these efforts by predicting continuous hydrodynamic fields rather than binary flood masks, leveraging SAR as a primary modality."* 这将 SAR 从“水体检测传感器”提升为“水动力状态反演约束”。

    Optical imagery contributes spectral water cues but suffers from clouds and temporal gaps

    光学洪水制图通常基于水体指数，如 NDWI 与 MNDWI。相关工作指出：*"Optical imagery has traditionally relied on water indices such as NDWI and MNDWI."* 但洪水期间常有云覆盖：*"cloud cover and temporal gaps limit its reliability during flood events."* 因而单独依赖 Sentinel-2 会在极端降雨背景下面临可用性问题。

    SAR-optical fusion exploits complementary sensing strengths

    深度学习模型，尤其是 CNNs and U-Net variants，已提高 Sentinel-2 分割精度：*"Deep learning models, particularly CNNs and U-Net variants, have improved segmentation accuracy using Sentinel-2 imagery."* 本框架采用 SAR 与光学融合：*"Our approach fuses optical imagery with SAR to exploit complementary strengths, ensuring robustness under cloud-obscured conditions."* SAR 保证云下观测，光学提供地物与水体光谱判别信息。

    DEM-derived terrain indicators provide hydrogeomorphic constraints

    DEM 提供高程、HAND、坡度、曲率等洪水易发性因子。原文写道：*"Digital Elevation Models (DEMs) provide terrain-derived indicators such as HAND, slope, and curvature, which are widely used for flood susceptibility mapping."* DEM conditioning 可增强水流方向判别：*"DEM conditioning enhances flow direction and supports hydrogeomorphic flood prediction."*

    DEM features enter the physics formulation through SWE source terms

    DEM 不只是附加图像通道，还参与物理方程项。原文指出：*"In our framework, DEM features inform SWE-based source terms (bed slope, friction) in the physics-guided formulation."* 这意味着 DEM 的坡度与床面信息影响动量方程中的压力梯度、床面坡度和摩阻近似。

    U-Net dominates segmentation but usually lacks physical interpretability

    U-Net 及其变体在洪水分割任务中占主导。原文总结：*"U-Net and its variants dominate flood segmentation tasks, often incorporating attention mechanisms and multi-scale encoders."* 多传感器融合已有进展：*"Multi-sensor fusion (SAR + optical) has shown promise."* 但大多数模型仍输出二值掩膜：*"most models output binary flood masks without physical interpretability."*

    Existing imagery-to-depth or imagery-to-velocity regression often lacks physical constraints

    直接从影像回归水深或流速的方法多依赖合成水动力模拟监督。相关工作指出：*"Efforts to regress water depth or velocity from imagery typically rely on supervised learning with synthetic hydraulic simulations."* 问题在于缺少守恒约束：*"These approaches often lack physical constraints, leading to unrealistic outputs."* 本框架用 SWE 残差惩罚约束水深和速度场：*"Our framework predicts depth and velocity fields under SWE residual penalties, ensuring physical plausibility."*

    PINNs enforce PDE residuals but are slow and unstable near wet-dry fronts

    物理信息神经网络已用于 SWE 和 Navier–Stokes。原文写道：*"Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) have been applied to incorporate physical laws including SWE and Navier–Stokes systems into machine learning models."* 但 PINN 存在收敛慢和湿干界面不稳定问题：*"While PINNs enforce PDE residuals, they suffer from slow convergence and instability near wet–dry fronts."*

    Physics-guided residual penalties are chosen over fully physics-enforced PINNs for scalability

    该框架不是全约束 PINN，而是physics-guided。原文明确：*"Our approach adopts a physics-guided, not fully physics-enforced, strategy using residual penalties and mesh-free sampling, enabling scalability to high-resolution imagery."* 这一选择降低了高分辨率遥感网格上的训练难度，并允许观测误差与物理残差之间灵活权衡。

    FNO provides global receptive fields but struggles with fine spatial detail

    FNO 已用于气候、海洋和洪水建模：*"FNO has emerged as a powerful tool for learning PDE operators in climate, ocean, and flood modeling."* 其优势是全局感受野：*"It offers global receptive fields."* 局限是细粒度边界不足：*"but struggles with fine-grained spatial details."*

    Hybrid CNN–FNO design addresses local-global complementarity

    CNN–FNO 混合设计可以结合局部特征与全局算子学习。原文总结：*"Hybrid CNN–FNO designs leverage local feature extraction and global operator learning."* 本框架具体实现为：*"Our UNet–FNO hybrid captures local flood boundaries while modeling basin-scale hydrodynamics, ensuring consistency with SWE constraints."*

    SWE is the governing hydrodynamic foundation but neural emulators often lack real observation assimilation

    浅水方程是多数洪水预报系统基础：*"The shallow water equations underpin most flood forecasting systems, assuming hydrostatic pressure and depth-averaged velocity."* 神经 SWE 代理可加速模拟，但通常依赖大量合成数据且不吸收真实观测：*"Neural emulators of SWE accelerate simulations but typically require large synthetic datasets and do not assimilate real observations."* 本框架直接从 SAR、光学和 DEM 输入预测 SWE 一致状态：*"Our model directly predicts SWE-consistent states from SAR, optical, and DEM inputs without relying on precomputed simulation libraries."*

    Five literature gaps motivate the framework

    相关工作总结出五个关键缺口：遥感洪水制图缺少物理整合、连续水动力场推断能力有限、多模态传感器大尺度融合困难、PINNs 对大网格低效、缺少局部-全局混合推理架构。原文概括为：*"Existing literature reveals critical gaps: lack of physics integration in remote sensing-based flood mapping, limited ability to infer continuous hydraulic fields, difficulty in multi-modal sensor fusion at scale, PINNs’ inefficiency for large grids, and absence of hybrid architectures combining local and global reasoning."*

    The declared contributions combine multi-scale reasoning, SWE residual learning, multi-modal inputs, continuous estimation, and mesh-free sampling

    相关工作最后归纳贡献：*"Our contributions include a UNet–FNO hybrid for multi-scale hydrodynamic reasoning, physics-guided learning via SWE residuals, multi-modal ingestion of SAR, optical, and DEM features, scalable continuous flood state estimation, and mesh-free residual sampling aligned with image grids."* 贡献结构覆盖模型、物理、数据、输出形式和训练采样策略五个层面。

    ---

    III Methodology

    The methodology targets both flood mapping and hydraulic state estimation

    方法部分定义任务为洪水制图与水动力状态估计。原文开篇写道：*"We propose a physics-guided deep learning framework for flood mapping and hydraulic state estimation using SAR, optical imagery, and DEM-derived terrain features."* 输出目标不仅是淹没范围，还包括连续水深与速度。

    Remote sensing observations are coupled with depth-averaged SWE for physical consistency

    方法框架将遥感观测与 SWE 融合：*"The approach integrates remote sensing observations with the depth-averaged shallow water equations (SWE) to enforce physical consistency while leveraging the representational power of neural networks."* 这体现了数据驱动表示能力与物理方程约束能力的结合。

    Four physical assumptions make training efficient under limited observations

    核心假设包括steady-state flow、hydrostatic pressure、incompressibility、depth-averaged velocity。原文列出：*"The key assumptions, steady-state flow, hydrostatic pressure, incompressibility, and depth-averaged velocity, simplify the governing dynamics and enable efficient training under limited observations."* 这些假设降低 PDE 复杂度，使单时相 SAR/光学输入也能训练。

    Physics enters through residual penalties, while data fidelity uses supervised flood extent and optional velocity losses

    训练信号分为物理一致性与数据一致性。原文说明：*"Physics constraints are incorporated through residual-based penalties, while data fidelity is enforced via supervised losses on flood extent and optional velocity fields."* 即使缺少完整真实水深/流速，模型仍可通过洪水范围与 PDE 残差获得约束。

    The overall pipeline combines image feature extraction with PDE-informed spatial reasoning

    方法总体逻辑是图像特征提取与 PDE-informed operator 的结合。原文表述为：*"The overall pipeline combines image-based feature extraction with PDE-informed operators for spatial reasoning."* 这一点为后续 UNet–FNO 架构铺垫。

    ---

    III-A Model Architecture

    The architecture integrates multi-modal inputs with physics-informed constraints

    架构目标是准确且物理一致的洪水预测。原文写道：*"Our architecture is designed to integrate multi-modal remote sensing inputs with physics-informed constraints, enabling accurate and physically consistent flood predictions."* 这使模型设计从输入层、特征层到输出层均服务于物理残差计算。

    UNet and FNO are complementary components for local and global flood dynamics

    模型由两个互补模块组成：*"It combines two complementary components, the UNet and the Fourier Neural Operator (FNO), to capture local and global patterns in flood dynamics."* UNet 用于局部纹理和边界，FNO 用于频域全局依赖建模。

    The hybrid design preserves fine details and models large-scale hydrodynamic interactions

    模型设计目标同时覆盖细节与全局水力过程。原文明确：*"This hybrid design ensures that fine-grained spatial details from SAR and optical imagery are preserved while large-scale hydrodynamic interactions are effectively modeled."* 对洪水任务而言，这对应淹没边界精度与流域连通性建模。

    The model ingests co-registered Sentinel-1, Sentinel-2, and DEM-derived features

    多模态输入包括配准后的 Sentinel-1 SAR backscatter、Sentinel-2 optical bands、cloud and shadow masks、DEM elevation、slope、HAND。原文写道：*"The model ingests co-registered Sentinel-1 SAR backscatter, Sentinel-2 optical bands (with cloud and shadow masks), and terrain derivatives from DEM (elevation, slope, HAND)."* 配准是关键前提，否则不同传感器像素无法形成一致空间监督。

    SAR contributes cloud-robust flood extent sensitivity

    SAR 对水面和粗糙度敏感，可在云下检测洪水。原文说明：*"SAR: Sensitive to water surfaces and roughness, which enables detection of flood extent under clouds."* 这使 SAR 成为洪水事件期间的主模态之一。

    Optical imagery adds spectral cues under clear-sky conditions

    光学影像补充地物和水体光谱信息。原文写道：*"Optical: Adds spectral cues for land cover and water presence in clear-sky conditions."* 当无云时，光学水体指数和波段组合有助于区分水体、湿土、阴影和植被。

    DEM supplies topographic context for flow paths and pressure terms

    DEM 提供流路、坡度、压力项相关信息。原文说明：*"DEM: Provides topographic context for flow paths and hydrostatic pressure terms."* 在 SWE 中，自由水面梯度和床面高程直接影响动量平衡。

    Multi-modal fusion is critical for robustness across landscapes and observation conditions

    三类输入的融合被定义为跨地貌和观测条件稳健性的关键。原文强调：*"This multi-modal fusion is critical for robust flood mapping across diverse landscapes and observation conditions."* 这对应不同地形、土地覆盖、云况和 SAR 散射条件下的泛化需求。

    Flood dynamics has both local-scale and global-scale dependencies

    洪水过程同时受局部和全局因素控制。原文列出：*"Flood dynamics exhibits both local and global dependencies."* 局部因素包括城市结构、小尺度地形；全局因素包括流域水量再分配、上下游联系。

    Local-scale prediction requires high-resolution spatial detail

    局部尺度上，洪水边界、城市要素和微地形需要高分辨率表达。原文说明：*"Accurate flood boundaries, urban features, and small-scale terrain variations necessitate high-resolution spatial detail to capture fine-grained dynamics."* 这是 UNet 编码器-解码器与 skip connections 的适用场景。

    Global-scale prediction requires long-range hydrological connectivity modeling

    大尺度上，流域水量再分配和上下游相互作用需要长程建模。原文写道：*"Basin-wide water redistribution and upstream-downstream interactions demand long-range modeling to account for broader hydrological processes and connectivity."* FNO 的频域算子学习正适合捕获这类全局低频结构。

    UNet preserves local spatial details through encoder-decoder and skip connections

    UNet 的优势来自编码-解码结构与跳跃连接。原文明确：*"UNet excels at local feature extraction through its encoder–decoder structure and skip connections, preserving fine spatial details."* 洪水边界、道路阻水、建筑阴影等局部特征可通过该结构保留。

    FNO learns low-frequency hydrodynamic patterns in the frequency domain

    FNO 在频域学习代表大尺度水动力模式的低频成分。原文写道：*"FNO complements this by operating in the frequency domain, learning low-frequency components that represent large-scale hydrodynamic patterns."* 低频成分对应流域尺度水面梯度、宽泛水体连通性与整体淹没趋势。

    The UNet-FNO synergy captures processes neither component alone can fully represent

    混合模型价值在于多尺度互补。原文指出：*"This synergy allows the model to capture multi-scale processes that neither component alone could fully represent."* 单独 UNet 易缺全局水力相互作用，单独 FNO 易损失高频边界细节。

    Feature fusion uses residual connections and concatenation at multiple resolutions

    UNet 与 FNO 输出通过多分辨率融合。原文描述：*"Outputs from UNet and FNO are fused using a multi-resolution strategy that combines residual connections and feature concatenation."* 这既保留 UNet 细节，又注入 FNO 全局上下文。

    The fused representation supports continuous hydrodynamic variable prediction

    融合特征用于预测连续状态变量。原文说明：*"The fused representation supports downstream prediction of continuous hydrodynamic variables."* 与分类 head 不同，连续输出可直接参与 PDE 残差计算。

    The MLP head predicts water depth, surface elevation, and depth-averaged velocity at each location

    最终输出层为 MLP head，输出每个空间位置的 water depth、surface elevation、depth-averaged velocity (u,v)。原文写明：*"The fused features are passed through a Multi-Layer Perceptron (MLP) head to predict water depth, surface elevation, and depth-averaged velocity (u, v) at each spatial location."*

    MLP is selected because scalar continuous outputs fit physics-informed residual computation

    MLP 的选择服务于连续变量而非离散类别。原文解释：*"The choice of an MLP is motivated by the need for continuous outputs rather than discrete classes."* 同时：*"This design also facilitates integration with physics-informed constraints, as scalar outputs can be directly used in shallow water equation residuals."*

    Continuous outputs enable shallow water residual computation

    架构与物理学习之间的连接依赖连续输出。原文指出：*"The continuous outputs from the MLP enable computation of residuals from the depth-averaged SWE."* 若只输出二值 mask，则无法直接计算质量与动量方程残差。

    The coupling improves generalization under sparse or noisy observations

    物理正则化使预测既符合观测又符合水动力原则。原文总结：*"This coupling ensures that predictions are not only accurate with respect to observed flood extent but also consistent with hydrodynamic principles, improving generalization under sparse or noisy observations."* 这对应少标签和噪声遥感条件下的主要收益。

    ---

    III-B Physics-Guided Learning with Remote Sensing Constraints

    The depth-averaged SWE acts as the physics backbone

    该部分以深度平均浅水方程作为物理主干。原文写道：*"Our approach leverages the depth-averaged shallow water equations (SWE) as a physics backbone, combined with SAR, optical imagery, and DEM-derived topography to guide learning."* 这里的 “backbone” 不是神经网络骨干，而是物理约束核心。

    Physical assumptions preserve essential hydrologic behavior while enabling efficient training

    稳态、静水压、不可压缩、深度平均速度等假设用于简化动力学。原文解释：*"These physical assumptions simplify the governing dynamics while preserving essential hydrologic behavior, enabling efficient training under limited observations."* 该取舍牺牲部分瞬态复杂性，换取可训练性与低监督适应性。

    Steady-state flow removes time derivatives and enables spatial-only autodifferentiation

    表 I 中稳态流假设实现为移除 SWE 时间导数，影响是简化残差并支持空间自动微分。原文表述为：*"Steady-state flow — Remove time derivatives from SWE — Simplifies residuals; enables spatial-only autodiff."* 对单时相 SAR/光学快照尤其重要。

    Hydrostatic pressure permits a two-dimensional depth-averaged formulation

    静水压力假设去除垂向动量方程。表 I 写明：*"Hydrostatic pressure — Drop vertical momentum equations — 2D depth-averaged formulation."* 适用于水平尺度远大于水深、垂向加速度可忽略的浅水场景。

    Depth-averaged velocity reduces output dimensionality and parameter burden

    速度输出为每点的水平平均速度 (u,v)。表 I 表述：*"Depth-averaged velocity — Predict (u, v) per point — Matches SAR-derived velocities; reduces parameters."* 与三维流速场相比，二维深度平均速度更易由遥感和 SWE 约束。

    Incompressibility treats density as constant

    不可压缩假设将密度 ρ 视为常数。表 I 写道：*"Incompressibility — Treat ρ as constant — Simplifies momentum equations."* 这符合洪水水体在常规水动力尺度下的近似。

    No-slip at bed is approximated through terrain slope source terms

    床面无滑移或摩阻作用通过 DEM 地形坡度进入源项。表 I 表述：*"No-slip at bed — Use terrain slope (∇zb) in source terms — Encodes bed friction implicitly."* 后文还使用 Manning 公式显式近似底摩阻。

    Mesh-free residual sampling supports adaptive grid-free training

    物理残差不必固定在传统数值网格上计算。表 I 写道：*"Mesh-free method — Sample residuals continuously — Adaptive, grid-free training; improves generalization."* 这使物理损失能够与遥感影像瓦片和像素网格灵活对齐。

    Available observations include flood extent, optional velocity proxies, and DEM-derived topography

    数据-物理耦合使用三类观测：洪水范围、SAR 速度代理、DEM 地形。原文列出：*"Available observations include: Flood extent from SAR/optical classification (binary mask). Surface velocity proxies from SAR coherence or offset tracking (optional). Topography derived from Copernicus GLO-30 DEM for bed elevation zb and slope ∇zb."* 其中 Copernicus GLO-30 DEM 提供床面高程与坡度。

    Flood extent defines the wet mask and drives the extent loss

    湿区定义为 Ωw=(x,y):h>ε。原文写明：*"Flood extent defines the wet mask Ωw = (x, y) : h > ε and drives Lext."* 该湿区用于限定水深/速度回归损失只在湿单元计算。

    DEM slopes support hydrostatic and friction terms

    DEM 坡度参与静水压与摩阻项。原文指出：*"DEM-derived slopes support hydrostatic and friction terms, while SAR-derived velocities constrain (u, v) predictions when available."* 这说明地形输入不是纯经验特征，而被嵌入方程残差。

    The governing variables are water depth, depth-averaged velocity, bed elevation, and free-surface elevation

    SWE 定义变量包括 h(x,y)、u=(u,v)、zb(x,y)、η=zb+h、g。原文给出：*"Let h(x,y) denote water depth, u=(u,v) the depth-averaged horizontal velocity, zb(x,y) the bed elevation, and η=zb+h the free-surface elevation. Gravity is g."* 这些变量构成质量与动量守恒残差。

    The continuity equation enforces mass conservation

    质量守恒方程为 ∂t h + ∇·(h u)=0。原文公式给出：*"∂t h + ∇ · (h u) = 0."* 在稳态或单时相情况下，时间项可置零，模型需满足空间通量散度近似为零或低残差。

    The momentum equations enforce x and y directional hydraulic balance

    二维动量方程包含动量时间变化、对流项、自由水面压力梯度与底摩阻。原文给出 x 方向：*"∂t(hu)+∇·(huu)+gh∂xη = −τbx/ρ"*，y 方向：*"∂t(hv)+∇·(hvu)+gh∂yη = −τby/ρ."* 这些方程约束水深与速度场之间的物理关系。

    Bottom shear stress uses Manning’s formula with roughness from land cover

    底部切应力采用 Manning 公式。原文写道：*"Bottom shear stress uses Manning’s formula: τb/ρ = gn² ||u||u / h¹/³, with roughness n from land-cover data."* 其中 n 是 Manning 粗糙系数，来自土地覆盖数据，反映不同地表阻力。

    Terrain slope implicitly encodes bed friction and approximates no-slip behavior

    地形坡度用于近似床面摩阻与无滑移影响。原文表述：*"Terrain slope ∇zb implicitly encodes bed friction, approximating a no-slip condition."* 从严格流体力学看，这是一种工程近似，不等同于完全解析床面边界层。

    Physics residuals are computed from predicted water depth and velocity

    残差由模型输出 ĥ、û 计算。原文说明：*"Residuals are computed from model outputs (ĥ, û)."* 质量残差为 Rh=∂tĥ+∇·(ĥû)，动量残差为 x/y 方向 SWE 平衡误差。

    Predicted free-surface elevation is computed as bed elevation plus predicted depth

    自由水面高程估计为 η̂=zb+ĥ。原文写明：*"with η̂ = zb + ĥ."* 这使 DEM 与水深预测共同决定压力梯度项。

    Characteristic scaling improves numerical stability

    变量使用特征尺度归一化。原文写道：*"Variables are normalized using characteristic scales (H0, U0, L0, T0) for stability."* 对 PDE 残差训练而言，不同量纲和数量级会导致梯度不平衡，特征尺度归一化是必要步骤。

    Spatial derivatives use central differences for pressure/slope and limited upwind stencils for advection

    空间差分策略区分压力/坡度项与对流通量项。原文描述：*"Spatial derivatives use second-order central differences for pressure and slope terms, and a limited upwind stencil for advective fluxes."* 中心差分适合平滑梯度项，上风格式更适合对流项稳定性。

    Temporal derivatives use backward differences when paired observations exist

    有成对时相观测时可计算时间导数。原文写道：*"Temporal derivatives use backward differences when paired observations exist."* 这允许时间序列版本扩展到非稳态 SWE 训练。

    Single-date snapshots are treated as quasi-steady with zero time derivatives

    对单时相 SAR/光学影像，时间导数置零。原文明确：*"For single-date SAR/optical snapshots, we set ∂t(·)=0, reducing output dimensionality and enabling spatial-only autodifferentiation."* 同时物理项会降权：*"Corresponding physics terms are down-weighted to reflect quasi-steady conditions."*

    The composite loss blends extent, depth, velocity, physics, and regularization terms

    总损失为多目标组合：L = λext Lext + λh Lh + λu Lu + λv Lv + λphys Lphys + λreg Lreg。原文给出：*"The composite loss blends data fidelity, physical consistency, and regularization."* 该结构允许根据监督信号可用性调节权重。

    Flood extent supervision uses focal binary cross-entropy

    洪水范围损失使用 focal BCE，处理类别不平衡和难样本。原文写明：*"Flood extent supervision uses focal binary cross-entropy."* 公式包含 α、γ、y∈0,1、p∈(0,1)：*"where y∈0,1 is the reference mask and p∈(0,1) the predicted probability."*

    Continuous water depth and velocity losses are computed on wet cells

    水深与速度回归损失只在 Ωw 湿区计算。原文给出：*"For continuous fields on wet cells"*，并定义 Lh、Lu、Lv 为湿区均方误差。这样避免干区零水深主导训练。

    Training uses AdamW, warm-up, cosine decay, mixed precision, and gradient accumulation

    训练协议包含多项深度学习工程策略。原文写道：*"We train end-to-end with AdamW, warm-up followed by cosine decay for the learning rate, mixed-precision to save memory, and gradient accumulation to keep an effective batch size stable."* 但具体学习率、batch size、epoch 数、权重 λ 数值未给出。

    Training begins with UNet flood extent pretraining before joint UNet-FNO physics training

    训练分阶段进行。原文说明：*"We first pretrain the UNet path on flood extent to stabilize wet–dry delineation, then switch to joint training with the FNO branch and the full objective."* 先稳定湿干边界，再引入 FNO 和完整物理损失，可减少早期训练冲突。

    Physics loss weight is ramped from zero to avoid early optimization conflicts

    物理权重采用渐进式增加。原文写道：*"We ramp λphys from zero to its target value over the initial epochs to avoid early conflicts."* 这符合 PINN/物理约束训练经验：早期预测很差时强物理约束可能阻碍数据拟合。

    Inputs are normalized per sensor using training split statistics

    输入归一化使用训练集统计量。原文写明：*"We normalize per-sensor using training-split statistics."* 这可避免测试集信息泄漏，并处理 SAR、光学、DEM 不同量纲。

    Large scenes are tiled with overlap to reduce boundary artifacts

    大幅影像通过重叠切片处理。原文表述：*"We tile large scenes with overlap to reduce boundary artifacts."* 对 UNet/FNO 瓦片推理而言，边界处上下文缺失会造成预测不连续，重叠可缓解。

    Data augmentation preserves DEM semantics

    增强包括旋转、翻转、强度扰动和随机裁剪。原文写道：*"We apply rotations, flips, modest intensity jitter, and random crops while preserving DEM semantics."* “preserving DEM semantics” 表示不能破坏地形高程、坡度、HAND 与空间方向关系。

    Evaluation uses spatial hold-outs and out-of-domain regions

    评估强调空间泛化。原文说明：*"We assess accuracy and physics on spatial hold-outs and out-of-domain regions."* 这比随机像素划分更严格，因为洪水地貌具有强空间自相关。

    Flood extent metrics are IoU and F1

    洪水范围使用 Intersection over Union 和 F1。原文公式为：*"IoU = |P ∩ G| / |P ∪ G|"* 以及 *"F1 = 2 Precision · Recall / (Precision + Recall)."* IoU 衡量预测与真值区域重叠，F1 平衡漏检与误检。

    Continuous variables use RMSE for depth and velocity where velocity estimates exist

    水深和速度用 RMSE。原文写道：*"For continuous variables, we use RMSE for depth and velocity where SAR-derived velocity estimates exist."* RMSE 公式为：*"RMSE = sqrt(1/N Σt(ŷt − yt)²⁾."*

    Physics consistency is measured using held-out residuals and wet-cell threshold fractions

    物理一致性指标包括 held-out tiles 上的均方残差，以及满足残差阈值的湿单元比例。原文说明：*"We measure physics consistency with the mean squared residuals of (4) on held-out tiles and the fraction of wet cells with |R̃h| < τh and |R̃u,v| < τm."* 具体阈值 τh、τm 未报告。

    Baselines include UNet-only, FNO-only, and no-physics ablations

    对比模型包括 UNet-only、FNO-only 与移除物理项的消融。原文写道：*"Comparisons include UNet-only and FNO-only baselines and ablations that remove the physics term."* 这对应架构贡献和物理损失贡献的分别验证。

    Performance is summarized with 95% bootstrap confidence intervals

    性能不只给点估计，还计划给置信区间。原文写道：*"We summarize performance with 95% bootstrap confidence intervals."* 结果表中只对混合模型的 IoU/F1 显示 ±0.03、±0.02，基线未给置信区间。

    ---

    IV Results and Discussion

    The results section combines quantitative evaluation and interpretation

    该章分为 IV-A Experimental Results 与 IV-B Discussion，覆盖模型性能、物理一致性、消融、部署潜力与局限。标题为 *"IV Results and Discussion"*，体现结果与解释合并呈现。

    ---

    IV-A Experimental Results

    Flood extent evaluation uses three spatially distinct unseen floodplain regions

    测试集由三个训练中未见过的空间独立洪泛区组成。原文写道：*"Table II presents the flood extent prediction performance evaluated on a held-out test set comprising three spatially distinct floodplain regions not seen during training."* 这是较强的空间泛化测试，但未给出每个区域面积、事件数量、影像数量或像素数。

    The hybrid model achieves the best flood extent metrics

    混合模型达到 IoU=0.82±0.03、F1=0.90±0.02。原文明确：*"The hybrid model (UNet + FNO) achieved an Intersection over Union (IoU) of 0.82 ± 0.03 and an F1 score of 0.90 ± 0.02."* 这表明预测淹没区域与真值重叠度较高，F1 也显示较好的精确率-召回率平衡。

    UNet-only baseline underperforms the hybrid model

    UNet-only 的洪水范围性能为 IoU=0.75、F1=0.85。表 II 给出：*"UNet-only — IoU 0.75 — F1 Score 0.85."* 与混合模型相比，IoU 低 0.07，F1 低 0.05，说明仅局部卷积特征不足以捕获完整流域水动力联系。

    FNO-only baseline also underperforms despite better global modeling

    FNO-only 的性能为 IoU=0.77、F1=0.87。表 II 给出：*"FNO-only — IoU 0.77 — F1 Score 0.87."* 与混合模型相比，IoU 低 0.05，F1 低 0.03，说明仅全局频域建模不够精细，可能损失局部边界。

    The hybrid model outperforms both baselines on flood extent

    结果文字明确比较：*"outperforming the UNet-only (IoU: 0.75, F1: 0.85) and FNO-only (IoU: 0.77, F1: 0.87) baselines."* 这验证了局部-全局混合结构的必要性。

    Water depth and velocity evaluation relies on HEC-RAS simulations because field observations are unavailable

    连续水动力变量没有现场实测数据，使用 HEC-RAS 模拟输出作为参考。原文写道：*"Given the lack of observed field data for water depth and surface velocity, we evaluated the model’s performance using outputs from hydrodynamic simulations (HEC-RAS)."* 这意味着 RMSE 是相对于模拟基准，而非真实现场测量。

    The hybrid model achieves the lowest water depth RMSE

    混合模型水深 RMSE=0.21 m，优于 UNet-only 和 FNO-only。原文写道：*"The hybrid model achieved a root mean square error (RMSE) of 0.21 m, outperforming the UNet-only model (RMSE = 0.34 m) and the FNO-only model (RMSE = 0.28 m)."* 相比 UNet-only，误差降低 0.13 m；相比 FNO-only，降低 0.07 m。

    Flow velocity RMSE reaches 0.15 m/s

    流速预测的 RMSE 为 0.15 m/s。原文写道：*"For flow velocity, the hybrid model achieves an RMSE of 0.15 m/s."* 未报告 UNet-only/FNO-only 的流速 RMSE，也未说明速度参考来自 HEC-RAS 还是 SAR proxy。

    Physics residuals remain low and mass imbalance is 2.1%

    物理一致性指标包括质量残差和动量残差。原文给出：*"the hybrid model maintained physical consistency, with mean squared residuals of 0.03 (mass) and 0.05 (momentum), and a relative mass imbalance of 2.1%."* 这为 SWE 约束有效性提供定量证据，但残差归一化尺度未详述。

    ---

    IV-B Discussion

    The hybrid model performs best across all evaluated metrics

    讨论部分总结混合模型在所有指标上优于基线。原文写道：*"The hybrid model demonstrates superior performance across all evaluated metrics."* 这包括洪水范围 IoU/F1、水深 RMSE、流速 RMSE 和物理一致性指标。

    Performance gains support the combination of UNet spatial extraction and FNO physics-informed modeling

    性能提升被解释为 UNet 与 FNO 的互补作用。原文表述：*"which confirms the effectiveness of combining spatial feature extraction (UNet) with physics-informed modeling (FNO)."* 更严格地说，FNO 本身不是物理方程，而是全局算子学习模块；物理信息来自 SWE 残差损失。

    Terrain derivatives and physics regularization improve delineation and hydraulic prediction in complex floodplains

    讨论指出 DEM 派生变量和物理正则化对复杂洪泛区有效。原文写道：*"The integration of terrain derivatives and physics-based regularization improved flood extent delineation and hydrodynamic predictions, particularly in complex floodplain regions."* 复杂洪泛区通常具有多通道、低坡度、植被、建筑物和局部蓄滞水等特征。

    Figure 2 visually compares ground truth and predictions across two sites

    图 2 展示两个站点的洪水范围真值与预测。原文图注为：*"Comparison of flood extent: Ground truth (left) and model prediction (right) for two sites, visualized on a unified color scale where darker tones indicate stronger agreement with ground truth."* 该图用于定性支持边界一致性，但没有提供像素级误差图或区域分项指标。

    The model is claimed to outperform recent literature and baselines

    讨论中给出广义比较：*"Compared to baseline models and recent literature, the hybrid model achieves higher IoU and F1 scores, and lower RMSE values for water depth and velocity."* 但文中未给出与具体文献方法的同数据集直接对照表，因此该结论主要由内部基线支撑。

    Physics-guided learning is especially beneficial in data-sparse environments

    物理约束对观测不足区域的补偿作用被强调。原文写道：*"These improvements are especially notable in data-sparse environments, where physics-guided learning compensates for limited observations."* 物理方程在此相当于先验约束，减少模型对密集标签的依赖。

    Removing physics regularization increases water depth RMSE by 18%

    消融结果显示物理项影响显著。原文给出：*"Ablation studies reveal that removing physics-based regularization increases water depth RMSE by 18%."* 若以混合模型 0.21 m 为基准，去除物理正则后的水深 RMSE 约为 0.248 m；若以无物理模型为分母，具体数值略有差异，原文未说明计算基准。

    Physical laws improve not only accuracy but operational reliability

    讨论将物理约束与可靠性联系起来。原文写道：*"This approach not only improves accuracy but also ensures model reliability in operational settings."* 其逻辑是守恒残差较低的预测更不容易产生水深突变、非物理速度或质量凭空产生/消失。

    Mass balance and governing-equation consistency support real-world forecasting potential

    模型保持质量平衡和方程一致性，被认为有应急应用潜力。原文写道：*"The model’s ability to preserve mass balance and remain consistent with governing equations suggests strong potential for real-world flood forecasting and emergency response applications."* 这类应用需要可解释和稳定预测，而不仅是图像分割精度。

    Scalability and remote sensing adaptability support geographic transfer

    模型适配遥感输入，具有跨区域部署潜力。原文表述：*"Its scalability and adaptability to remote sensing inputs make it suitable for deployment in diverse geographic contexts."* 但该判断受限于测试集仅报告三个空间独立洪泛区，跨气候区、土地覆盖区和传感器条件的证据仍不足。

    Steady-state and hydrostatic assumptions limit dynamic flood applicability

    局限之一是稳态流和统一静水压力假设。原文承认：*"Despite its strengths, the model assumes steady-state flow and uniform hydrostatic pressure, which may limit its applicability during dynamic flood events."* 快速涨落、堤坝溃决、城市排水瞬态过程可能违反这些假设。

    SAR-optical temporal and spatial alignment is a practical challenge

    多传感器数据对齐困难。原文指出：*"the scarcity of temporally and spatially aligned SAR and optical data posed a challenge."* 洪水期间 Sentinel-1 与 Sentinel-2 过境时间不同，光学受云影响，严格同日同状态数据稀缺。

    Sequential learning mitigates SAR-optical alignment scarcity

    为缓解多模态对齐问题，训练采用顺序学习策略。原文写道：*"to mitigate this, we implemented a sequential learning concept, initially trained the model using SAR data alone and later incorporated optical imagery."* 这有助于先学习云下稳定洪水边界，再在可用时吸收光学信息。

    Computational demand hinders real-time large-scale deployment

    计算成本是部署瓶颈。原文明确：*"Computational demands also hinder large-scale real-time deployment."* FNO、UNet、多模态高分辨率瓦片、物理残差计算都增加显存和推理开销。

    Future work targets relaxed flow assumptions, memory optimization, and better heterogeneous-dynamics regularization

    未来方向包括放松流动假设、优化内存、增强正则化。原文总结：*"Future work will focus on relaxing flow assumptions, optimizing memory usage, and enhancing regularization to better capture heterogeneous flood dynamics across diverse land covers and sensor modalities."* 这直接对应当前稳态近似、计算负担、多土地覆盖泛化的局限。

    ---

    V Conclusion

    The work addresses flood extent and hydraulic state estimation under sparse truth and sensor limitations

    结论重申任务难点：从多模态遥感中产生准确且物理一致的洪水范围和水动力状态。原文写道：*"This work addresses the challenge of producing accurate and physically consistent flood extent and hydraulic state estimates from multi-modal remote sensing observations."* 难点来自：*"sparse ground truth, sensor limitations, and the nonlinear dynamics governing inundation processes."*

    The solution integrates SAR, optical imagery, DEM terrain features, and depth-averaged SWE

    结论概括方法为物理引导多模态框架。原文写道：*"we proposed a physics-guided deep learning framework that integrates SAR, optical imagery, and DEM-derived terrain features with the depth-averaged shallow water equations."* 该组合构成数据-物理混合建模主线。

    The UNet-FNO architecture captures local detail and basin-scale hydrodynamic interactions

    结论强调架构动机：*"The hybrid UNet–FNO architecture was specifically designed to capture local spatial detail while modeling basin-scale hydrodynamic interactions."* UNet 与 FNO 的组合是论文核心模型创新点。

    Residual-based physics regularization constrains the model

    结论指出模型通过残差物理正则进一步约束：*"and was further constrained through residual-based physics regularization."* 这使输出具有 SWE 一致性，而非纯经验拟合。

    Flood extent mapping improves substantially over UNet-only and FNO-only baselines

    结论给出主要定量结果：*"Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method yields substantial improvements in flood extent mapping, achieving an IoU of 0.82 and an F1 score of 0.90, outperforming both UNet-only and FNO-only baselines."* 该结果是最直接的性能证据。

    Water depth estimation improves relative to hydrodynamic simulation benchmarks

    结论说明连续水动力变量也有优势：*"The model also showed superior performance in estimating water depth relative to hydrodynamic simulation benchmarks."* 具体数值在 IV-A 为 RMSE=0.21 m，但结论段未重复列出。

    Coupling deep learning with shallow-water physics enhances reliability and interpretability

    结论的学术判断为：*"coupling deep learning with shallow water physics can significantly enhance flood mapping reliability and improve the interpretability of remote sensing–derived hydrodynamic products."* 这里的可解释性来自输出变量符合守恒方程和物理关系，而非只是神经网络注意力或特征可视化。

    Future work focuses on non-steady dynamics, time-series imagery, and computational efficiency

    未来方向包括三点。原文写道：*"Future work will focus on relaxing the steady-state flow assumption, integrating time-series imagery, and optimizing computational efficiency for large-scale deployment."* 这对应从单时相准稳态模型走向动态洪水预报系统。

    ---

    Acknowledgment

    Funding support comes from Microsoft AFMR and NSF Award 2401942

    研究获得 Microsoft 与 NSF 支持。原文写道：*"This research article has been made possible partly with the support of Microsoft’s Accelerate Foundation Models Academic Research Initiative (AFMR) and in part by the National Science Foundation (NSF) Grant under Award 2401942."* 资金来源显示其与基础模型学术研究和美国国家科学基金项目相关。

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持 (Understanding & Nuance)

    1. 术语解析

    Physics-guided vs. physics-informed vs. physics-enforced

    Physics-guided 在该语境中表示物理方程作为软约束/正则项参与训练，而不是强制精确满足 PDE。原文中特别区分：*"Our approach adopts a physics-guided, not fully physics-enforced, strategy using residual penalties and mesh-free sampling."*

    微妙差别：

    • physics-informed：广义术语，表示机器学习模型纳入物理知识；
    • physics-guided：物理作为引导和约束，允许数据与物理之间折中；
    • physics-enforced：更强约束，通常要求解严格满足边界条件、初始条件或 PDE 残差趋近零。

    本研究选择 physics-guided，原因是高分辨率遥感网格、湿干界面、观测噪声使强约束训练容易不稳定。

    Depth-averaged shallow water equations

    Depth-averaged SWE 指将三维流体速度沿水深方向平均，得到二维平面上的水深 h 和水平速度 u,v。原文定义：*"assuming hydrostatic pressure and depth-averaged velocity."*

    学术含义是：洪水水体通常水平尺度远大于垂向水深，因此可忽略垂向速度结构，用二维方程近似水流。该假设适用于大多数河漫滩洪水，但不适合强三维湍流、跌水、闸门附近或局部急变流。

    Wet–dry fronts

    Wet–dry fronts 指淹没区与未淹没区的移动边界，即水深从正值接近零的位置。原文指出 PINNs 在此处存在困难：*"PINNs enforce PDE residuals, they suffer from slow convergence and instability near wet–dry fronts."*

    微妙之处在于：湿干界面既是图像分割边界，也是 PDE 数值求解难点。水深接近零时，Manning 摩阻项中出现 h⁻¹/³，速度、水深梯度和通量项容易数值不稳定。

    Fourier Neural Operator

    FNO 不是普通 CNN，而是学习从输入函数到输出函数的算子映射，通常在频域中保留若干 Fourier modes 来建模全局依赖。原文描述：*"operating in the frequency domain, learning low-frequency components that represent large-scale hydrodynamic patterns."*

    关键区别：

    • CNN 学习局部卷积核；
    • Transformer 学习 token 间注意力；
    • FNO 学习函数空间中的 PDE-like operator，可跨网格或分辨率泛化，但对高频边界细节较弱。

    Mass imbalance

    Mass imbalance 指预测流场中质量守恒偏差，即输入、输出和储水变化之间不平衡的比例。原文报告：*"relative mass imbalance of 2.1%."*

    在洪水预测中，低质量不平衡意味着模型没有凭空产生或消失大量水体。该指标比单纯 IoU 更接近水动力可信度。

    ---

    2. 疑难查证

    为什么二值洪水图不足以支持应急决策？

    二值洪水图只回答“哪里被淹”，不能回答“淹多深、流多快、危险程度多高”。应急调度需要判断道路是否可通行、房屋受损高度、人员涉水风险、堤防压力、下游到达时间。原文中的关键差异是：*"Sensors capture raw observations... while emergency response depends on water depth, surface elevation, and flow velocity."*

    因此，研究目标从 segmentation 升级为 hydraulic state estimation。

    为什么 UNet 和 FNO 必须结合？

    洪水预测同时需要两种能力：

    • 局部高频能力：识别建筑物边界、道路、窄沟渠、小尺度地形导致的水边界变化；
    • 全局低频能力：理解上游来水、下游排水、流域连通性、整体水面坡度。

    UNet 擅长第一类，FNO 擅长第二类。单独 UNet 容易“看图分割”，但缺少流域尺度水力传播；单独 FNO 容易捕获大趋势，但边界粗糙。结果支持这一点：UNet-only IoU=0.75，FNO-only IoU=0.77，Hybrid IoU=0.82±0.03。

    为什么物理残差能改善泛化？

    纯深度学习模型可能学习训练区域中的相关性，例如暗色 SAR 回波等于水体、低洼区域更可能淹没。但在新区域，散射条件、土地覆盖和传感器噪声会变化。SWE 残差提供一种跨区域更稳定的约束：水深、速度、坡度之间必须大致满足质量和动量守恒。

    原文机制是：*"The physics loss acts as a regularization term, constraining the solution space to physically plausible states."* 这相当于把无限可能的神经网络输出压缩到水动力可行空间中。

    为什么单时相影像要假设准稳态？

    单张 SAR/光学影像没有时间维度，无法直接计算 ∂t h、∂t(hu)、∂t(hv)。为使用 SWE，模型将时间导数设为零：*"For single-date SAR/optical snapshots, we set ∂t(·)=0."*

    这不是说真实洪水完全不变化，而是把影像时刻近似看作一个局部平衡状态。适用于缓慢扩展或接近峰值/退水阶段的洪水，不适合溃坝波、暴雨内涝快速汇流等强非稳态过程。

    为什么 HEC-RAS 参考数据既有价值也有限？

    HEC-RAS 是成熟水动力模拟工具，可提供水深和流速场作为监督或评估参考。文中使用它是因为：*"lack of observed field data for water depth and surface velocity."*

    但 HEC-RAS 不是现场真值。其结果依赖 DEM 精度、边界条件、粗糙系数、河道断面、降雨/流量输入。模型相对于 HEC-RAS 的低 RMSE 说明它学到了模拟水动力关系，但不能完全证明其现场水深精度达到同等水平。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联 (Synthesis & Novelty)

    1. 创新性判断

    Novelty 1: 从遥感二值洪水制图推进到 SWE-consistent 连续水动力状态估计

    过去 2–5 年大量洪水遥感深度学习工作集中于 SAR/optical flood segmentation，输出通常是二值 flood mask。该研究明确突破这一点：*"predicting continuous hydrodynamic fields rather than binary flood masks."*

    创新价值在于同时输出水深、自由水面高程、深度平均速度，并以 SWE 残差检查物理可行性。该方向更接近实际应急需求。

    Novelty 2: UNet–FNO 混合架构直接对应洪水过程的局部-全局多尺度结构

    近年 FNO 已用于快速洪水模拟，UNet 已广泛用于洪水分割，但二者在多模态遥感洪水水动力反演中的结合仍较新。该研究将 UNet 的边界细节能力与 FNO 的流域尺度算子学习结合：*"captures both local inundation patterns and large-scale flow dynamics."*

    这解决了单一 CNN 缺少长程水动力联系、单一 FNO 边界细节不足的问题。

    Novelty 3: 将真实 SAR-derived flood extent 作为观测同化约束，而非只做模拟代理

    许多神经水动力代理依赖预计算模拟库，学习 HEC-RAS 或其他水动力模型输入到输出的映射。该研究强调：*"Unlike pure emulators that rely solely on simulation data, our framework actively assimilates SAR-derived flood extent."*

    这点解决了静态水动力模型因过时 bathymetry、地形误差、灾时地物变化而错过真实边界的问题。

    Novelty 4: Physics-guided residual penalties 在高分辨率遥感网格上比标准 PINNs 更可扩展

    传统 PINN 在大网格、湿干界面和复杂边界上训练慢且不稳定。该研究采用软残差约束与 mesh-free sampling：*"using residual penalties and mesh-free sampling, enabling scalability to high-resolution imagery."*

    创新点不是提出全新 PDE，而是在遥感洪水高分辨率场景下选择更实用的物理引导范式。

    Novelty 5: SAR、光学、DEM 与 SWE source terms 的耦合更紧密

    多模态融合并非简单堆叠通道。DEM 派生特征进入 SWE 源项：*"DEM features inform SWE-based source terms (bed slope, friction)."* SAR 提供 flood extent 和可选速度 proxy，光学补充清空条件下的光谱线索。

    这种设计比一般 SAR+optical segmentation 更接近物理因果结构。

    ---

    2. 解决的前人问题

    Problem solved: 物理不可解释的 flood mask

    传统 UNet/DeepLab 等分割模型可以给出淹没范围，但难以解释水从哪里来、是否守恒、速度是否合理。SWE 残差让预测具有物理诊断指标：质量残差 0.03、动量残差 0.05、质量不平衡 2.1%。

    Problem solved: 纯模拟代理与真实观测脱节

    纯 HEC-RAS emulator 学习模拟结果，可能继承模拟中的地形、粗糙度和边界条件误差。SAR-derived flood extent 强迫模型尊重实际观测边界，缓解“模拟正确但现实错误”的问题。

    Problem solved: 单一模型尺度偏置

    UNet 偏局部，FNO 偏全局。混合模型在测试集上超过两者：Hybrid IoU=0.82±0.03、F1=0.90±0.02；UNet-only IoU=0.75、F1=0.85；FNO-only IoU=0.77、F1=0.87。

    Problem solved: 少监督环境下连续水深估计不稳定

    物理损失在标签稀缺时充当先验。消融结果显示，去除物理正则化使水深 RMSE 增加 18%，说明 SWE 约束对水深场稳定性具有实质贡献。

    ---

    3. 仍未完全解决的问题

    Field validation remains insufficient

    水深与流速评估依赖 HEC-RAS，不是实测水尺、无人机测深、ADCP 或现场速度观测。原文承认：*"Given the lack of observed field data for water depth and surface velocity."* 因而现实水动力精度仍需外部验证。

    Temporal dynamics remain simplified

    稳态或准稳态假设限制动态洪水模拟。原文承认：*"assumes steady-state flow and uniform hydrostatic pressure, which may limit its applicability during dynamic flood events."* 时间序列 SWE、降雨源项、边界流量条件仍未系统纳入。

    Experimental reporting lacks several reproducibility details

    文中未给出训练样本数量、影像数量、区域面积、空间分辨率、FNO Fourier modes、UNet depth、通道数、学习率、epoch、batch size、λ 权重、Manning n 数据源细节、bootstrap 重采样次数。结果可信但复现性仍受限制。

    Operational deployment remains computationally challenging

    模型面向大尺度部署，但原文承认：*"Computational demands also hinder large-scale real-time deployment."* FNO 与物理残差计算在高分辨率、多区域、近实时场景下仍需优化。

    阅读原文 ↗

  12. 12
    铁电 HfO2 薄膜异常尺寸效应起源#
    Origin of Reverse Size Effect in Ferroelectric Hafnia Thin Films#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 物理 / 凝聚态📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 Tianyuan Zhu, Jingxuan Li, Zuhuang Chen, Shi Liu🔥 AI 93

    💡 亮点：解析超薄 HfO2 面外晶格膨胀悖论。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题为什么铁电 HfO₂/HZO 超薄膜在厚度降至约 1 nm 甚至 0.6 nm 时仍保持铁电性，并且 d₁₁₁ 面间距随薄膜变薄反常增大？这一膨胀究竟代表极化增强，还是隐藏着相反的极化抑制机制？
    创新方法提出“退极化场诱导负纵向压电响应 + 正表面应力诱导厚度依赖应变”的双机制解释：残余退极化场抑制面外极位移，却因 HfO₂ 固有负 d₃₃ 使面外晶格膨胀；超薄表面正应力造成面内压缩，再经泊松效应进一步拉大 d₁₁₁。另提出“取向诱导超铁电性”：通过 (111) 取向降低面外极化分量，使开路薄膜无需电极筛选也能保持极化。
    工作流程以 HfO₂(111) 超薄 slab 为输入，构建不同厚度开路自由薄膜、graphene/HfO₂ 与 Ca₂N/HfO₂ 电容器；用 DFT 计算结构弛豫、d₁₁₁、局域极位移和退极化场，用 Berry phase/DFPT 得到极化与压电响应；用 LGD 自由能比较 (001)/(111) 开路极化稳定性；用表面弹性模型分离表面应力贡献；最后与 PLD 制备的 HZO 薄膜 d₁₁₁ 厚度趋势对照。
    关键结果HfO₂(111) 在开路条件下低至 0.6 nm 仍保留有限极化；退极化场将面外极位移 δ₁₁₁ 从体相 0.16 Å 压低到约 0.06 Å，而面内 δ₁₁₂̄ 仍接近 0.22 Å，说明 d₁₁₁ 膨胀与极化抑制共存。负有效压电系数 d₃₃eff ≈ −1.02 pm/V，与 d₁₁₁–电场斜率 −1.28 pm/V 接近；表面应力拟合为 σ = 0.38 eV/Å²。Ca₂N 电极可将退极化场从裸 slab 的 −12.8 MV/cm 过筛选到 +3.9 MV/cm，并恢复接近体相的极化性质。
    应用价值为超薄铁电存储器突破传统临界厚度提供晶向工程路径：选择 (111) 等降低面外极化投影的取向，可在纳米尺度维持铁电性；重新校正 HfO₂ 薄膜 XRD 中 d₁₁₁ 膨胀的物理解读，避免误判为极化增强；提出二维电子化物 Ca₂N 作为强筛选、晶格匹配的潜在电极材料，可用于高密度铁电电容器与存储器集成。

    第一部分：核心概览 (Overview)

    铁电铪氧薄膜的反常尺寸效应被归因于退极化场诱导的负纵向压电响应与表面应力驱动的厚度依赖应变的耦合，而非纳米尺度极化增强。DFT、LGD 与表面弹性模型共同表明，(111) 取向 HfO₂ 在开路边界下仍保持极化，体现取向诱导超铁电性。该机制还可推广至 PbTiO₃，为突破传统钙钛矿铁电薄膜临界厚度提供取向工程路径，并提出二维电子化物 Ca₂N 作为近理想电极材料。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Origin of Anomalous Size Effects in Ferroelectric Hafnia Thin Films》（None，）

    背景

    HfO₂ 基铁电薄膜在约 1 nm 甚至亚纳米尺度仍能保持铁电性，并在厚度减小时出现 d₁₁₁ 面间距增大。这一行为不同于传统钙钛矿铁电体中由退极化场导致的临界厚度效应。既有解释包括相变增强极化、巨大面内应变、平带声子、极性/反极性模耦合，但均难以同时解释无临界厚度与面外晶格膨胀。

    方法

    采用 DFT 计算 HfO₂(111) 开路自由薄膜、石墨烯/HfO₂ 与 Ca₂N/HfO₂ 电容器；用 Berry phase 计算极化、DFPT 计算压电张量；建立 LGD 自由能模型 分析开路退极化能；建立 表面弹性模型 拟合表面应力诱导的面内压缩应变；通过 PLD 制备不同厚度 Hf₀.₅Zr₀.₅O₂ 薄膜用于实验对比。

    结果

    HfO₂(111) 在开路条件下仍保持有限极化，0.6 nm 自由薄膜也未失去铁电性。退极化场将面外极位移 δ₁₁₁ 从体相 0.16 Å 降至约 0.06 Å，而面内 δ₁₁₂̄ 保持约 0.22 Å。与此同时 d₁₁₁ 反常增大。Ca₂N 电极可将退极化场从裸 slab 的 −12.8 MV/cm 过筛选至 +3.9 MV/cm，并恢复接近体相的极化性质。

    讨论

    d₁₁₁ 膨胀不是极化增强证据，而是与极化抑制共存。机制包括：残余退极化场作用于 HfO₂ 固有 负 d₃₃，使极化越弱、面外晶格越大；正表面应力 σ = 0.38 eV/Å² 在超薄极限诱导面内压缩，经泊松效应进一步产生面外膨胀。LGD 模型显示，(111) 取向降低面外极化分量，从而降低退极化能，使 HfO₂ 和 PbTiO₃ 均可表现开路稳定极化。

    局限

    自由表面应力代表理想化上限，真实界面会产生不同界面应力；Ca₂N/HfO₂ 界面可能存在 charge spill-out，但未深入展开；实验对比主要集中于 d₁₁₁ 厚度趋势，未提供系统统计显著性检验；部分大厚度无筛选/部分筛选曲线为渐近示意。

    结论

    铁电 HfO₂ 薄膜反常尺寸效应源于负压电响应 + 表面应力，而非增强极化或巨大外延应变。(111) 取向产生的取向诱导超铁电性可消除临界厚度限制，并可推广到传统钙钛矿。Ca₂N 是兼具晶格匹配与强筛选能力的潜在电极材料。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析 (Section-by-Section Condensing)

    Abstract

    • Anomalous expansion is coupled to suppressed polarization

    HfO₂ 超薄膜中面外晶格常数随厚度减小而增大，这一现象并不代表 out-of-plane polarization 增强，而是与其被抑制相耦合。摘要直接指出核心反转：*"this lattice expansion is counterintuitively coupled to a suppressed out-of-plane polarization."* 这一判断推翻了将 d₁₁₁ 增大直接解释为铁电增强的常见思路。

    • Two mechanisms generate lattice expansion

    反常膨胀来自两个可分离机制：residual depolarization field 触发的 negative longitudinal piezoelectric response，以及薄膜变薄时增强的 positive surface stress。核心表述为：*"two mechanisms behind this expansion: a negative longitudinal piezoelectric response to the residual depolarization field and a positive surface stress that becomes significant at reduced thickness."*

    • Orientation determines open-circuit ferroelectric stability

    (111) 取向 HfO₂ 在 open-circuit conditions 下仍可支持面外极化，而 (001) 取向则趋于非极性基态。摘要给出强对比：*"(111)-oriented HfO₂ films can support out-of-plane polarization even under open-circuit conditions, in contrast to (001) films that stabilize a nonpolar ground state."*

    • Orientation-induced hyperferroelectricity is proposed

    orientation-induced hyperferroelectricity 被定义为无需电极筛选仍可保留极化的取向工程机制。关键判断为：*"This behavior points to the emergence of orientation-induced hyperferroelectricity, an unrecognized mechanism that enables polarization persistence through orientation engineering without electrode screening."*

    • Ca₂N provides a device-oriented electrode solution

    二维电子化物 Ca₂N 被识别为近理想电极，可在超薄电容器中恢复 HfO₂ 的铁电性质。摘要结论为：*"the two-dimensional electride Ca₂N as a near-ideal electrode that fully restores the ferroelectric properties of HfO₂ in ultrathin capacitors."*

    ---

    Main text

    • HfO₂ challenges the conventional critical-thickness paradigm

    传统钙钛矿薄膜中，厚度降低会增强 depolarization field，最终导致极化消失；HfO₂ 则在约 1 nm 仍保持稳定极化。关键背景为：*"Ferroelectric hafnia (HfO₂) has emerged as a promising candidate for high-density ferroelectric memories, owing to its stable polarization down to one-nanometer scale"*，并且传统机制为：*"the depolarization field in a thin film increases with decreasing thickness under the imperfect screening hypothesis, resulting in a critical thickness below which polarization disappears."*

    • The d₁₁₁ expansion is experimentally central but theoretically unresolved

    (111) 取向铪氧薄膜中，厚度越小 d₁₁₁ spacing 越大，是反常尺寸效应的直接结构证据。核心表述为：*"A direct manifestation of this size effect is the increase in the d₁₁₁ spacing with decreasing thickness in (111)-oriented hafnia thin films."* 这一效应被归入钙钛矿中不存在的异常行为：*"both behaviors constitute anomalous size effects absent in perovskite ferroelectrics."*

    • Phase-transition interpretation is structurally problematic

    将 d₁₁₁ 增大解释为从顺电四方相 T, P4₂/nmc 到铁电正交相 O, Pca2₁ 的相变并不充分，因为两相晶格参数非常接近，XRD 峰几乎重叠。关键证据为：*"the ferroelectric O and paraelectric T phases of HfO₂ exhibit nearly identical lattice parameters, which typically results in almost completely overlapping XRD reflections for the O (111) and T (111) planes."*

    • Large-strain explanation lacks experimental support

    既有理论要求约 3.2% tensile 或 5.8% compressive 的巨大面内双轴应变，但典型 domain-matching epitaxy 会释放错配应变。直接数值为：*"large in-plane biaxial strains, approximately 3.2% tensile or 5.8% compressive"*；反证机制为：*"the resulting m/n domain-matching arrangements effectively reduces the lattice mismatch and alleviates epitaxial strain."*

    • Previous microscopic theories do not fully address the anomaly

    flat phonon band theory 可解释局域偶极的弱横向耦合，却不能直接解释面外退极化场抗性；极性模与反极性模耦合机制也未预测无临界厚度或 d₁₁₁ 膨胀。关键引述为：*"This theory mainly explains the weak coupling of local dipoles in directions perpendicular to the polarization, rather than directly addressing the film’s resilience to the out-of-plane depolarization field."* 以及：*"this mechanism does not explicitly predict the absence of a critical thickness or explain the out-of-plane lattice expansion."*

    • Most prior theory uses [001], whereas experiments are mostly (111)

    既有模型常聚焦极化轴沿 [001] 的晶胞，但实验薄膜多数为 (111) orientation，导致解释适用性受限。关键表述为：*"these theoretical studies have largely focused on unit cells with polarization axis along the [001] direction, whereas experimentally realized films are most often grown in the (111) orientation."*

    • DFT + LGD + surface elasticity forms the central strategy

    研究框架由 density functional theory, Landau–Ginzburg–Devonshire theory, surface elastic model 构成，用于分解反常尺寸效应来源。核心方法语句为：*"we integrate density functional theory (DFT) calculations with Landau–Ginzburg–Devonshire (LGD) theory and surface elastic model analysis to elucidate the origin of the experimentally observed anomalous size effects."*

    • HfO₂(111) slabs are built from stoichiometric [111] layers

    氟石结构沿 [111] 由化学计量层堆叠，因此构建不同层数 HfO₂(111) slabs 研究厚度效应。关键基础为：*"As the fluorite structure consists of stoichiometric layers stacked along the [111] crystallographic direction, we construct HfO₂ (111) slabs with varying numbers of such layers."*

    • The four-layer slab defines the thinnest bulk-like interior

    四层 slab 厚度为 0.9 nm，是具有清晰 bulk-like interior 的最薄构型。局域极位移 δ 定义为氧原子相对周围 Hf₄ tetrahedron 中心的位移；bulk region 由顶部和底部次表面 Hf 层限定。关键引述为：*"the four-layer slab of 0.9 nm represents the thinnest configuration with a well-defined bulk-like interior."*

    • Polar displacement is evaluated excluding surface layers

    为降低表面伪影，净极位移只对 bulk region 中氧原子的 δ 求平均，不含表面层；d₁₁₁ 定义为沿 [111] 相邻 Hf 平面的垂直距离。关键方法为：*"excluding surface layers to minimize surface-related artifacts"*，以及：*"the interplanar lattice spacing d₁₁₁ is defined as the vertical separation between neighboring Hf atomic planes along the [111] direction."*

    • Depolarization suppresses out-of-plane displacement from 0.16 Å to 0.06 Å

    开路无筛选退极化场显著压低 δ₁₁₁：从体相 0.16 Å 降至 0.06 Å。原始数值为：*"the out-of-plane polar displacement, δ₁₁₁, reduces from its bulk value of 0.16 Å to just 0.06 Å."*

    • In-plane polar displacement remains near 0.22 Å

    与 δ₁₁₁ 不同，δ₁₁₂̄ 基本不受退极化场影响，保持接近体相 0.22 Å。关键证据为：*"the in-plane component, δ₁₁₂̄, remains largely unaffected and close to its bulk value of 0.22 Å."*

    • Suppression is driven by depolarization rather than in-plane strain

    fix-IP 与 relax-IP 两种设置下极位移几乎一致，说明 δ₁₁₁ 抑制主要来自退极化场，而非面内应变。原句为：*"the polar displacement values remain nearly identical in the fix-IP and relax-IP configurations"*，并明确结论：*"the suppression of δ₁₁₁ is primarily driven by the depolarization field rather than in-plane strain."*

    • Fixed in-plane slabs show a thickness-independent d₁₁₁ offset of ≈0.03 Å

    在 fix-IP 条件下，d₁₁₁ 相对体相 2.96 Å 有约 0.03 Å 的恒定膨胀，且不随厚度收敛。关键数值为：*"d₁₁₁ exhibits a constant expansion of ≈0.03 Å above the bulk value (2.96 Å)."* 其物理归因是：*"it can be unambiguously attributed to the presence of the depolarization field."*

    • HfO₂(111) differs from BaTiO₃-like perovskites

    BaTiO₃ 等传统钙钛矿中，界面势降近似厚度无关，退极化场随厚度减小按反比增强；HfO₂(111) 的超铁电特征使退极化场近似厚度无关。关键对比为：*"This behavior differs fundamentally from conventional perovskite ferroelectrics such as BaTiO₃"*，以及：*"HfO₂ (111) exhibits a hyperferroelectric character, resulting in a nearly thickness-independent depolarization field and d₁₁₁ under different screening conditions."*

    • Relaxed in-plane slabs add a surface-stress-driven thickness dependence

    relax-IP 条件下 d₁₁₁ 进一步增大，并与厚度反相关，归因于表面应力诱导的面内应变。关键表述为：*"d₁₁₁ increases even further"*，并且：*"the magnitude of this additional expansion is inversely correlated with film thickness."* 物理来源为：*"confirming its origin in surface stress, an intrinsic mechanical tension arising from the distinct atomic environment at the film surfaces."*

    • Experimental d₁₁₁ expansion should not be read as enhanced polarization

    开路计算直接澄清实验反常膨胀的物理含义：不是极化增强或应变驱动铁电性，而是与极化显著抑制共存。关键结论为：*"the experimentally observed out-of-plane lattice expansion should not be interpreted as evidence of enhanced polarization or strain-driven ferroelectricity."* 以及：*"it coexists with a significantly suppressed polar displacement."*

    • Depolarization-field contribution is thickness-independent under OCBC

    开路下退极化场满足 ℰd = −Ps/ϵ，Ps 与 ℰd 在电学平衡中自洽确定，因此近似厚度无关，类似理想平行板电容器。关键公式与解释为：*"ℰd = −Ps/ϵ"*，以及：*"both ℰd and Ps are determined self-consistently at electrical equilibrium under OCBC and are therefore nearly thickness-independent."*

    • Depolarization is not a surface chemical artifact

    退极化场来自极化束缚电荷未完全筛选，而非特定表面化学；非极性 P4₂/nmc slab 同表面终止但无势降。关键证据为：*"the depolarization field originates from the incomplete screening of polarization-induced bound charges"*，并且：*"the nonpolar P4₂/nmc slab with identical surface termination exhibits a symmetric potential profile and no depolarization field."*

    • Free-standing HfO₂(111) remains polar down to 0.6 nm

    最强结论之一是，在开路自由薄膜中，厚度低至 0.6 nm 仍有有限极化。原句为：*"a finite polarization persists in free-standing HfO₂ (111) slabs as thin as 0.6 nm."* 因而：*"fundamentally avoid the conventional critical thickness limit."*

    • Ca₂N is selected as an ideal screening electrode

    通过 Computational 2D Materials Database 搜索，二维电子化物 Ca₂N 因六角近似对称性和与 HfO₂(111) 表面良好晶格匹配被选中。关键表述为：*"we identify the two-dimensional electride Ca₂N as an ideal electrode, given its compatible hexagonal-like symmetry and excellent lattice match with the HfO₂ (111) surface."*

    • Capacitor models span strong negative field to overscreening

    裸 HfO₂ slab、HfO₂/graphene、HfO₂/Ca₂N 构成筛选强度序列。面内失配分别为 Ca₂N (1.1%, −0.8%)，graphene (−1.5%, −3.3%)；退极化场从裸 slab −12.8 MV/cm，到 graphene −10.4 MV/cm，到 Ca₂N +3.9 MV/cm。关键数值为：*"(η[1̄10], η[01̄1]) = (1.1%, −0.8%) for the (2×2) Ca₂N and (−1.5%, −3.3%) for the (3×3) graphene"*，以及：*"from strong negative fields in the bare slab (−12.8 MV/cm), to partial screening with graphene (−10.4 MV/cm), and finally to overscreening with Ca₂N (+3.9 MV/cm)."*

    • Ca₂N screening involves enhanced interfacial charge transfer

    Ca₂N 的优越筛选来自界面电荷转移增强与短筛选长度，并可能类似金属/铁电界面的 charge spill-out。关键表述为：*"enhanced charge transfer and a short screening length at the HfO₂/Ca₂N interface."* 以及：*"suggestive of a charge spill-out effect."*

    • Screening restores δ₁₁₁ but reduces d₁₁₁

    随筛选增强，ℰd 由负趋近零，δ₁₁₁ 恢复体相值；同时 d₁₁₁ 反而降低，证明极化越强晶格越短。关键证据为：*"δ₁₁₁, is progressively restored to its intrinsic bulk value"*，以及：*"the out-of-plane lattice spacing, d₁₁₁, systematically decreases."*

    • Negative effective piezoelectricity quantitatively matches DFT slope

    HfO₂ 的固有 negative longitudinal piezoelectric coefficient 导致 [111] 方向负有效压电响应。实验和理论已有支持；该工作计算得 d₃₃eff = −1.02 pm/V，与 d₁₁₁–ℰd 线性区斜率 ∂ηOP/∂ℰd = −1.28 pm/V 接近。关键引述为：*"HfO₂’s intrinsic negative longitudinal piezoelectric coefficient (d₃₃ < 0)"*，以及：*"d₃₃eff = −1.02 pm/V"*，*"∂ηOP/∂ℰd = −1.28 pm/V."*

    • Surface elasticity model separates the second contribution

    表面应力效应用总弹性能表示：

    Uslab = 1/2 C ηIP² A t + 2A(σ ηIP + 1/2 S ηIP²)。

    原式为：*"Uslab=Ubulk+2Aγ=1/2 CηIP²At+2A(σηIP+1/2SηIP²)."* 该模型将体相弹性能与两侧表面能相加。

    • Fitted surface parameters are σ = 0.38 eV/Å² and S = −4.78 eV/Å²

    表面应力与表面弹性常数由四层 OCBC slab 拟合得到，且为包含退极化场影响的有效参数。关键数值为：*"σ = 0.38 eV/Å² and S = −4.78 eV/Å² are fitted directly from our OCBC slab calculations at a thickness of four layers."* 物理限定为：*"effective parameters that implicitly capture the influence of the depolarization field on the surface energetics."*

    • Positive surface stress induces compressive in-plane strain

    最小化总能得 ηIP(t)=−2σ/(Ct+2S)。正 σ 预测超薄膜强面内压缩，厚度增加后衰减。关键公式为：*"ηIP(t)=−2σ/(Ct+2S)."* 结论为：*"Since the DFT-calculated surface stress σ is positive, the model predicts a compressive in-plane strain that is most pronounced in ultrathin films and vanishes with increasing thickness."*

    • The full strain model has Poisson and piezoelectric terms

    总面外应变分解为 ηOP(t)=−ν ηIP(t)+ηOP(ℰd)：第一项是表面应力诱导面内应变经泊松效应造成的厚度依赖膨胀；第二项是残余退极化场通过负压电效应造成的筛选依赖膨胀。原式为：*"ηOP(t)=−νηIP(t)+ηOP(ℰd)."*

    • Perfect, partial, and no screening define lower, intermediate, and upper bounds

    完全筛选对应体相无退极化场，仅保留泊松膨胀下限；graphene 部分筛选居中；自由 slab 无筛选为上限。关键表述为：*"The no-screening case ... represents the upper bound"*，*"perfect screening scenario (ℰd = 0), where the piezoelectric term vanishes"*，以及：*"The resulting curve ... lies neatly between the perfect- and no-screening limits."*

    • Experimental d₁₁₁ lies within theoretical bounds

    文献 Ref. [24] 与当前实验测得的 Hf₀.₅Zr₀.₅O₂ d₁₁₁ 厚度依赖落在自由 slab 无筛选上限与体相完全筛选下限之间。核心证据为：*"the observed thickness dependence of d₁₁₁ falls within the range bounded by our theoretical predictions for the free-standing slab (no screening) and the bulk (perfect screening) limit."*

    • Hyperferroelectricity is defined by stable polarization under OCBC

    hyperferroelectric 的判据是开路边界下仍有稳定自发极化。关键定义为：*"A hyperferroelectric is defined by its ability to maintain a stable, spontaneous polarization even under OCBC."*

    • LGD free energy adds depolarization energy penalty

    开路条件下位移场 D = 0，退极化场为 ℰd(λ)=−Ps(λ)/ϵ₀[1+χe(λ)]；代回得到自由能中正的退极化能罚项。关键公式为：*"D=ϵ₀[1+χe(λ)]ℰd(λ)+Ps(λ)=0"*，以及：*"F(λ)=U(λ)+Ω(λ)Ps²(λ)/2ϵ₀[1+χe(λ)]²."*

    • HfO₂(001) becomes nonpolar under OCBC

    对 HfO₂(001)，极化完全面外，退极化能最大，超过体相双阱深度 27 meV/atom，使非极性相成为基态。关键数值与结论为：*"This penalty completely overwhelms the intrinsic double-well potential with a well depth of 27 meV/atom, stabilizing the nonpolar phase as the ground state."*

    • HfO₂(111) preserves a shallow double well

    (111) 取向只有 Ps 的 [111] 分量贡献退极化能，因此开路自由能仍有双阱并保持铁电基态。关键表述为：*"only the [111] component of Ps contributes to the depolarization energy"*，以及：*"exhibits a shallower, yet still distinct, double-well potential that preserves the ferroelectric ground state."*

    • PbTiO₃ generalizes the orientation principle

    LGD 分析预测 PbTiO₃(001) 开路非极性，但 PbTiO₃(111) 可保持稳定极化；直接 DFT 计算 0.9 nm PbO₃-terminated PbTiO₃(111) slab 证实有强面外极位移。关键证据为：*"a PbTiO₃ (001) film becomes nonpolar under OCBC"*，*"a PbTiO₃ (111) film ... stable polarized ground state"*，以及：*"a PbO₃-terminated PbTiO₃ (111) slab of 0.9 nm ... relaxes to a structure with robust out-of-plane polar displacements."*

    • Orientation engineering can eliminate the critical thickness limit

    选择降低面外极化分量的晶向，可使薄膜无需筛选电极仍保留极化，从而有效消除临界厚度限制。关键总结为：*"By selecting a crystallographic orientation that reduces out-of-plane polarization, ferroelectric thin films can retain polarization without screening electrodes, effectively eliminating the critical thickness limit."*

    • Final physical resolution combines negative piezoelectricity and surface stress

    结论将反常尺寸效应的根源明确为两个机制的相互作用：negative longitudinal piezoelectric response 与 positive surface stress。总结性原句为：*"This expansion originates from the interplay between two distinct mechanisms: a negative longitudinal piezoelectric response to the residual depolarization field, and a positive surface stress that becomes increasingly pronounced at reduced thickness."*

    ---

    Methods

    #### Density functional theory calculations

    • DFT implementation and functionals are explicitly specified

    所有第一性原理计算使用 VASP 与 PAW 方法；HfO₂ 用 PBE，PbTiO₃ 用 PBEsol。关键方法为：*"DFT calculations were performed using the Vienna ab initio simulation package (VASP) with the projector augmented-wave (PAW) method."* 以及：*"The Perdew–Burke–Ernzerhof (PBE) and PBE for solids (PBEsol) exchange correlation functionals were employed for HfO₂ and PbTiO₃, respectively."*

    • Numerical convergence settings are defined

    平面波截断能为 600 eV；k 点为 HfO₂ 4×4×4、PbTiO₃ 6×6×6、HfO₂(111) slabs/capacitors 3×3×1；力收敛阈值 0.01 eV/Å。关键数值为：*"The plane-wave cutoff was set to 600 eV."*，*"4×4×4 for HfO₂, 6×6×6 for PbTiO₃, and 3×3×1 for HfO₂ (111) slabs and capacitors."*，以及：*"residual atomic forces were below 0.01 eV/Å."*

    • Polarization and piezoelectric coefficients use standard first-principles formalisms

    极化由 Berry phase approach 获得，压电系数由 DFPT 获得，slab 计算沿表面法向使用偶极修正。关键方法为：*"Dipole corrections were applied along the surface normal in slab calculations."*，*"Polarization was determined using the Berry phase approach"*，以及：*"piezoelectric coefficients were obtained via density functional perturbation theory (DFPT)."*

    #### Pulsed laser deposition of HZO thin films

    • Epitaxial HZO films are grown on LSMO-buffered STO

    不同厚度外延 Hf₀.₅Zr₀.₅O₂ 薄膜通过 PLD 生长在 La₀.₆₇Sr₀.₃₃MnO₃-buffered SrTiO₃(001) 单晶衬底上。关键实验描述为：*"Epitaxial Hf₀.₅Zr₀.₅O₂ (HZO) thin films of various thicknesses were grown on La₀.₆₇Sr₀.₃₃MnO₃ (LSMO)-buffered SrTiO₃ (001) single-crystal substrates by pulsed laser deposition."*

    • LSMO bottom electrode deposition conditions are fixed

    LSMO 底电极厚度 10 nm，沉积温度 700 ℃，激光重复频率 3 Hz，能量密度 0.8 J/cm²。关键数值为：*"A 10-nm-thick LSMO bottom electrode was first deposited at 700 ℃ with a laser repetition rate of 3 Hz and a fluence of 0.8 J/cm²."*

    • HZO deposition and cooling conditions are specified

    HZO 层在 600 ℃、2 Hz、1.3 J/cm² 下沉积，随后在 10⁴ Pa 静态氧压下以 10 ℃/min 冷却至室温。关键数值为：*"The ferroelectric HZO layer was subsequently deposited at 600 ℃ using a repetition rate of 2 Hz and a fluence of 1.3 J/cm²."* 以及：*"cooled to room temperature at a rate of 10 ℃ per minute under a static oxygen pressure of 10⁴ Pa."*

    • Pt top electrodes define electrical test geometry

    Pt 顶电极为圆形，直径 12.5 μm，厚度约 100 nm，通过光刻与磁控溅射制备。关键描述为：*"circular platinum (Pt) top electrodes (12.5 μm in diameter, ∼100 nm in thickness) were patterned by photolithography and deposited via magnetron sputtering."*
