    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持 (Understanding & Nuance)

    1. 术语解析

    • Anomalous size effects

    字面是“反常尺寸效应”，语境中专指 HfO₂ 薄膜在变薄时出现两种违反传统预期的行为：一是没有明显铁电临界厚度，二是 d₁₁₁ 面间距随厚度减小而增大。微妙之处在于，“anomalous” 不是泛指异常，而是相对于传统钙钛矿铁电薄膜的尺寸标度规律异常。

    • Depolarization field

    指极化在表面/界面产生束缚电荷后，由未完全筛选电荷形成的反向电场。对普通铁电薄膜，它通常抑制极化并导致临界厚度。这里的关键细节是 HfO₂(111) 中退极化场仍抑制 δ₁₁₁，但不完全消灭极化。

    • Negative longitudinal piezoelectric response

    普通直觉中，极化增强常伴随同向晶格伸长；但 HfO₂ 的 d₃₃ < 0 意味着沿极化方向施加有效场或增强极化时，纵向晶格反而缩短。这里正是该负号导致“极化被抑制—晶格反而膨胀”的反直觉关系。

    • Surface stress

    不是外加应力，而是表面原子环境不同导致的内禀表面机械张力。对于超薄膜，表面积/体积比高，表面应力可诱导显著面内应变，并通过泊松效应改变面外间距。这里 σ = 0.38 eV/Å² 为正，导致面内压缩和面外膨胀。

    • Orientation-induced hyperferroelectricity

    “超铁电性”通常指开路条件下仍能稳定极化；“取向诱导”强调材料本身在某一取向下因面外极化分量降低，从而减小退极化能罚项。HfO₂(111) 与 PbTiO₃(111) 的稳定极化并非来自电极筛选，而来自晶向几何投影降低退极化惩罚。

    2. 疑难查证

    • 为什么 d₁₁₁ 增大不等于极化增强？

    对许多钙钛矿铁电体，极化增强常伴随 c 轴伸长，因此 XRD 面间距变大容易被解释为铁电增强。但 HfO₂ 的关键差异在于 负纵向压电系数。当退极化场抑制面外极化时，负压电耦合使面外晶格反而变长。因此 d₁₁₁ 增大与 δ₁₁₁ 减小可以同时发生，不矛盾。

    • 为什么 (111) 取向能避免临界厚度，而 (001) 取向不能？

    开路退极化能主要惩罚面外极化分量。(001) 薄膜中极化几乎完全沿法向，退极化能最大，足以抹平 27 meV/atom 的双阱势，使非极性相稳定。(111) 中自发极化相对表面法向有几何投影，只有 [111] 分量贡献退极化能，因此能罚降低，双阱虽变浅但仍存在。

    • 表面应力如何导致 d₁₁₁ 随厚度减小而增大？

    表面能中含 σ ηIP 项。正 σ 使自由薄膜通过面内压缩降低总能，且 ηIP(t)=−2σ/(Ct+2S)，厚度 t 越小，表面项相对于体项越大，面内压缩越强。泊松效应使面内压缩转化为面外拉伸，因此 d₁₁₁ 在超薄膜中更大。

    • Ca₂N 为什么比 graphene 更接近理想电极？

    graphene 只将退极化场从 −12.8 MV/cm 降至 −10.4 MV/cm，筛选有限；Ca₂N 则产生 +3.9 MV/cm 的过筛选，说明界面电荷足以过度补偿极化束缚电荷。其二维电子化物性质提供可迁移阴离子电子，并与 HfO₂(111) 表面具有良好晶格与对称匹配。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联 (Synthesis & Novelty)

    1. 创新性判断

    • 从“极化增强”转向“极化抑制伴随晶格膨胀”

    近年关于 HfO₂ 超薄铁电性的实验常将厚度减小时 d₁₁₁ 增大解释为铁电性增强或相结构转变。该工作给出相反解释：d₁₁₁ 膨胀与 δ₁₁₁ 从 0.16 Å 降至 0.06 Å 同时发生，因而不是增强极化证据。这一点直接改变了对 HfO₂ 纳米尺度结构表征的判读逻辑。

    • 首次将反常尺寸效应分解为两个可量化机制

    过去 2–5 年内的相关理论多集中于 flat phonon band、局域偶极、反极性模耦合或应变稳定相，但未能同时解释 d₁₁₁ 膨胀、无临界厚度和开路极化残留。该工作用 DFT + 表面弹性模型将膨胀拆成：厚度近似无关的退极化场/负压电项，以及厚度依赖的表面应力/泊松项，并用 σ = 0.38 eV/Å²、S = −4.78 eV/Å²、d₃₃eff = −1.02 pm/V 等参数实现定量闭环。

    • 提出取向诱导超铁电性机制

    超铁电性过去通常被视为材料内禀纵向光学模不稳定或特殊电学边界下的性质。这里的关键新意是：即使常规铁电材料 PbTiO₃，也可通过 (111) 取向降低面外极化投影，在开路条件下保留极化。这把“超铁电性”从材料筛选问题扩展为“晶向设计问题”。

    • 解决了 (001) 理论与 (111) 实验之间的错位

    既有 HfO₂ 理论常以 [001] 极化轴为主，而高质量外延 HfO₂/HZO 实验常见 (111) 取向。该工作直接建模 HfO₂(111) slab，并解释 d₁₁₁ 面间距这一实验最相关可观测量，增强了理论与实验结构表征之间的对应性。

    • 提出 Ca₂N 作为面向器件的二维电极方案

    金属电极筛选不足一直是超薄铁电电容器的核心问题。二维电子化物 Ca₂N 不仅晶格/对称性匹配 HfO₂(111)，还可将退极化场从裸 slab 的 −12.8 MV/cm 转为 +3.9 MV/cm，接近完全恢复体相铁电性质。这提供了从机制理解到材料集成的具体路径。

    • 对传统钙钛矿临界厚度问题给出非传统解决方案

    Junquera–Ghosez 以来，钙钛矿铁电薄膜临界厚度通常通过改善电极筛选、界面工程或应变调控解决。该工作展示 PbTiO₃(111) 在 0.9 nm slab 中可保持稳健面外极位移，说明合适取向本身可降低退极化能罚项，从几何上绕开临界厚度限制。

    阅读原文 ↗
    原文链接页内定位
  13. 13
    铬硫卤 Janus 单层高温铁磁体#
    Chromium chalcohalide Janus monolayer ferromagnets with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy and high Curie temperature#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 物理 / 凝聚态📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 M. Bosnar, J. M. Lendinez, A. Yu. Vyazovskaya, I. Yu. Sklyadneva, R. Heid, S. V. Eremeev, U. Atxitia, S. Gallego, E. V. Chulkov, A. Arnau, M. M. Otrokov🔥 AI 90

    💡 亮点：CrXY Janus 单层兼具垂直各向异性。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题如何在 CrXY（X=S/Se/Te，Y=Cl/Br/I）Janus 铬硫族卤化物单层中，可靠筛选出同时具备动力学稳定、铁磁交换、垂直磁各向异性和高居里温度的二维铁磁体；重点解决以往研究忽略 1H 相、偶极形状各向异性和真实有限温度磁性的误判风险。
    创新方法将 1T 八面体相与 1H 三角棱柱相放入同一筛选框架，并把 SOC 磁晶各向异性与偶极-偶极形状各向异性相加判断真实 PMA；再结合 DFT+U 稳健性测试、DMI 计算和原子自旋动力学模拟，把“看似高温铁磁”区分为“均匀 PMA 铁磁体”与“手性磁畴/skyrmion 候选体”。
    工作流程输入 18 种 CrXY Janus 单层组合与 1T/1H 两类结构；先用声子谱筛除动力学不稳定相，再比较 1T/1H 总能；随后用 DFT+U 计算 FM/AFM 能量差并映射交换参数，加入 SOC 计算面内/面外能量差，同时叠加偶极形状各向异性得到真实易轴；对候选体系计算 DMI，最后将 DFT 参数送入 ASD/LLG 模拟输出居里温度和磁畴纹理。
    关键结果除 1H-CrTeY 外多数体系动力学稳定，且 1T 相普遍比 1H 相低能至少 0.55 eV/f.u.；所有稳定体系具有最近邻铁磁耦合，交换强度通常比单层 CrI3 高 3–5 倍；稳健 PMA 主要集中在 CrSI 与 CrSeI；筛选出 1T-CrSI、1H-CrSI、1H-CrSeI，其中 1H-CrSI 的 TC 达 370–410 K，超过室温；1T-CrSeI 因较强 DMI 在零场形成虫状磁畴，外加垂直磁场可稳定 skyrmion。
    应用价值1H-CrSI 提供室温以上二维 Janus PMA 铁磁候选，可用于非易失自旋电子器件和垂直磁化存储；CrSI/CrSeI 的反演对称性破缺和 SOC 可服务于 Rashba 自旋调控、DMI 手性磁纹理与 skyrmion 器件；CrXY 还可作为范德华异质结构功能层，用于调控 BiTeI Rashba 表面态或增强 MnBi2Te4 拓扑磁性薄膜。

    第一部分：核心概览

    二维 CrXY Janus 铬硫族卤化物单层 被系统重估为兼具 本征反演对称性破缺、铁磁交换、垂直磁各向异性、高居里温度 的候选磁体。核心贡献在于同时比较 1T/1H 多晶型、显式纳入 偶极-偶极形状各向异性、考察 Hubbard (Uₑff) 稳健性，并用 DFT+原子自旋动力学 筛选出 1T-CrSI、1H-CrSI、1H-CrSeI。其中 1H-CrSI 预测 (T_C=370–410) K，具备室温二维铁磁应用潜力。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Chromium chalcohalide Janus monolayer ferromagnets with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy and high Curie temperature》（None，）

    背景

    二维磁体在有限温度下维持长程磁有序需要 易轴磁各向异性；Janus 单层因上下表面元素不同而天然破缺反演对称性，可诱导 Bychkov-Rashba 效应、DMI、压电性 等功能。CrXY 单层此前被预测为高温铁磁体，但 1H 相、形状各向异性、真实居里温度 等关键问题仍未充分解决。

    方法

    采用 DFT/GGA+(U)、声子谱、磁交换映射、SOC 磁各向异性计算、DMI 计算与 大规模原子自旋动力学 ASD。考察 (Uₑff=2.1,3.0,4.0) eV；结构包括 1T 八面体配位 与 1H 三角棱柱配位。

    结果

    除 1H-CrTeY 外，其余体系动力学稳定；1T 相能量普遍低于 1H 相至少 0.55 eV/f.u.。所有动力学稳定体系均表现 最近邻铁磁耦合。稳健 面外磁各向异性 仅出现在 CrSI 与 CrSeI 的若干 1T/1H 构型中。居里温度预测：1T-CrSI ≥210 K，1H-CrSeI 235–260 K，1H-CrSI 370–410 K。

    讨论

    PMA 来自 单离子各向异性 与 各向异性交换 的建设性叠加，并需克服倾向于面内磁化的 偶极-偶极相互作用。1T-CrSeI 中较强 DMI 导致零场 虫状磁畴，外加垂直磁场可稳定 skyrmions。

    局限

    精确 (Uₑff) 值未知；部分性质对 (Uₑff) 可能敏感。1H 相虽具潜在高 (T_C)，但能量显著高于 1T 相，实验合成可能依赖非平衡条件。所给内容未完整呈现 III.2.2 之后的具体数值表与后续全部章节。

    结论

    最有前景的二维 Janus 铁磁体为 1T-CrSI、1H-CrSI、1H-CrSeI；其中 1H-CrSI 兼具 PMA 与 室温以上 (T_C)。CrXY 单层还可作为异质结构功能层，用于调控 BiTeI Rashba 表面态 或增强 MnBi(₂)Te(₄) 薄膜磁性。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析

    Abstract

    • Janus chromium chalcohalide family is re-evaluated by first principles

    研究对象为非中心对称二维磁性材料 CrXY，其中 (X=S,Se,Te)，(Y=Cl,Br,I)。体系由三层原子面按 X–Cr–Y 堆叠，天然破缺反演对称性，形成 Janus 单层；原文明确为 *"chromium chalcohalide monolayers, CrXY (X = S, Se, Te; Y = Cl, Br, I)"*，并说明 *"three atomic planes stacked in the X–Cr–Y sequence, which breaks inversion symmetry"*。

    • Both 1T and 1H polymorphs are included

    同时考察 1T 与 1H 两种结构多晶型，起点是通过 声子谱 判断动力学稳定性；原文为 *"We consider both 1T and 1H structural polymorphs of CrXY, beginning with an assessment of their dynamical stability via phonon spectra calculations."*

    • Most systems are dynamically stable, but 1H tellurides are unstable

    除 1H-CrTeY 变体外，其余体系动力学稳定；原文给出结论：*"All systems, except for the 1H-CrTeY variants, are found to be dynamically stable."*

    • 1T phase is energetically dominant

    1T 相 相对 1H 相 普遍更稳定，能量优势超过 0.55 eV/f.u.；原文为 *"the 1T phase is consistently more favorable, with energy gains exceeding 0.55 eV per formula unit."*

    • Ferromagnetic coupling is universal among dynamically stable systems

    所有动力学稳定的 CrXY 单层都表现 铁磁耦合；原文为 *"all dynamically stable CrXY monolayers exhibit ferromagnetic coupling."*

    • Robust perpendicular magnetic anisotropy is composition-selective

    稳健 面外磁各向异性 PMA 只在 CrSI 与 CrSeI 中出现，且适用于 1T 与 1H 两种结构；原文为 *"robust out-of-plane magnetic anisotropy is observed only in the CrSI and CrSeI compositions, for both 1T and 1H structures."*

    • PMA comes from competing anisotropy terms

    PMA 源于 单离子各向异性 与 各向异性交换 的建设性作用，并克服 偶极-偶极相互作用；原文为 *"The perpendicular magnetic anisotropy results from a constructive interplay between single-ion and anisotropic exchange contributions that overcome the dipole–dipole interaction."*

    • DMI is weak-to-moderate relative to isotropic exchange

    对 CrSI 与 CrSeI 的两种结构均量化 Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction, DMI，其强度相对各向同性交换为弱到中等；原文为 *"reveal a weak-to-moderate DMI strength as compared to the isotropic exchange interaction term."*

    • Curie temperatures reach and exceed room temperature in selected systems

    对具有 铁磁耦合 + PMA 的体系，DFT 参数输入 ASD 模拟 得到 (T_C)：1T-CrSI 至少 210 K，1H-CrSeI 为 235–260 K，1H-CrSI 为 370–410 K；原文为 *"The calculated Curie temperatures are at least 210 K for 1T-CrSI, 235–260 K for 1H-CrSeI, and 370–410 K for 1H-CrSI."*

    • 1T-CrSeI supports chiral textures instead of simple ferromagnetism

    1T-CrSeI 因较大 DMI 在零外场形成 worm-like domain ground state，垂直磁场下可稳定 skyrmions；原文为 *"the sizable DMI in 1T-CrSeI results in a worm-like domain ground state at zero external field and enables the stabilization of skyrmions under a perpendicular magnetic field."*

    • Heterostructure functionality is proposed

    CrXY 可用于调控 BiTeI 的 Bychkov-Rashba 分裂表面态，也可增强 MnBi(₂)Te(₄) 薄膜磁性；原文为 *"used to tune the Bychkov-Rashba split surface state of BiTeI or to enhance magnetism of thin films of the intrinsic antiferromagnetic topological insulator MnBi2Te4."*

    ---

    I Introduction

    • Finite-temperature 2D ferromagnetism requires anisotropy

    二维各向同性 Heisenberg 模型中有限温度磁有序被 Mermin-Wagner 定理 禁止，但 易轴磁各向异性 可解除限制；原文为 *"the Mermin-Wagner theorem prohibits magnetic ordering in the 2D isotropic Heisenberg model at finite temperatures. However, the presence of easy-axis magnetic anisotropy lifts this restriction."*

    • 2D magnets enable van der Waals heterostructure engineering

    二维层状磁体适合通过 范德华异质结构工程 精确调控应变、组分、光学与电子性质；原文为 *"compatibility with van der Waals heterostructure engineering, enabling precise control over strain, composition, as well as optical and electronic properties."*

    • Broken inversion symmetry plus SOC produces Rashba physics

    非中心对称体系中 SOC 导致本来自旋简并能带发生动量依赖劈裂，即 Bychkov-Rashba effect；原文为 *"SOC leads to momentum-dependent splitting of otherwise spin-degenerate bands, a phenomenon known as the Bychkov-Rashba effect."*

    • Rashba plus exchange splitting is relevant to spin-orbit torque switching

    强 Rashba 劈裂与显著交换劈裂结合的电子态被认为对含重元素异质结构中的 电流诱导磁化翻转 关键；原文为 *"electronic states combining a strong Bychkov-Rashba effect with significant exchange splitting play a crucial role in current-induced magnetization switching."*

    • Ferromagnetic Rashba materials may host topological superconductivity when proximitized

    具有 Rashba 劈裂的铁磁材料若近邻 s-wave 超导体，可能形成拓扑非平庸超导相并支持 零能 Majorana 模式；原文为 *"can host a topologically non-trivial superconducting phase supporting zero-energy Majorana modes."*

    • DMI arises from broken inversion symmetry, magnetism, and SOC

    DMI 是常规 Heisenberg 交换的一阶 SOC 修正，偏好手性非共线自旋纹理；原文为 *"DMI is an antisymmetric exchange interaction that arises from a first-order spin-orbit correction to the conventional Heisenberg exchange"*，并且 *"favors chiral non-collinear spin textures."*

    • Skyrmions motivate noncentrosymmetric 2D magnets

    磁性 skyrmion 因拓扑保护、纳米尺寸和低驱动电流而适合未来自旋电子器件；原文为 *"topological protection, nanoscale dimensions, and extremely low driving current requirements."*

    • Noncentrosymmetric 2D materials can also be piezoelectric and ferroelastic

    非中心对称二维材料可能表现 本征压电性 与 铁弹性，适合纳米机电与能量采集；原文为 *"noncentrosymmetric 2D materials can also exhibit intrinsic piezoelectricity and ferroelasticity."*

    • Intrinsic inversion breaking is preferable to external symmetry breaking

    反演对称性可通过异质组合、偏压或应变外部破缺，但更直接的方法是使用本征非中心对称二维磁体；原文为 *"the most straightforward and desirable approach is to employ a 2D van der Waals magnet that intrinsically lacks inversion symmetry."*

    • Janus TMDs provide synthesis precedent

    MoSSe Janus 单层 可通过 CVD MoS(₂) 后硫去除与热硒化两步合成；原文为 *"MoSSe can be synthesized via a two-step process involving chemical vapor deposition of MoS2, followed by sulfur removal and thermal selenization."*

    • Magnetic Janus analogues can host large DMI

    MnSeTe 与 MnSTe Janus 单层中 DMI 振幅可与 铁磁体/重金属异质结构 相当；原文为 *"DMI amplitudes in MnSeTe and MnSTe Janus MLs are comparable to those found in ferromagnet/heavy-metal heterostructures."*

    • CrXY chalcohalide Janus monolayers may outperform chalcogen-only Janus systems

    卤素更强电负性可产生更强电偶极，从而增强 Rashba、DMI、压电响应；原文为 *"the presence of more electronegative halogen atoms is expected to induce stronger electric dipoles, thereby enhancing the Bychkov-Rashba effect, DMI, and piezoelectric response."*

    • Earlier CrXY predictions reported very high Curie temperatures

    先前研究给出 CrSY 的 (T_C=161–275) K、CrSeBr 的 (T_C=550) K、CrTeI 的 (T_C=956) K；原文为 *"Reported TC values reached 161–275 K for CrSY and 550 K for CrSeBr, climbing as high as 956 K for CrTeI."*

    • Later refinements found non-collinear states in heavier compositions

    含较重硫族/卤素元素的体系 (X=Se,Te)、(Y=Br,I) 并非简单铁磁体，而易出现由 DMI 与受挫交换驱动的非共线态；原文为 *"not simple ferromagnets but are instead prone to pronounced non-collinearities."*

    • Known examples include worm domains, skyrmions, and bimerons

    CrTeI 预测零场存在虫状畴与 skyrmion 共存；CrSeCl 与 CrSeBr 被提出可承载 bimerons；原文为 *"coexistence of worm-like domains and skyrmions at zero field for CrTeI"*，以及 *"CrSeCl and CrSeBr have been proposed to host bimerons."*

    • Previous CrXY work mainly focused on the 1T structure

    早期 CrXY 研究主要考察 畸变八面体 1T 结构，对应 CrSe(₂)、CrTe(₂) 结构；原文为 *"the distorted octahedral (1T) structure of CrXY MLs has been considered."*

    • 1H trigonal-prismatic phase was underexplored for CrXY

    1H 相 在 TMD 中常见，但此前 CrXY Janus 单层的 1H 变体缺乏系统 DFT 验证；原文为 *"the trigonal prismatic (1H) phase is frequently realized within the TMD family"*，并指出 *"this structural variant had not been explored for MXY Janus MLs in the aforementioned studies."*

    • Shape anisotropy had often been neglected

    对 1T-CrXY，许多研究未考虑局域磁矩间 偶极-偶极相互作用 产生的形状各向异性，可能导致磁各向异性定量甚至定性错误；原文为 *"the shape anisotropy contribution arising from dipole-dipole interactions between local moments has been considered neither..."*，以及 *"Neglecting this contribution may result in an inaccurate description of magnetic anisotropy, both quantitatively and qualitatively."*

    • Machine-learning predictions for 1H-CrXY require ab initio verification

    1H-CrXY 的磁性此前主要由机器学习预测，缺少 DFT + Monte Carlo/ASD 独立验证；原文为 *"their magnetic properties had only been addressed using machine learning approach"*，并强调 *"independent verification of these machine learning predictions using the state-of-the-art density functional theory..."* 仍然缺失。

    • Universal positive MAE assumption is untested

    此前 1H-CrXY 估算临界温度时假设所有体系都有 +1 meV 磁晶各向异性能 与面外易轴，该假设尚未验证；原文为 *"an assumption of a universal, positive magnetocrystalline anisotropy energy of 1 meV was made for all 1H-CrXY MLs"*，以及 *"The validity of this assumption remains untested."*

    • Research goal is targeted screening of robust PMA ferromagnets

    目标是可靠筛选 稳定铁磁、强 PMA、高 (T_C) 的 CrXY Janus 单层；原文为 *"reliably identifying among these systems stable ferromagnets with robust perpendicular magnetic anisotropy (PMA) and elevated Curie temperatures."*

    • Key candidates are 1T-CrSI and 1H-CrSI/CrSeI

    最终识别出 1T-CrSI 与 1H-CrXI, (X=S,Se) 为目标铁磁 PMA 体系；原文为 *"we identify among all 1T- and 1H-CrXY systems the following three: 1T-CrSI and 1H-CrXI (X = S, Se)."*

    • Predicted Curie temperatures are application-relevant

    (T_C) 预测为 1T-CrSI 至少 210 K、1H-CrSeI 235–260 K、1H-CrSI 370–410 K；原文为 *"at least 210 K for 1T-CrSI... 235–260 K for 1H-CrSeI and well above room temperature for 1H-CrSI (370-410 K)."*

    • Functional heterostructures are proposed

    1T-CrSI 与 BiTeI 或 MnBi(₂)Te(₄) 构成异质结构，用于 Rashba 表面态调控和拓扑反铁磁薄膜磁性增强；原文为 *"we propose functional heterostructures, in which 1T-CrSI MLs are interfaced with (i) BiTeI... and (ii) thin films of the intrinsic AFM topological insulator MnBi2Te4."*

    ---

    II Computational details

    • DFT implementation and exchange-correlation treatment are specified

    除声子谱外，DFT 计算采用 VASP 中的 PAW 方法 与 GGA 交换关联泛函；原文为 *"All DFT calculations, except for those of the phonon spectra, were performed using the projector augmented-wave (PAW) method, as implemented in the VASP code"*，以及 *"The generalized gradient approximation (GGA) was employed."*

    • Plane-wave cutoff and Hubbard correction are defined

    平面波截断能为 500 eV；Cr (3d) 局域态采用 GGA+(U)，(Uₑff=U-J)，测试 2.1、3.0、4.0 eV；原文为 *"The plane wave cutoff energy was set to 500 eV"*，以及 *"The values of Ueff = 2.1 eV... 3.0 eV, and 4.0 eV were considered for the Cr 3d states."*

    • Structure and magnetism are treated consistently for each U value

    每个 (Uₑff) 下均独立优化结构并计算对应磁性，避免结构-磁性参数不匹配；原文为 *"All reported quantities at a given Ueff correspond to the structure optimized with the same Ueff."*

    • Robustness rather than exact U determination is the strategy

    不追求唯一 (Uₑff)，而考察性质随 (Uₑff) 的定性稳定性；原文为 *"we do not attempt to determine an unambiguous value of Ueff"*，以及 *"If a property... remains qualitatively unchanged across the tested range, it can be regarded as a robust theoretical prediction."*

    • Vacuum and relaxation parameters are specified

    周期薄膜模型中真空间隔约 13 Å；原子力收敛标准 0.01 eV/Å；原文为 *"repeating films separated by a vacuum gap of about 13 Å"*，以及 *"a force convergence criterion of 0.01 eV/Å."*

    • Structural optimization uses the FM 1×1 cell

    结构优化采用含一个 Cr 的六角 (1×1) 原胞，等价于先在 FM 态优化；原文为 *"A hexagonal (1×1) cell containing one Cr atom was used for structural optimization, which implies that all systems were optimized in the FM state."*

    • Nearest-neighbor exchange uses a rectangular two-Cr supercell

    最近邻交换 (J) 使用矩形 (1×sqrt3) 超胞，含两个 Cr，可描述 FM 与 AFM；k 网格分别为 (11×11×1) 与 (11×7×1)；原文为 *"a rectangular (1×√3) supercell containing two Cr atoms was employed"*，以及 *"11×11×1 k-point mesh... 11×7×1 mesh."*

    • Longer-range exchange is checked in selected systems

    部分体系用 OstravaJ 计算到第三近邻交换，采用 (4×4) 超胞与 (3×3×1) k 网格；原文为 *"calculated the isotropic exchange coupling constants up to the third-NNs... using OstravaJ code"*。

    • Phonon spectra use mixed-basis pseudopotential linear response

    声子谱通过 线性响应 + mixed-basis pseudopotential method 获得；截断能 24 Ry，k 网格 (12×12×1)，Cr 加 (Uₑff=2.1) eV；原文为 *"Phonon spectra were obtained... using the linear response technique in combination with the mixed-basis pseudopotential method"*。

    • Magnetic anisotropy is calculated with SOC non-self-consistently

    磁各向异性计算在 (1×sqrt3) 超胞中包含 SOC，采用非自洽方法以避免 AFM SOC 收敛问题，并用自洽 FM 结果验证；k 网格 (33×21×1)；原文为 *"performed including SOC, using a non-self-consistent approach"*，以及 *"we verified the accuracy of the non-self-consistent results against fully self-consistent calculations and found good agreement."*

    • DMI calculations use large supercell and tight convergence

    DMI 计算采用 (4×1) 超胞，k 网格 (11×45×1)，总能收敛阈值 (10⁻⁸) eV；原文为 *"To compute the DMI, we constructed a (4×1) supercell"*，以及 *"A total energy convergence threshold of 10−8 eV was applied."*

    • Finite-temperature magnetism is simulated with ASD and LLG

    温度依赖磁性通过 classical Heisenberg spin Hamiltonian + stochastic LLG equation 的 ASD 模拟研究；原文为 *"we employed ASD simulations using a classical Heisenberg spin Hamiltonian with parameters extracted from the DFT calculations"*，以及 *"stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert (LLG) equation."*

    • ASD is cross-validated with Monte Carlo

    LLG-ASD 与 VAMPIRE Monte Carlo 模拟对比，结果一致；原文为 *"tested against the Monte Carlo simulations, performed using the VAMPIRE code, and a good agreement was found."*

    • CrSI/BiTeI heterostructures exploit lattice matching

    1T-CrSI 与 BiTeI 的 (2×2) 和 (sqrt3×sqrt3) 超晶格面内参数完美匹配；原文为 *"the pair of materials which has perfect matching in the in-plain parameters of their (2×2) and (√3×√3) superlattices."*

    • Two CrSI/BiTeI interfaces are modeled

    考察 Te-I 与 I-S 两种卤素-硫族界面；BiTeI 用 8 个三层 表示，反面分别 H 或 F 钝化；原文为 *"Two halogen–chalcogen interfaces were considered: Te-I and I-S interfaces"*，以及 *"modeled by eight trilayers with either H- or F-passivated opposite side."*

    • CrSI/MnBi2Te4 heterostructures include SOC, vdW, and U corrections

    CrSI/[MnBi(₂)Te(₄)](ₙSL) 中 CrSI (2×2) 超胞扩张 0.2% 匹配 MnBi(₂)Te(₄) (sqrt3×sqrt3)；Cr (Uₑff=3) eV，Mn (Uₑff=5.34) eV，vdW 用 Grimme DFT-D3 with Becke–Johnson damping；原文为 *"expanding the lattice parameter... by 0.2%"*，以及 *"Ueff = 5.34 eV was used for the Mn 3d orbitals."*

    • Chern number is evaluated with Wannier-based tools

    Chern 数通过 Wannier90 构造紧束缚哈密顿量，并用 WannierTools 进行 Wannier charge center 求和；原文为 *"Wannier functions and the corresponding tight-binding Hamiltonian were constructed using the Wannier90 package"*，以及 *"Wannier charge center summation was performed using the WannierTools package."*

    ---

    III Results and discussion

    III.1 Crystal structure

    • 1T and 1H structures share the same space group but differ in stacking and coordination

    1T 与 1H 分别为 ABC 与 ABA 堆叠，均属于 P3m1 (No. 156) 空间群；1T 中 Cr 处于畸变八面体，1H 中 Cr 处于畸变三角棱柱；原文为 *"characterized by ABC and ABA stackings, respectively"*，以及 *"Both the 1T and 1H phases belong to the same P3m1 (No. 156) space group."*

    • Dynamical stability excludes 1H tellurides

    1T-CrXY 以及 (X=S,Se) 的 1H 结构无虚频、无声子异常，动力学稳定；1H-CrTeY 最低振动模强烈软化，所有原子沿 (z) 方向位移，因而被排除；原文为 *"have neither imaginary modes nor phonon dispersion anomalies"*，以及 *"the 1H phase of the tellurides is dynamically unstable, showing a strong softening of the lowest vibrational mode."*

    • Lattice constants increase with heavier chalcogen or halogen atoms

    (a₀) 随硫族元素 (X) 或卤素 (Y) 原子序数增加而增大，符合离子半径趋势；原文为 *"a0 increases with the atomic number of either the chalcogen (X) or halogen (Y) atom, which is consistent with the increase of the corresponding ionic radii."*

    • Larger Ueff expands the lattice through d-electron localization

    增大 (Uₑff) 使 Cr (3d) 电子更局域，降低与 (X/Y) 的 (p) 轨道杂化，从而增大 (a₀)；原文为 *"increasing Ueff results in a larger a0, which is attributed to the stronger localization of the Cr-3d electrons."*

    • 1T-CrTeCl is an anomalous case

    1T-CrTeCl 在 (Uₑff) 从 3.0 到 4.0 eV 时 (a₀) 略降，并与交换耦合、MAE 异常相关；可能因 (Uₑff=4.0) eV 时体系变为无带隙；原文为 *"An exception to this monotonic trend occurs for 1T-CrTeCl"*，以及 *"may be linked to the system becoming gapless at Ueff = 4.0 eV."*

    • 1T lattice constants span 3.47–4.03 Å and 1H is about 2.5% smaller

    1T (a₀) 从 CrSCl 约 3.47 Å 到 CrTeI 约 4.03 Å；1H 晶格常数系统性小约 2.5%；原文为 *"for the 1T polymorphs, a0 ranges from approximately 3.47 Å (CrSCl) to 4.03 Å (CrTeI), while the 1H structures exhibit lattice constants that are systematically ∼2.5% smaller."*

    • 1T is consistently more stable than 1H

    FM 态下总能差 (Δ EH/T=E₁H-E₁T) 显示所有成分中 1T 能量更低，每化学式单元至少低 0.55 eV；原文为 *"the 1T structure is consistently more favorable, exhibiting an energy gain of at least 0.55 eV per formula unit."*

    • 1H metastability remains experimentally plausible

    尽管 1H 能量较高，但 TMD 中高能亚稳相可通过非平衡方法合成；例如 MoS(₂)、WS(₂) 的 1T 相比 1H 高 0.8–0.9 eV/f.u.，仍可在 9 T 磁场水热合成 中稳定；原文为 *"metastable polymorphs with significantly higher formation energies have been successfully synthesized"*，以及 *"hydrothermal synthesis under a magnetic field of 9 T."*

    • Raman modes provide experimental structural fingerprints

    Raman 光谱 可直接区分 1T 与 1H 多晶型，已计算特征 A(₁) 与 E 模式频率；原文为 *"Raman spectroscopy provides a direct structural fingerprint that can distinguish these two polymorphs experimentally"*。

    ---

    III.2 Magnetic characterization

    #### III.2.1 Magnetic ordering

    • Magnetic exchange is extracted from AFM-FM total energy differences

    在标量相对论近似下计算 (Δ EA/F=EAFM-EFM)，并映射到最近邻 Heisenberg 哈密顿量

    [

    Hᵢₛₒ=-fracJ2sumᵢ,ⱼMᵢḑotMⱼ

    ]

    原文为 *"compute the total energy differences ΔEA/F = EAFM − EFM within the scalar-relativistic approximation"*，以及 *"map the results to the isotropic exchange term of the Heisenberg Hamiltonian."*

    • Magnetic moment vectors are used instead of spin vectors

    Cr 局域磁矩为 3.2–3.8 (μ_B)，处于 (S=3/2) 与 (S=2) 难以明确归类的中间区间，因此哈密顿量使用 (Mᵢ) 而非 (Sᵢ)；原文为 *"local Cr moments of CrXY span an intermediate range of 3.2-3.8 μB, preventing a clear assignment to either S = 3/2 or S = 2."*

    • All dynamically stable CrXY monolayers have ferromagnetic nearest-neighbor coupling

    所有动力学稳定 CrXY 单层均有 (Δ EA/F>0) 与 (J>0)，确认最近邻 FM 耦合；原文为 *"all dynamically stable CrXY MLs show FM NN interaction"*，以及 *"ΔEA/F > 0... exchange constants J are positive."*

    • Direct Cr-Cr exchange is negligible

    COHP 分析显示即便在晶格常数最小的 CrSCl 中，相邻 Cr 的 (d) 态重叠也可忽略；1T-CrSCl 平均 (a₀simeq3.49) Å，1H-CrSCl 平均 (a₀simeq3.40) Å；原文为 *"negligible overlap of the Cr-d states from the adjacent sites even for CrSCl"*。

    • Ferromagnetism in gapped systems follows Goodenough-Kanamori rules

    除半金属与特殊无带隙体系外，多数有带隙体系通过接近 90° 的 Cr–X(Y)–Cr 超交换路径实现 FM 耦合；原文为 *"Cr–X(Y)–Cr bonds with angles close to 90°, which favors FM coupling."*

    • Half-metallic 1H-CrSI and 1H-CrSeI gain enhanced double exchange

    1H-CrXI, (X=S,Se) 为半金属，Cr-X(Y)-Cr 桥进入 double-exchange regime，自由载流子增强 FM (J)；原文为 *"For the half-metallic 1H-CrXI (X = S, Se)... operate in the double-exchange regime, giving the enhanced FM J."*

    • Tellurides are not deeply analyzed for frustration because they lack clear PMA

    Te 体系存在第三近邻交换导致的磁受挫倾向，但因未表现出明确 垂直磁各向异性，不作为主要筛选对象；原文为 *"we do not investigate frustration effects in CrTeY, as they do not exhibit a clear tendency toward perpendicular magnetic anisotropy."*

    • 1T-CrTeCl has anomalously weak J

    1T-CrTeCl 的 (J) 显著下降，与 Cr (3d) 与 (X/Y) (p) 态杂化减弱相关；NN-only 描述还可能把进一步邻居耦合吸收到有效 NN 项中，尤其因 (J₃) 负且较大；原文为 *"The strong drop of J found for 1T-CrTeCl"*，以及 *"further-neighbor couplings are inadvertently absorbed into the effective NN term."*

    • DFT contradicts previous machine-learning predictions for 1H systems

    机器学习曾预测多数 1H-CrXY 为 AFM，仅 1H-CrSI 为 FM；直接 DFT 结果显示所有这些 1H 体系均为 FM 基态；原文为 *"predicted them to mostly be AFM, with 1H-CrSI as the only FM case"*，以及 *"our direct DFT results... yield an FM ground state for all these 1H systems."*

    • Discrepancy is attributed to data-driven model limitations

    1H 相差异可能源于机器学习训练集范围与偏差；ab initio 方法对每个结构和磁构型自洽处理电荷密度，可靠性更高；原文为 *"likely stems from inherent limitations of the data-driven approach"*，以及 *"self-consistently treats the charge density of each specific structural and magnetic configuration."*

    • Exchange in CrXY exceeds CrI3 and MnBi2Te4 by large margins

    单层 CrI(₃) 的 NN (J=0.5) meV/(μ_B²)，单七层 MnBi(₂)Te(₄) 的 (J=0.07) meV/(μ_B²)；CrXY 通常为 1.5–2.5 meV/(μ_B²)，比 CrI(₃) 高 3–5 倍，比 MnBi(₂)Te(₄) 高一个数量级以上；原文为 *"typically ranging from about 1.5 to 2.5 meV/μB2"*，以及 *"by up to 3–5 times."*

    • Cr local moments indicate Cr3+-to-Cr2+ crossover

    Cr 磁矩 3.2–3.8 (μ_B)，低端接近 (3d³)，高端接近 (3d⁴)，反映 Cr(³⁺)-like 到 Cr(²⁺)-like 过渡；原文为 *"with the lower end tending to the 3d3 configuration and the upper end approaching 3d4."*

    • Magnetic moments increase with heavier elements and larger Ueff

    (mCᵣ) 随 (X/Y) 原子序数与 (Uₑff) 增大略增；1H 相通常比 1T 相局域磁矩稍大；原文为 *"weak upward trend with the atomic number Z of both the chalcogen and halogen atoms, as well as with increasing Ueff"*。

    • Chalcogen atoms carry sizable antiparallel induced moments

    硫族原子 (X) 上诱导磁矩与 Cr 反平行，最高可达 0.5 (μ_B)；卤素 (Y) 上诱导磁矩通常低于 0.2 (μ_B)；原文为 *"induced moments mX can reach up to 0.5 μB"*，以及 *"moments induced on the halogen atoms Y are significantly smaller, generally remaining below 0.2 μB."*

    ---

    #### III.2.2 Magnetic anisotropy

    • Available content defines the key anisotropy quantities

    磁各向异性通过 SOC 能量差

    [

    ESOC=Eᵢₚ-Eₒₒₚ

    ]

    与偶极-偶极能量

    [

    Ed₋d

    ]

    以及总量

    [

    Eₛᵤₘ=ESOC+Ed₋d

    ]

    表征；图 5 说明原文为 *"Total energy difference between the states with the in-plane (ip) and out-of-plane (oop) directions of the Cr magnetic moment, ESOC = Eip − Eoop"*，以及 *"Esum = ESOC + Ed−d."*

    • Both 1T and 1H structures are compared under FM ordering

    图 5 同时给出 1T 与 1H 结构在 FM 排布下的 (ESOC)、(Ed₋d)、(Eₛᵤₘ)；原文为 *"of the CrXY Janus MLs... with the 1T... and 1H... structures, as calculated for the FM ordering."*

    • PMA assessment must include dipolar shape anisotropy

    仅 SOC 能量不足以确定真实易轴，必须加上 classical dipole-dipole interaction 的形状各向异性能；图 5 直接把 (ESOC)、(Ed₋d)、(Eₛᵤₘ) 分开展示，呼应引言中 *"Neglecting this contribution may result in an inaccurate description of magnetic anisotropy, both quantitatively and qualitatively."*

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持

    1. 术语解析

    • Perpendicular magnetic anisotropy (PMA)

    指磁矩更偏好垂直于二维平面的方向排列。二维磁体中 PMA 不只是器件指标，更是绕开 Mermin-Wagner 定理 的关键条件。若 (Eᵢₚ-Eₒₒₚ>0)，面外磁化能量更低，倾向 PMA。

    • Shape anisotropy / dipole-dipole interaction

    形状各向异性 来自磁偶极之间的经典长程相互作用，二维薄膜中通常倾向让磁矩躺在平面内，以减少退磁场。它常与 SOC 产生的磁晶各向异性竞争，因此忽略它可能把“面外易轴”误判为“面内易轴”或反之。

    • Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI)

    一种反对称交换项，典型形式为 (Dᵢⱼḑot(Sᵢ×Sⱼ₎)。只有在 反演对称性破缺 + SOC 条件下显著。它不简单增强或削弱铁磁性，而是倾向让相邻自旋以固定手性扭转，从而产生 螺旋、自旋畴壁、skyrmion。

    • Bychkov-Rashba effect

    非中心对称体系中 SOC 导致的动量依赖自旋劈裂。与一般“自旋轨道耦合导致能带变化”相比，Rashba 效应强调 自旋-动量锁定 与 能带在 (k) 空间分裂，对电流诱导自旋极化和磁化翻转尤其重要。

    • Janus monolayer

    “Janus” 指上下两面由不同元素终止的单层材料，例如 X–Cr–Y。其核心不是单纯化学不对称，而是产生面外极性和反演对称性破缺，从而激活 Rashba、DMI、压电等效应。

    2. 疑难查证

    • 为什么二维铁磁体需要磁各向异性？

    纯二维各向同性 Heisenberg 模型中，长波长自旋波在任意有限温度下都能破坏长程有序。磁各向异性相当于给自旋波谱打开能隙，使低能涨落不再发散。因此 PMA 不只是“磁矩方向”的问题，而是决定二维铁磁能否在有限温度存在的基本物理量。

    • 为什么 (Uₑff) 会影响晶格常数和磁性？

    (Uₑff) 增大意味着 Cr (3d) 电子更局域，Cr-(p) 杂化减弱。杂化影响超交换路径、带隙、局域磁矩和磁各向异性。因此固定一个任意 (U) 值可能带来偶然结论；跨 (2.1–4.0) eV 检验定性稳定性更严谨。

    • 为什么 1T 更稳定但 1H 仍值得研究？

    热力学最低能相通常更容易合成，但二维材料常存在可由非平衡生长、衬底、应变、外场或动力学路径稳定的亚稳多晶型。1H-CrSI 的预测 (T_C=370–410) K，性能上明显值得关注，即便其能量高于 1T。

    • 为什么 1T-CrSeI 不是简单高温铁磁候选？

    铁磁 NN 交换倾向让自旋平行，但 DMI 倾向让自旋扭转。若 DMI 相对交换足够大，零场基态可从均匀铁磁变为虫状畴或螺旋纹理；外场下可稳定 skyrmion。因此“有 FM 交换”不等于“基态是均匀 FM”。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联

    1. 创新性判断

    • 从“预测高 TC”推进到“可用高 TC PMA 铁磁体筛选”

    过去 2–5 年内 CrXY Janus 单层已有大量理论预测，但不少结论依赖简化模型、未完整处理形状各向异性，或只关注 1T 相。新的关键推进是把 动力学稳定性、结构相竞争、FM/AFM 能量、SOC 各向异性、偶极各向异性、DMI、ASD 居里温度 放进同一闭环筛选流程。

    • 显式纠正形状各向异性缺失导致的 PMA 风险

    多数早期工作未纳入偶极-偶极项。二维薄膜中该项通常偏向面内磁化，会抵消 SOC 产生的面外磁晶各向异性。显式计算 (Eₛᵤₘ=ESOC+Ed₋d) 使 PMA 判断更接近真实物理。

    • 首次系统验证 1H-CrXY 的磁性而非依赖机器学习预测

    1H 相此前主要由机器学习给出磁性判断，并假设统一正 MAE。直接 DFT 结果推翻“多数 1H-CrXY 为 AFM”的预测，显示所有动力学稳定 1H-CrXY 均有 FM 最近邻耦合，并筛选出 1H-CrSI 与 1H-CrSeI。

    • 发现室温以上 Janus 2D PMA 铁磁候选 1H-CrSI

    1H-CrSI 的 (T_C=370–410) K 同时满足 PMA 与 室温以上铁磁性，在二维磁体领域极具吸引力。相较 CrI(₃) 等低温二维磁体，CrXY 的 NN 交换通常大 3–5 倍。

    • 区分“均匀铁磁候选”与“手性磁纹理候选”

    1T-CrSI、1H-CrSI、1H-CrSeI 更接近 PMA 铁磁候选；1T-CrSeI 因 DMI 导致虫状畴与场诱导 skyrmion，更适合手性自旋纹理研究。这种分类解决了早期“只报高 (T_C)”而忽视非共线基态的问题。

    • 将材料筛选连接到拓扑与 Rashba 异质结构功能

    CrXY 不仅是单层磁体，还可与 BiTeI 和 MnBi(₂)Te(₄) 构建功能异质结构，分别服务于 Rashba 表面态调控 与 拓扑反铁磁薄膜磁性增强。这把 Janus 磁体从孤立材料预测推进到可设计界面功能层。

    💡 亮点：三维交错磁超导可出现交叉平带。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题三维超导交错磁体中，零净磁化但动量自旋劈裂的交错磁序，如何与节点型手性 d 波超导共同塑造新的拓扑表面态？核心关注：[001] 表面是否会出现零能交叉表面平带、其几何角点由什么决定，以及 Bogoliubov-Fermi 面如何影响 [100] 表面弧态和隧穿电导。
    创新方法构建三维 Bogoliubov-de Gennes 模型，把 dxy、dx²−y² 与 gxy(x²−y²) 交错磁项嵌入自旋单态三维手性 d 波超导；关键 Aha 点是：交错磁节点决定平带的“交叉几何与角点数”，超导节点线负责把平带钉扎在零能，而伪磁镜面对称性与粒子-空穴对称性共同生成手征保护机制。
    工作流程输入三维紧束缚电子能带、交错磁动量质量项 M(k) 与手性 d 波配对 Δ(k)；计算 BdG 体能谱，识别超导节点线、交错磁节点和 Bogoliubov-Fermi 面；在 [001] 与 [100] 表面投影动量空间，分析零能平带和表面弧态；用伪磁镜面对称性、粒子-空穴对称性和一维绕数判定拓扑保护；最后通过递归 Green 函数与 Lee-Fisher 公式生成动量分辨和总隧穿电导图谱。
    关键结果[001] 表面产生零能交叉表面平带：dxy 与 dx²−y² 交错磁体形成四角交叉图案，dx²−y² 图案相对旋转 π/4，gxy(x²−y²) 形成八角交叉图案；交错磁性把手性 d 波超导节点线膨胀为 Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces，并在 [100] 表面削弱或打断零能弧态；零偏压动量分辨电导同时出现三类透明度幂律：平带/弧态为常数律，BFS 为线性律，有隙区为二次律；总电导显示可观测零偏压峰或自旋劈裂双峰。
    应用价值为三维交错磁超导体提供可视化拓扑指纹：交叉平带角点数可反映交错磁晶体对称性，方向依赖隧穿谱可区分 [001] 平带、[100] 弧态和体 Bogoliubov-Fermi 面；可通过低温低透明度隧穿谱、零偏压电导峰、ARPES、Doppler shift 与准粒子干涉实验检验，并直接关联 Sr₂RuO₄、CrSb、La₂CuO₄、UPt₃ 和 half-Heusler 等候选材料。

    第一部分：核心概览

    三维超导交错磁体中，交错磁对称性与节点超导对称性共同产生一种新的高维拓扑表面态：交叉表面平带。在具有自旋单态手性 d 波超导的 d 波与 g 波交错磁体中，位于 xy 平面的超导节点线保证 [001] 表面零能平带，而交错磁节点决定平带交叉形状与角点数；同时，节点线在交错磁作用下膨胀为 Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces，并调制 [100] 表面弧态。工作将此前主要局限于二维交错磁超导体系的拓扑研究推广到三维，提出可由零偏压电导峰、动量分辨电导幂律和隧穿谱实验检验的可观测判据，对 Sr₂RuO₄ 等候选材料具有直接关联。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Crossed surface flat bands in three-dimensional superconducting altermagnets》（None，）

    背景

    交错磁体具有零净磁化但存在动量依赖自旋劈裂，已在二维超导体系中展现 Josephson 异常输运、拓扑超导、奇异配对和稳定亚能隙态。三维交错磁超导体系尚未充分探索，尤其是可能同时具有交错磁序与三维手性 d 波超导的 Sr₂RuO₄。

    方法

    构建三维 Bogoliubov-de Gennes 模型，包含最近邻紧束缚色散、dxy / dx²−y² / gxy(x²−y²) 交错磁项，以及自旋单态三维手性 d 波配对。通过能谱、对称性、绕数、递归 Green 函数和 Lee-Fisher 电导公式分析体态、表面态与输运响应。

    结果

    [001] 表面出现零能交叉表面平带，角点数由交错磁节点决定：dxy 与 dx²−y² 情形为四角，gxy(x²−y²) 情形为八角。手性 d 波节点线在交错磁作用下形成 Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces，并影响 [100] 表面零能弧态。动量分辨零偏压电导同时呈现三类透明度依赖：平带/弧态的常数律、BFS 的线性律、能隙区的二次律。

    讨论

    交叉平带受到伪磁镜面对称性与粒子-空穴对称性联合形成的手征对称性保护，是三维交错磁超导中零能 Andreev 束缚态的高维对应物。电导信号具有方向依赖性，[001] 方向突出交叉平带，[100] 方向突出表面弧态与 BFS 调制。

    局限

    模型主要采用单轨道交错磁 BdG 哈密顿量，交错磁项形式上为有效二维动量结构；多轨道、强自旋轨道耦合、标量无序和破坏对称性的扰动仅作原则性讨论。BFS 存在区域绕数不良定义，表面弧态在某些动量附近可能失去零能共振。

    结论

    三维超导交错磁体可实现由晶体对称性保护的高维拓扑相。交叉平带、表面弧态与 Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces 可通过低透明度、低温隧穿谱、ARPES、Doppler shift 和准粒子干涉实验检测；Sr₂RuO₄、CrSb、La₂CuO₄、UPt₃ 与 half-Heusler 化合物构成潜在材料平台。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析

    Abstract

    • Three-dimensional superconducting altermagnets extend a previously two-dimensional research frontier

    超导交错磁体已被识别为新兴现象平台，但既有研究集中在二维系统；三维体系成为关键空白。摘要直接界定问题边界：*"Superconducting altermagnets have proven to be a promising ground for emergent phenomena, but their study has involved two-dimensional systems."* 核心推进在于把交错磁超导拓扑态从 2D 推向 3D。

    • d- and g-wave altermagnets with chiral d-wave superconductivity host crossed surface flat bands

    研究对象为三维 d 波与 g 波交错磁体，超导态为自旋单态手性 d 波；关键结果是产生交叉表面平带。摘要给出机制来源：*"we investigate three-dimensional d- and g-wave altermagnets with spin-singlet chiral d-wave superconductivity and show the formation of crossed surface flat bands due to the interplay between superconducting and altermagnetic symmetries."*

    • Zero-energy crossed flat bands are tied to xy-plane superconducting nodal lines

    交叉平带位于 z 方向表面 / [001] 表面，能量钉扎在零能；根源是手性 d 波超导在 xy 平面的节点线。核心表述为：*"appear at zero energy in the surface along z due to the superconducting nodal lines in the xy-plane."*

    • The number of corners is determined by altermagnetic crystal symmetry

    平带形状并非任意，而由交错磁节点与晶体对称性决定；角点数成为区分 d 波与 g 波交错磁序的拓扑几何指纹。摘要给出结论：*"their number of corners is determined by the crystal symmetry of altermagnets."*

    • Superconducting nodal lines generate Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces and surface arcs

    交错磁性使超导节点线膨胀为 Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces, BFSs，进而影响 x 方向 / [100] 表面上的零能弧态。摘要中写明：*"the superconducting nodal lines give rise to Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces, which then affect the appearance of zero-energy arcs in the surface along x."*

    • Conductance reveals coexistence of three transparency dependences

    检测方案依赖隧穿电导；交叉平带或弧态与 BFS 共存时，零偏压电导对正常态透明度呈现三种不同幂律。摘要强调实验可检性：*"the crossed flat bands or surface arcs, and Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces give rise to the coexistence of three distinct dependences of the charge conductance on the normal transparency."*

    ---

    Introduction / unlabeled opening section

    • Altermagnetism combines zero net magnetization with momentum-dependent spin splitting

    交错磁体不同于常规铁磁体和反铁磁体：总磁化为零，但能带出现动量依赖的自旋劈裂，并形成各向异性自旋极化 Fermi 面。定义性表述为：*"Altermagnets (AMs) are characterized by a zero net magnetization as a result of their momentum dependent spin splitting of energy bands and anisotropic spin-polarized Fermi surfaces."* 这使其在无宏观磁场背景下仍可产生强自旋选择效应。

    • Superconducting altermagnets already support a broad set of unconventional phenomena

    交错磁性与超导结合后，可产生异常 Josephson 输运、拓扑超导、奇异 Cooper 配对、非互易输运、非平庸光-物质耦合和稳定亚能隙态。直接罗列为：*"including anomalous Josephson transport, topological superconductivity, exotic superconducting pairs, nonreciprocal transport, nontrivial light-matter coupling, and distinct types of stable subgap states."*

    • Stable subgap states are important because they diagnose symmetry- and topology-protected superconductivity

    稳定亚能隙态不是普通边界共振，而是非常规超导、对称性与拓扑保护的指示器。核心论断为：*"The appearance of stable subgap states is of particular relevance because they signal unusual superconductivity protected by symmetry and topology."*

    • Previous altermagnetic superconductivity studies remained two-dimensional

    虽然已有研究发现 BFSs、flat bands、Andreev bound states 与交错磁和超导对称性密切相关，但空间维度局限明显。关键空白为：*"the existing studies only addressed two-dimensional (2D) systems, leaving unexplored the large family of 3D AMs."*

    • Sr₂RuO₄ supplies a concrete three-dimensional motivation

    Sr₂RuO₄近期被预测具有交错磁序，并可能共存三维手性 d 波超导；NMR 提供相关实验背景。原文指出：*"Sr2RuO4, which has very recently been predicted to host altermagnetic order as a phase that coexists with a very likely 3D chiral d-wave superconductivity probed by nuclear magnetic resonance."*

    • Crossed flat bands are proposed as a generic topological phenomenon in 3D superconducting AMs

    核心目标是利用三维交错磁超导的对称性与拓扑设计高维拓扑超导相。开场明确：*"we consider 3D superconducting AMs and demonstrate the emergence of crossed surface flat bands as a generic topological phenomenon due to the interplay between superconducting and altermagnetic symmetries."*

    • Flat bands generalize zero-energy Andreev bound states and projected-Fermi-surface flat-band concepts

    交叉平带被定位为三维超导交错磁体中零能 Andreev bound states, ABSs 的高维对应物，同时扩展 Weyl 超导与投影 Fermi 面决定平带形状的早期观念。关键表述为：*"The crossed surface flat bands are topologically protected and represent the higher-dimensional analog of zero-energy ABSs in 3D superconducting AMs."*

    ---

    3D superconducting AMs .—

    • The BdG Hamiltonian contains kinetic, altermagnetic, and superconducting sectors

    三维超导交错磁体由 BdG 哈密顿量描述：

    [

    hatHαBdG(bmk)

    =

    ǎrepsilon(bmk)hatσ₀hatτ₃

    +

    hatHαAM(bmk)

    +

    hatHSC(bmk)

    ]

    其中 (α=d,g)。原文定义为：*"We consider a 3D superconducting AM modelled by the following Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG) Hamiltonian."* 自旋空间 Pauli 矩阵为 (hatσⱼ)，粒子-空穴空间为 (hatτⱼ)。

    • The normal-state dispersion is a cubic-lattice nearest-neighbor tight-binding band

    色散为

    [

    ǎrepsilon(bmk)=-μ-2to̧skₓ-2to̧sk_y-2to̧sk_z.

    ]

    具体参数含义清楚：*"Here, (bmk=(kₓ,k_y,k_z)), (μ) is the chemical potential, (t) is the hopping integral."* 后续数值计算采用 (μ=-4.5t)、(Δ=0.01t)。

    • Altermagnetism enters as a spin-dependent particle-hole diagonal mass

    交错磁项为

    [

    hatHαAM(bmk)

    =

    Mbₘₖαhatσ₃hatτ₃.

    ]

    原文说明：*"Altermagnetism is modelled by (hatHαAM(bmk)=Mbₘₖαhatσ₃hatτ₃)."* 该项产生动量依赖自旋劈裂，但无净磁化。

    • dxy and dx²−y² altermagnets have distinct nodal structures

    dxy 波交错磁序定义为

    [

    Mbₘₖd¹=2td₁sinkₓsink_y,

    ]

    节点在 (kₓ₌₀) 或 (k_y=0)。dx²−y² 波交错磁序定义为

    [

    Mbₘₖd²=td₂(o̧skₓ-o̧sk_y),

    ]

    节点近似沿对角线 (kₓ₌± k_y)。原文为：*"We focus on (dₓy)- and (dₓ²-y²)-wave AMs described by..."*

    • gxy(x²−y²) altermagnetism combines dxy and dx²−y² nodal factors

    g 波交错磁序为

    [

    Mbₘₖg=4t_gsinkₓsink_y(o̧skₓ-o̧sk_y).

    ]

    它同时包含 (kₓ₌₀)、(k_y=0)、(kₓ₌± k_y) 类节点，因此投影表面平带可形成更多角点。原文给出：*"We also consider g-wave AMs with (Mbₘₖg=4t_gsinkₓsink_y(o̧skₓ-o̧sk_y))."*

    • The altermagnetic model is effectively two-dimensional but conclusions persist in 3D AMs

    虽然 (Mbₘₖ^α) 不显含 (k_z)，整体 BdG 模型仍为三维；相关稳健性在补充材料 S3 中验证。原文限定为：*"While (hatHAM(bmk)) is described by an effective 2D model, our findings remain in 3D AMs."*

    • Spin-singlet 3D chiral d-wave superconductivity has a kz-dependent nodal factor

    超导项为

    [

    hatHSC(bmk)

    =

    -Δsink_z[sinkₓhatτ₂₊sink_yhatτ₁]hatσ₂.

    ]

    配对函数可写成

    [

    barΔ(bmk)=Δsink_z[sinkₓ+isink_y].

    ]

    原文为：*"we assume spin-singlet 3D chiral superconductivity modelled by..."* 其中 (sin k_z) 导致 (k_z=0) 相关节点结构。

    • Altermagnetic and superconducting amplitudes are chosen comparable through self-consistency

    交错磁强度 (t_α) 在 (Δ) 量级内变化，以保证二者共存；数值图中常用 (t_α=Δ)、(Δ=0.01t)。脚注给出依据：*"The chosen values of the superconducting and altermagnetic amplitudes are obtained by ensuring the coexistence of altermagnetism and 3D chiral d-wave superconductivity in the self-consistent gap equation."*

    • The pairing choice is linked to proposed Sr₂RuO₄ interorbital or interlayer-like pairing structure

    自旋单态三维手性 d 波配对通过二近邻吸引相互作用自洽获得，并可类比 Sr₂RuO₄ 中提出的轨道间配对。原文说明：*"this justifies our choice of 3D chiral d-wave pairing in 3D superconducting AMs and can apply the interorbital pairing of Sr2RuO4 because the relating symmetry and gap structure are similar to interlayer pairings."*

    • The framework is not restricted to one specific nodal superconductor

    尽管主要分析特定三维节点超导体，理论结构可推广到其他非常规超导交错磁体。原文直接说明：*"Although we focus on a particular 3D nodal superconductor, our analysis can be straightforwardly generalized to other superconducting AMs with unconventional superconductivity."*

    ---

    Emergence of crossed surface flat bands .—

    • The quasiparticle spectrum shows how altermagnetism creates zero-energy bulk manifolds

    能谱为

    [

    Ebₘₖ,±s,α

    =

    sMbₘₖ^α

    ±

    sqrtǎrepsilon²⁽bmk)+|barΔ(bmk)|²,

    quad s=± .

    ]

    原文说明：*"These energy bands help understand the appearance of bulk phases."* 由于 (sMbₘₖ^α) 对不同自旋符号相反，交错磁性可使某一 BdG 分支穿过零能。

    • Without altermagnetism, chiral d-wave superconductivity has xy-plane line nodes and z-plane point nodes

    无交错磁性时，三维手性 d 波超导在 xy 平面有节点线，在 z 平面有点节点。原文为：*"In the absence of AMs, the 3D chiral superconductor has line nodes in the xy-plane, while point nodes in the z-plane."* 这些节点分别对应 [001] 表面平带和 [100] 表面弧态。

    • Line nodes and point nodes produce different surface states

    节点线产生 [001] 表面零能平带，点节点产生 [100] 表面弧态。原文表述：*"These line and point nodes give rise, respectively, to zero-energy surface flat bands on the [001] surface and to surface arc states on the [100] surface."*

    • Conventional flat-band shapes follow projected Fermi surfaces

    在非交错磁节点超导中，平带形状通常由投影 Fermi 面决定；球形 Fermi 面对应圆盘状平带。原文指出：*"the shape of the flat bands is determined by that of the projected Fermi surface, with a disk shape for a spherical Fermi surface."* 新结果偏离这一简单规则，因为交错磁节点重塑平带边界。

    • Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces are defined by a zero-energy condition

    零能条件来自

    [

    Ebₘₖ,₊⁻,α=0

    ]

    即

    [

    [Mbₘₖ^α]²⁼ǎrepsilon²⁽bmk)+|barΔ(bmk)|².

    ]

    原文写明：*"This defines the formation of a BFS."* BFS 是零能 Bogoliubov 准粒子在三维动量空间中的二维面状结构。

    • Altermagnetism expands superconducting line nodes into BFSs except at altermagnetic nodes

    交错磁项使手性 d 波超导原本的线节点变为 Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces，但在 (Mbₘₖ^α=0) 的交错磁节点处例外。原文表述为：*"the line nodes of the chiral d-wave superconductor become BFSs due to altermagnetism, except for the nodal lines of AMs."*

    • Altermagnetism strongly deforms chiral-superconductor surface states

    交错磁性不是微扰地移动表面态，而是强烈改变其形状：在 [001] 表面形成交叉平带，在 [100] 表面改变弧态。原文为：*"altermagnetism strongly deforms the surface states of the chiral superconductor, giving rise to crossed flat bands and modified surface arcs in the [001] and [100] surfaces."*

    • Crossed flat bands arise entirely from altermagnetism–superconductivity interplay

    表面弧态可从原手性超导继承，但交叉平带本质上来自交错磁性与手性 d 波超导的联合效应。原文强调：*"the crossed flat bands are entirely due to the interplay between altermagnetism and chiral d-wave superconductivity."*

    • Altermagnetic nodes determine the number of crossed-flat-band corners

    投影交错磁 Fermi 面后，三维中自旋简并的交错磁节点线决定交叉平带的角点数。原文表述：*"the altermagnetic nodes (spin-degenerate lines in 3D) define the number of corners of the crossed flat band."* 因此 dxy / dx²−y² 为四角，gxy(x²−y²) 为八角。

    • Superconducting nodes pin crossed flat bands to zero energy

    交叉平带之所以位于零能，不仅因为交错磁节点，还需要三维手性 d 波超导的节点结构。原文给出机制：*"due to the nodes of the 3D chiral d-wave superconductivity, the crossed flat bands appear at zero energy."*

    • The phenomenon generalizes beyond chiral d-wave to spin-triplet pz-wave superconductivity

    相同分析可作用于自旋三重态 (p_z) 波超导，说明机制依赖节点超导性与交错磁对称性，而非某个偶然模型。原文为：*"This analysis also applies to spin-triplet (p_z)-wave superconductivity."*

    • Crossed flat bands are generic and symmetry-tied

    交叉平带被归纳为由交错磁性与节点超导共同产生的通用现象，并与内禀晶体对称性相连。原文总结：*"the emergence of crossed flat bands is a generic phenomenon resulting from the interplay between altermagnetism and nodal superconductivity and hence tied to the inherent crystal symmetries."*

    ---

    Topological origin of crossed surface flat bands .—

    • Crossed flat bands have a symmetry-protected topological origin

    产生交叉平带所需的对称性也保证其拓扑来源。原文开宗明义：*"The symmetries required for the emergence of crossed flat bands also imply that they have a topological origin."*

    • In nodal superconductors without altermagnetism, 1D winding numbers use chiral symmetry from pTRS and PH

    无交错磁时，节点线超导中的一维绕数来自伪时间反演对称性 pTRS 与粒子-空穴对称性 PH 的组合。原文说明：*"a nonzero 1D winding number can be obtained with the chiral operator by combining the pseudo-time-reversal (pTRS) and particle-hole (PH) symmetries."*

    • pTRS removes the internal phase of the pair potential by a local gauge transformation

    手性配对具有内禀复相位，需通过局域规范变换抵消。原文解释：*"pTRS is the product of conventional TRS and local gauge transformation. This local gauge transformation is introduced to cancel out the inner phase of the pair potential."*

    • Altermagnetism breaks ordinary chiral symmetry by breaking time-reversal symmetry

    交错磁性破坏常规时间反演对称性，因此原有手征对称性不再成立。原文为：*"In the presence of altermagnetism, the chiral symmetry is broken because of the broken TRS by AMs."*

    • Pseudo-magnetic mirror symmetry replaces broken time-reversal symmetry

    尽管 TRS 被破坏，体系保留伪磁镜面对称性 pMMS，即 pTRS 与镜面对称性的乘积。原文表述：*"Still, the Hamiltonian keeps the pseudo-magnetic mirror symmetry (pMMS), which is given by the product of pTRS and mirror symmetry."*

    • dxy-wave altermagnetism has pMMS in xz and yz planes

    对 dxy 波交错磁体，pMMS 为

    [

    hatΘ'bₘₖhatHd¹BdG(kₓ,k_y,k_z)

    hatΘbₘₖ^{{}'dagger}

    =

    [hatHd¹BdG(-ν kₓ,ν k_y,k_z)]^*

    ]

    其中 (ν=+1) 对应 xz 平面，(ν=-1) 对应 yz 平面。原文明确：*"(ν=+1) and (ν=-1) in Eq. (4) indicate pMMSs for (dₓy)-wave AMs in the xz- and yz-planes, respectively."*

    • dx²−y²-wave altermagnetism has pMMS in diagonal mirror planes

    对 dx²−y² 波交错磁体，pMMS 为

    [

    hatΘ'bₘₖhatHd²BdG(kₓ,k_y,k_z)

    hatΘbₘₖ^{{}'dagger}

    =

    [hatHd²BdG(-ν k_y,-ν kₓ,k_z)]^*

    ]

    (ν=+1) 与 (ν=-1) 分别对应 (x=y) 与 (x=-y) 对角镜面。原文为：*"(ν=+1) and (ν=-1) in Eq. (5) indicate pMMSs for (dₓ²-y²)-wave AMs in the diagonal planes on (x=y) and (x=-y), respectively."*

    • g-wave altermagnetism inherits both pMMS sets

    gxy(x²−y²) 波交错磁体同时具有 dxy 与 dx²−y² 两类镜面对称性，因此能产生更多交叉平带角点。原文为：*"For (gₓy(x²-y²))-wave AMs, the system has both pMMSs given by Eq. (4) and Eq. (5)."*

    • Particle-hole symmetry is exact in the BdG Hamiltonian

    粒子-空穴对称性为

    [

    hatChatHαBdG(kₓ,k_y,k_z)hatCdagger

    =

    -

    [hatHBdGα(-kₓ,-k_y,-k_z)]^*,

    quad

    hatC=hatσ₀hatτ₁.

    ]

    原文给出：*"In addition to the pMMSs, (hatHαBdG(bmk)) has particle-hole symmetry."*

    • pMMS and PH generate chiral symmetry on magnetic mirror planes

    手征算符为

    [

    hatΓbₘₖ=-ihatChatΘ'bₘₖ.

    ]

    在磁镜面对称平面上，BdG 哈密顿量与该算符反对易。原文表述：*"Then, (hatHαBdG(bmk)) anticommutes with the chiral operator (hatΓbₘₖ=-ihatChatΘ'bₘₖ) on the magnetic mirror plane."*

    • Smooth surfaces perpendicular to magnetic mirror planes preserve the protecting symmetries

    拓扑表面态要求表面不破坏保护对称性；光滑且垂直于磁镜面的表面保留这些对称性。原文为：*"these magnetic mirror and chiral symmetries are still available on the smooth surfaces, which are perpendicular to the magnetic mirror planes."*

    • Nonzero winding numbers on symmetry lines protect crossed flat bands

    在表面 Brillouin 区的对称线上可定义绕数；非零值标志拓扑相和受保护表面态。原文说明：*"a winding number can be obtained on the symmetric lines, whose nonzero values signal the appearance of topological phases with topologically protected surface states."*

    • [001] crossed flat bands and [100] arcs are both topologically protected

    (kₓ,k_y) 轴或对角方向上的非零绕数保护 [001] 方向的交叉平带；xz 平面的 pMMS 保护 [100] 表面零能弧态。原文总结：*"both surface arcs and crossed flat bands are topologically protected and can be realized in 3D superconducting AMs."*

    • BFS regions invalidate the winding number because the bulk is gapless

    当 BFS 存在时，体能谱零能无隙，绕数不再良定义；因此 (k_zsim0) 附近表面弧态不预期产生零能共振。脚注指出：*"This topological protection does not happen in the case when BFS exists because the winding number is ill-defined for the gapless dispersion."*

    ---

    Conductance signatures of crossed flat bands .—

    • Detection is formulated through normal-metal / 3D superconducting-AM junctions

    为检测交叉平带，构建正常金属与三维超导交错磁体的隧穿结，分别考察 z 方向 [001] 与 x 方向 [100] 输运。原文为：*"we couple the 3D superconducting AM to a normal metal, such that we can assess transport along z and x directions."*

    • Conductance is computed using the Lee-Fisher tunneling Hamiltonian method

    电导公式为

    [

    σ(eV)=frac12πint₋ππint₋ππdtildebmk,

    barσ(tildebmk,eV),

    ]

    动量分辨电导由 Green 函数表达。原文说明：*"We obtain the conductance following the common tunneling Hamiltonian approach based on the Lee-Fisher formula."*

    • Momentum-dependent conductance is built from recursive Green functions

    (barσ(tildebmk,eV)) 使用 (hatGₙₘ) 与界面跃迁矩阵 (hatVⱼᵢ) 计算，其中 Green 函数由递归法得到。原文为：*"Green’s functions numerically obtained by using the recursive Green’s function method."*

    • Key numerical parameters are fixed in the figures

    [001] 电导图采用 (t_α=Δ)、(μ=-4.5t)、(Δ=0.01t)、势垒 (U_b=5t)、展宽 (δ=0.01Δ)。图注给出：*"Parameters: (tα=Δ), (μ=-4.5t), (Δ=0.01t), (Ub=5t), and (δ=0.01Δ)."*

    • Zero-bias [001] momentum-resolved conductance is dominated by crossed flat bands

    在 (eV=0) 时，(barσ(tildebmk,0)) 的最强强度来自 [001] 表面的交叉平带。原文指出：*"the strongest intensities come from the contribution of the crossed surface flat bands."*

    • dxy-wave AM produces four crossed-flat-band corners

    对 dxy 波交错磁体，零偏压动量分辨电导显示四个角点。原文为：*"For (dₓy)-wave AM, (barσ(tildebmk,eV=0)) reveals four corners."*

    • gxy(x²−y²)-wave AM produces eight crossed-flat-band corners

    对 gxy(x²−y²) 波交错磁体，零偏压动量分辨电导显示八个角点。原文为：*"while eight corners for (gₓy(x²-y²))-wave AM."* 这正对应其更多交错磁节点。

    • dx²−y²-wave AM gives four corners rotated by π/4

    对 dx²−y² 波交错磁体，角点数同为四个，但整个交叉平带相对 dxy 情形旋转 (π/4)。原文为：*"(barσ(tildebmk,eV=0)) also exhibits four corners but with a crossed flat band rotated by (π/4)."*

    • BFSs produce weaker but finite zero-bias conductance around crossed flat bands

    交叉平带附近存在较弱但非零强度，来源为 Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces。原文说明：*"(barσ(tildebmk,eV=0)) ... acquires lower but nonzero intensities around the crossed flat bands, which arise due to the BFS."*

    • A dark region appears from gapped dispersion with vanishing z velocity

    BFS 与交叉平带之间的暗区不是数值噪声，而来自有隙色散中沿 (z) 方向速度趋零的准粒子。原文指出：*"There also appears a darkish area between the BFS and crossed flat band ... originated from a gapped dispersion where quasiparticles attain vanishing velocity along z."*

    • Three transparency power laws coexist in the same superconducting AM

    零偏压动量分辨电导在三类区域有不同正常态透明度依赖：

    • 交叉平带：(barσsim abarσN⁰)
    • BFS：(barσsim bbarσN¹)
    • 有隙区：(barσsim cbarσN²)

    原文为：*"we obtain (barσ(tildebmk,eV=0)sim abarσₘ̊ N⁰+bbarσₘ̊ N¹+cbarσₘ̊ N²), ... unveiling three distinct types of fundamental power laws that coexist in 3D superconducting AMs."*

    • The constant and quadratic laws distinguish resonant and nonresonant Andreev reflection

    常数项 (2barσN⁰) 来自 Andreev 反射完美共振；二次项 (barσN²) 来自非共振 Andreev 反射。脚注说明：*"(2barσₘ̊ N⁰) and (barσₘ̊ N²) originates due to perfect resonance of Andreev reflections and Andreev reflection without resonance."*

    • Total [001] conductance develops a zero-bias peak reduced by altermagnetism

    总电导 (σ(eV)) 随偏压显示零偏压峰；交错磁强度 (t_α) 增大时峰高降低。原文写明：*"(σ(eV)) develops a zero-bias peak whose height decreases as the altermagnetic strength increases."*

    • The zero-bias conductance peak without altermagnetism comes from zero-energy ABSs

    无交错磁性时，大零偏压电导峰来自手性 d 波超导中的零能 Andreev 束缚态。原文表述：*"The presence of a large zero-bias conductance peak (ZBCP) without any altermagnetism is due to the zero-energy ABSs of chiral d-wave superconductors."*

    • g-wave altermagnets give a stronger and better formed ZBCP

    虽然三类交错磁体均表现为 ZBCP 被削弱，gxy(x²−y²) 情形峰形更清晰、更强。原文指出：*"the latter exhibits a stronger and well-formed ZBCP."*

    • ZBCP directly evidences [001] crossed surface flat bands

    [001] 总电导中的零偏压峰构成交叉平带的直接输运证据。原文总结：*"In all cases, the ZBCP constitutes direct evidence of the crossed surface flat bands formed at the [001] surface of 3D superconducting AMs."*

    ---

    Conductance along x direction and signatures of surface arcs .—

    • Transport is strongly direction dependent in 3D superconducting AMs

    沿 (x) 方向的电导与沿 (z) 方向不同，体现三维交错磁超导中的各向异性表面拓扑。开头表述为：*"Conductance along x reveals distinct signatures of the 3D superconducting AM, giving rise to direction-dependent transport in these systems."*

    • Zero-bias [100] conductance has high intensity near ky = 0

    对 dxy 与 gxy(x²−y²) 交错磁体，(barσ(tildebmk,0)) 在 (k_y=0) 附近出现高强度，源于 [100] 表面零能弧态。原文为：*"(barσ(tildebmk,eV=0)) develops high intensities around (k_y=0) due to the contribution of zero-energy surface arc states formed at the [100] surface."*

    • [100] surface arcs originate from xz-plane pMMS

    这些零能表面弧态不是普通边界态，而由 xz 平面伪磁镜面对称性保护。原文指出：*"these zero-energy surface arcs originate from the pMMS on the xz-plane."*

    • BFS interrupts the surface-arc conductance near kz = 0

    在 (k_z=0) 附近，表面弧态电导信号被 BFS 削弱或中断。原文为：*"the surface arc conductance signal is interrupted around (k_z=0) due to a reduced contribution coming from the BFSs."*

    • Bulk density of states confirms the role of BFSs

    BFS 对 [100] 表面电导的影响可通过对 (kₓ) 积分的零能体态密度确认。原文说明：*"the role of the BFS can indeed be confirmed by the bulk density of states integrated in (kₓ)."*

    • dx²−y²-wave AM produces spin-split surface arcs

    对 dx²−y² 波交错磁体，动量分辨零偏压电导显示自旋劈裂的表面弧态；这些弧态随 (k_y,k_z) 色散，并被 BFS 涂抹。原文表述：*"(barσ(tildebmk,eV=0)) reveals the formation of spin-split surface arc states, which disperse with (ky,z) and is smeared by the BFSs."*

    • The same three transparency power laws also appear for [100] transport

    与 [001] 类似，[100] 输运中零能表面弧态、BFS、有隙区分别对应 (2barσN⁰)、(barσN¹)、(barσN²)。原文为：*"we also find that (barσ(tildebmk,eV=0)) is given by (2barσₘ̊ N⁰), (barσₘ̊ N¹), and (barσₘ̊ N²) in the presence of zero-energy surface arcs, BFS, and gapped region."*

    • Without altermagnetism, [100] conductance is broad because of chiral edge modes

    无交错磁性时，总电导在零偏压附近是宽峰，而非尖锐 ZBCP；其来源是手性边缘模式。原文为：*"It exhibits a broad peaked profile around zero bias without altermagnetism ... resulting from the chiral edge modes."*

    • Finite dxy or g-wave altermagnetism sharpens the broad conductance profile into a ZBCP

    有限 dxy 或 gxy(x²−y²) 交错磁性改变手性边缘模式色散，使宽峰变尖，形成清晰零偏压峰。原文写明：*"This broad conductance profile sharpens at finite altermagnetism ... producing a clear ZBCP ... that stems from the surface arc states."*

    • dx²−y²-wave AM splits the zero-bias resonance into two peaks

    对 dx²−y² 波交错磁体，(σ(eV=0)) 共振分裂成两个峰，峰位偏移依赖交错磁强度。原文为：*"the resonance in (σ(eV=0)) splits into two, and the resonance shift depends on the altermagnetic strength."*

    • Spin-split total conductance originates from spin-split surface arcs

    双峰结构直接对应动量分辨电导中的自旋劈裂弧态。原文表述：*"this spin-split total conductance originates from the spin-split surface arcs observed in (barσ(tildebmk,eV=0))."*

    • The behavior resembles reported Sr₂RuO₄ transport

    [100] 方向的电导特征与 Sr₂RuO₄ 已报道输运类似，从而支持其可能由表面弧态与 BFS 控制。原文为：*"This behavior is similar to the reported transport in Sr2RuO4, supporting the idea that conductance along x is determined by the surface arc states and the BFS."*

    ---

    Conclusion / concluding unlabeled section

    • Crossed surface flat bands are generic topological states protected by crystal symmetries

    三维超导交错磁体中存在由内禀晶体对称性保护的交叉表面平带。结论句为：*"crossed surface flat bands emerge in three-dimensional superconducting altermagnets as a generic topological phenomenon protected by intrinsic crystal symmetries."*

    • Conductance can simultaneously detect crossed flat bands, arcs, and BFSs

    电导不仅探测 [001] 交叉平带，还可因输运方向不同而探测 [100] 表面弧态与 BFS。原文总结：*"the crossed flat bands can be detected by means of conductance, which depends on the transport direction and can also assess the formation of topological surface arcs and Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces."*

    • Momentum-resolved zero-bias conductance provides three diagnostic power laws

    三类幂律构成实验判据：拓扑零能表面态对应透明度零次幂，BFS 对应一次幂，有隙区对应二次幂。原文为：*"the zero-bias momentum-resolved conductance exhibits three distinct types of fundamental power laws, offering a solid way for detecting the emergent topological phases."*

    • Experimental probes include Doppler shift, ARPES, and quasiparticle interference

    可行实验包括 Doppler shift measurements、ARPES 和 quasiparticle interference。原文列出：*"by Doppler shift measurements ... ARPES ... and quasiparticle interference experiments."*

    • Low transparency and low temperature are needed to observe crossed flat bands

    交叉平带检测要求低界面透明度与低温，以增强隧穿谱中的零能表面态分辨率。原文指出：*"which would require low transparencies and low temperatures for observing the crossed flat bands."*

    • The results apply to multiple predicted 3D altermagnets and superconductors

    适用材料包括 CrSb、La₂CuO₄、UPt₃ 和 half-Heusler compounds。原文为：*"Our results apply to the large family of predicted 3D AMs, such as CrSb and La2CuO4, and superconducting UPt3 and half-Heusler compounds."*

    • Sr₂RuO₄ is highlighted as the most direct material platform

    Sr₂RuO₄ 同时具备预期交错磁性与手性 d 波超导，是测试预测的优先候选。原文强调：*"our work holds direct relevance in Sr2RuO4, where altermagnetism and chiral d-wave superconductivity are expected to coexist."*

    • Symmetry-preserving perturbations should not destroy crossed flat bands

    基于拓扑分析，保持保护对称性的扰动不会破坏交叉平带；多轨道、自旋轨道耦合和标量无序被列为可能稳健的扰动类型。原文为：*"found crossed flat bands are robust against symmetry-preserving perturbations, such as multi-orbital, spin-orbit coupling, and scalar disorder."*

    • Symmetry-breaking perturbations remain a key unresolved issue

    破坏伪磁镜面对称性或相关手征结构的扰动可能摧毁平带，需要进一步系统研究。原文指出：*"symmetry-breaking perturbations are very likely detrimental and require a thorough investigation."*

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持

    1. 术语解析

    • Altermagnetism / altermagnets（交错磁性 / 交错磁体）

    不是普通反铁磁性。关键特征是零净磁化与动量依赖自旋劈裂同时存在。普通共线反铁磁体常因 PT 或其他联合对称性保持 Kramers-like 自旋简并；交错磁体则允许无自旋轨道耦合条件下的自旋劈裂，但总磁矩仍为零。这里的 (Mbₘₖ^ασ₃τ₃) 正是这种交错磁劈裂的最小模型。

    • Crossed surface flat bands（交叉表面平带）

    “flat band” 指在表面 Brillouin 区的一条或一片动量区域中能量几乎固定；这里固定在零能。 “crossed” 不只是两条线相交，而是由不同镜面对称线保护的零能平带在表面动量空间形成带有角点的交叉几何结构。角点数由交错磁节点投影决定。

    • Bogoliubov-Fermi surfaces, BFSs（Bogoliubov-Fermi 面）

    在超导体中通常期待 Fermi 面被能隙打开；BFS 是 Bogoliubov 准粒子在零能处形成的二维闭合面。这里的条件是

    [

    [Mbₘₖ^α]²⁼ǎrepsilon²⁽bmk)+|barΔ(bmk)|².

    ]

    其物理含义是交错磁劈裂补偿了正常态能量与超导配对能，导致零能准粒子面残留。

    • Pseudo-magnetic mirror symmetry, pMMS（伪磁镜面对称性）

    “pseudo” 表示不是单纯时间反演或单纯镜面，而是包含局域规范变换的伪时间反演再乘以镜面对称。手性超导配对有复相位，单纯 TRS 不成立；通过规范变换去掉配对相位，再结合镜面操作，可恢复某些动量平面上的有效反对易结构。

    • Winding number（绕数）

    一维拓扑不变量，衡量沿某条动量路径时 BdG 哈密顿量相位结构绕原点的次数。非零绕数意味着边界必须出现零能态。这里绕数只能在 pMMS 允许定义手征对称性的对称线上成立；BFS 处体态无隙，绕数不良定义。

    2. 疑难查证

    • 为什么交错磁性既破坏 TRS，又能保护零能表面态？

    常规时间反演对称性被交错磁序破坏，因此传统节点超导中的手征保护机制失效。但交错磁序具有特定晶体镜面对称结构：某些镜面操作会把 (Mbₘₖ^α) 的符号以恰当方式变换回来。手性配对的复相位又可通过局域规范变换处理。于是 pTRS × mirror = pMMS 替代普通 TRS，与粒子-空穴对称性组合后，在镜面对称线上重新产生手征算符 (Γbₘₖ)。因此，保护来自“磁性 + 晶体镜面 + 超导规范结构”的联合对称性，而非普通 TRS。

    • 为什么 BFS 会削弱表面弧态的零能共振？

    零能表面态的拓扑保护通常要求给定表面动量下，垂直方向的一维体哈密顿量是有隙的，这样才能定义绕数。BFS 出现后，体态本身在零能处有连续谱；表面零能态不再是孤立共振，会与体零能态混合。结果是 [100] 表面弧态在 (k_zsim0) 附近被“打断”或涂抹，电导强度降低，且绕数不再良定义。

    • 为什么 [001] 和 [100] 表面看到不同拓扑态？

    [001] 表面投影保留 (kₓ,k_y)，正好暴露手性 d 波超导在 xy 平面节点线与交错磁节点的交织结构，因此形成交叉平带。[100] 表面投影保留 (k_y,k_z)，更直接看到由点节点连接而来的表面弧态，同时 (k_z=0) 附近 BFS 对其产生强烈调制。方向差异本质上来自节点结构和镜面对称平面相对于表面法向的几何关系。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联

    1. 创新性判断

    • 从二维交错磁超导拓扑态推进到三维交错磁超导拓扑态

    过去 2–5 年内，交错磁超导研究主要集中在二维异质结、Majorana 模式、Josephson 效应、有限动量配对、非互易输运和二维平带/ABS。关键未解问题是：三维交错磁体中的节点超导、表面态与拓扑保护如何组织。此工作给出三维 BdG 模型、对称性分类、拓扑绕数和电导判据，填补 3D AM superconductivity 的表面拓扑空白。

    • 提出“交叉表面平带”作为三维交错磁超导的独特拓扑对象

    传统节点超导平带通常继承投影 Fermi 面形状；Weyl 超导表面态通常表现为弧态。这里的表面态具有新几何：由交错磁节点决定角点数，由超导节点线钉扎零能，由 pMMS 保护。角点数 = 交错磁晶体对称性指纹 是明确的新颖结构。

    • 揭示交错磁性把超导节点线转化为 BFS，并与表面态共存

    BFS 过去多见于多轨道、TRS 破缺或非常规配对讨论；这里在单轨道交错磁 BdG 模型中，由零净磁化的交错磁性产生 BFS。更重要的是，BFS 不是孤立讨论，而是与交叉平带、表面弧态共同决定输运谱。

    • 建立三类透明度幂律共存的实验诊断

    零偏压动量分辨电导中同时出现

    [

    barσN⁰,quad barσN¹,quad barσN²

    ]

    三类幂律，对应拓扑零能表面态、BFS、有隙区。这比单纯报告 ZBCP 更有判别力，因为 ZBCP 可能来自多种机制，而透明度幂律能区分共振 Andreev 反射、BFS 贡献和非共振过程。

    • 提供与 Sr₂RuO₄ 直接相关的理论路线

    Sr₂RuO₄ 的超导配对长期争议极大；近期交错磁序预测与三维手性 d 波方案使其成为天然测试平台。若低温隧穿谱、ARPES 或 QPI 在 [001] 与 [100] 表面分别观测到交叉平带与被 BFS 调制的弧态，将为“Sr₂RuO₄ 中交错磁性与手性 d 波超导共存”提供强证据。

    • 解决前人尚未系统处理的问题

    具体解决了四个问题：

    • 三维交错磁节点如何决定表面零能态几何；
    • TRS 被交错磁性破坏后，何种对称性继续保护零能态；
    • BFS 与拓扑表面态如何共存、竞争和调制电导；
    • 如何用方向依赖隧穿谱区分交叉平带、表面弧态与体 BFS。
    阅读原文 ↗
    原文链接页内定位
  15. 15
    准零脉冲驱动自旋量子位交换#
    Driving Exchange Interaction in Spin Qubits with Quasi-Zero Pulses#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 物理 / 凝聚态📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 Julian D. Teske, Remy L. Delva, Shobhan Kulshreshtha, Yuval Baum, Florian Luthi, Fahd A. Mohiyaddin, Rostyslav Savytskyy, Thomas Watson, Pranav S. Mundada🔥 AI 82

    💡 亮点：准零脉冲抑制交换门畸变误差。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题交换耦合自旋量子比特需要用栅压脉冲精确驱动量子点中电子的交换相互作用，但交换能对电压近似指数敏感，控制链路中的 RC 尾迹、bias-tee 滤波、低频残余偏置和长时间记忆会把微小波形畸变放大成过旋转、Rabi 条纹弯曲和门保真度下降；传统全预失真可补偿畸变，却需要大量传递函数参数，难以扩展到大规模自动校准。
    创新方法提出 quasi-zero pulses：把传统正负面积完全抵消的 net-zero 脉冲，改造成“净正但显著减小面积”的正-负矩形原子脉冲；用幅度比 γ 调低负脉冲强度，使负片段主要抵消电路/电荷畸变而不执行反向量子门。Aha 点在于发现严格 net-zero 因正片段总先于负片段会动态过补偿，最优不是零面积，而是约 γ≈70% 的准零面积，让 Rabi 中心条纹从弯曲变直。
    工作流程输入为交换量子比特的目标单量子比特门和测得的阶跃响应畸变；先构造正电压驱动段、负电压补偿段和 spacer 间隔组成的原子脉冲；扫描 γ、片段时长和 spacer，让重复 N(ψ) 脉冲产生的 Rabi fringe 中心峰尽量排成直线；再将优化原子脉冲替换标准方波片段，形成完整 exchange-only 单量子比特门集；最后用 Boulder Opal 仿真、Intel Tunnel Falls 六量子点硬件开放环测试和 blind randomized benchmarking 输出门保真度、泄漏率、门时长与所需调参量。
    关键结果无滤波纯正方波参考脉冲在 30 ns 门时长下保真度仅 99.66%；12 参数全滤波预失真达到 99.96%。无滤波 quasi-zero 脉冲在 30 ns、0 个滤波参数下达到 99.93%，在 40 ns 下达到 99.94%；quasi-zero 结合 752 ns 或 1 µs 长时间尺度滤波，仅需 2 个参数即可达到 99.95%，几乎贴近全滤波性能，同时泄漏约 0.01%。短时间尺度滤波反而降至 99.90%，说明 quasi-zero 已有效压制短时畸变。
    应用价值该研究把高保真交换控制从“多参数传递函数校准”转向“低复杂度脉冲形状工程”，显著减少自旋量子比特 tune-up 的调参维度和漂移风险，适合工业化量子处理器中的自动化、大规模交换相互作用校准；方法可望扩展到 singlet-triplet qubit 的单量子比特门、Loss-DiVincenzo qubit 的双量子比特门，以及滤波能力受限但传输线更短的低温电子学控制系统。

    第一部分：核心概览 (Overview)

    提出quasi-zero pulses，把传统net-zero脉冲从零时间积分推广为“净正但显著减小”的时间积分，用于抑制交换耦合自旋量子比特中的线性动态脉冲畸变。在 Intel Tunnel Falls 六量子点器件上，单量子比特门保真度达到 99.93–99.95%，接近全预失真滤波的 99.96%，但调参量从 12 个降至 0–2 个。该工作将高保真交换控制与可扩展自动校准直接关联，突出低复杂度脉冲工程在工业化自旋量子处理器中的价值。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Driving Exchange Interaction in Spin Qubits with Quasi-Zero Pulses》（None，）

    背景

    半导体自旋量子比特具备短门时间、高门保真度、小尺寸和工业制造兼容性。交换耦合是实现单量子比特与双量子比特门的核心机制，但交换能对栅压近似呈指数依赖，导致控制信号中的微小畸变显著放大为门误差。传统预失真滤波可补偿线性动态畸变，但需要标定大量参数。

    方法

    构造由正、负矩形片段组成的原子脉冲，引入幅度比 γ 控制负脉冲强度。net-zero pulse 对应零时间积分，quasi-zero pulse 对应 0 < γ < 1 的净正积分。结合 Boulder Opal 数值仿真、开放环硬件测试和 blind randomized benchmarking，系统比较不同脉冲长度、γ、滤波方案和调参复杂度。

    结果

    纯正方波参考脉冲无滤波时保真度为 99.66%；全滤波方案达到 99.96%，需 12 个滤波参数。无滤波 quasi-zero 脉冲在 30 ns 总门时长达到 99.93%，在 40 ns 达到 99.94%。结合长时间尺度滤波，仅需 2 个参数即可达到 99.95%。

    讨论

    严格 net-zero 脉冲会在实验相关时间尺度上产生过补偿，原因与正负片段顺序偏置有关：正片段总是先于负片段。quasi-zero 通过降低负片段幅度，使正负曲率尽可能抵消；典型最优幅度比约 γ ≈ 70%。

    局限

    未给出随机基准测试的不确定度、样本量或统计显著性。负电压片段对量子点形变、位移、串扰、杂散耦合的影响仍需深入分析。双量子比特门尚未验证。

    结论

    quasi-zero 脉冲在保持高保真和短门时长的同时显著减少校准参数，适合大规模、自自动化的交换耦合校准。该策略有望推广至 singlet-triplet qubit 和 Loss-DiVincenzo qubit 等依赖交换驱动的体系。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析 (Section-by-Section Condensing)

    Abstract

    Pulse distortions limit exchange-gate accuracy

    交换耦合自旋量子比特的高保真门依赖对电子间exchange interaction的精确控制，而控制脉冲畸变会直接限制精度。核心问题被明确限定为：*"The implementation of high-fidelity quantum gates for spin qubits requires accurate control of exchange interactions between electrons confined in quantum dots, but pulse distortions can limit this control accuracy."* 交换控制对象是量子点中受限电子之间的相互作用，误差来源是控制链路中的脉冲形状偏离。

    Convolution-based compensation is accurate but calibration-heavy

    线性动态畸变原则上可通过对控制信号做适当卷积来补偿，但需要知道系统transfer function，因此必须标定大量参数。摘要给出清晰限制：*"Although linear-dynamical distortions can be compensated for by appropriately convolving the control signal, determining the necessary convolution requires detailed knowledge of the distortion’s transfer function, and therefore the calibration of numerous parameters."* 这直接指向可扩展性瓶颈：不是补偿不可行，而是参数标定成本过高。

    Net-zero pulses motivate a low-parameter alternative

    另一条路线是设计总时间积分为零的控制脉冲，使正负片段相互抵消，从而削弱线性动态畸变。关键表述为：*"Alternatively, control pulses can be designed to have a net-zero time integral canceling out linear-dynamical pulse distortions."* 这里的“canceling out”并非通过系统辨识反卷积，而是利用脉冲对称性和面积抵消降低低频残留。

    Quasi-zero pulses generalize net-zero pulses

    核心创新是将严格零积分推广到quasi-zero pulses：允许净正时间积分，但显著小于普通正脉冲。摘要中的定义为：*"We generalize net-zero pulse designs to quasi-zero pulses allowing net-positive but reduced time integrals."* 这一点解决了严格 net-zero 在实际交换控制中可能过补偿的问题，同时保留畸变抵消能力。

    Complete exchange-only gate sets are constructed and benchmarked

    quasi-zero 设计不仅用于单个脉冲，而是系统发展为exchange-only qubits的完整门集，并分析时长、保真度与调参复杂度的权衡。证据为：*"Using these pulse designs, we systematically develop complete gate sets for exchange-only qubits, and study the resulting tradeoffs between pulse duration, fidelity, and the required number of tunable parameters, both in simulation and experiment."* 方法层面同时包含仿真与实验。

    Tunnel Falls experiments show near full-filter fidelity with fewer parameters

    优化后的门脉冲在 Intel Tunnel Falls six-dot device上测试，达到与全滤波方法相近的保真度和相同门时长，但调参量更少。摘要给出结果定位：*"We benchmark the optimized gate pulses on Intel’s Tunnel Falls six-dot device and show they achieve fidelities similar to those obtained with a full filtering approach, with identical pulse durations and fewer tuning parameters."* 该结果直接支撑大规模校准价值：*"This reduction in complexity opens the door to fast and easily automated calibration schemes compatible with large-scale commercial quantum devices."*

    ---

    I Introduction

    Semiconductor spin qubits combine speed, fidelity, and compactness

    半导体自旋量子比特被定位为容错量子计算的重要候选，因为同时具备短门时长、高门保真度和小特征尺寸。原文表述为：*"Semiconductor spin qubits are among the most promising candidates for the realization of a fault-tolerant quantum computer, since they combine short gate times and high gate fidelities with small feature sizes."* 这种组合使其相比许多平台更适合高密度集成。

    Industrial fabrication progress strengthens scalability

    自旋量子比特向工业化扩展的基础来自 300 mm 和 200 mm 制造线上的高质量阵列制备。具体证据包括：*"high-quality qubit arrays in 300 mm ... and 200 mm ... fabrication lines for silicon-germanium-based systems"*，以及全硅器件：*"all-silicon devices ... in a 300 mm ... fabrication line."* 这些数字说明研究背景并非小规模实验室器件，而是面向晶圆级制造。

    Cryogenic controllers further support scaling

    低温控制器部署进一步支持 exchange-only qubit 的扩展。原文为：*"The recent deployment of cryogenic controllers for exchange-only qubits further facilitates the scaling of spin qubits for building a fault-tolerant quantum computer."* 低温控制与短传输路径相关，也与后文对 cryo-electronics 的展望呼应。

    Exchange interaction is the central entangling and control mechanism

    交换相互作用是量子点受限电子自旋纠缠的主要机制，也是多数自旋量子比特实现单、双量子门的常用技术。关键表述为：*"The exchange interaction is the primary mechanism used to entangle the spins of confined electrons in quantum dots."* 以及：*"manipulation of the exchange coupling is a commonly used technique to realize single- and two-qubit quantum gates in most spin qubit implementations."*

    Electric base-band pulses control exchange via wave-function overlap

    交换相互作用可通过电学基带脉冲驱动，改变静电限制势并改变电子波函数重叠。机制描述为：*"This interaction can be driven with electric base-band pulses, which manipulate the electrostatic confinement potential and consequently the electrons’ wave-function overlap."* 这也解释了为什么控制链路中的电压畸变会转化为交换误差。

    Exchange-only qubits use only exchange-driving electrical signals

    exchange-only qubit 是完全依靠电信号驱动交换相互作用的自旋量子比特平台。定义为：*"The exchange-only qubit is designed as a spin qubit platform that is exclusively controlled via such electrical signals driving the exchange interaction."* 这使得脉冲形状工程成为该平台的核心控制问题，而非辅助优化。

    Exchange-only qubits already support high-fidelity gates and 2D scalability

    已有 exchange-only qubit 实现高保真单量子比特门与双量子比特门，并展示二维阵列可扩展性。证据为：*"Exchange-only qubits have been used to realize high-fidelity single-qubit and two-qubit gates, and have also been shown to be scalable into two-dimensional arrays."* 研究目标因此是提高控制鲁棒性和校准可扩展性，而不是证明平台可行性。

    Exponential voltage dependence amplifies pulse distortions

    交换能对电压近似呈指数依赖，因此对电信号畸变极其敏感。原文为：*"The exchange interaction energy has an approximate exponential dependence on the voltage and is, therefore, extremely sensitive to any distortion of the electric signals."* 这是整项工作的物理根源：微小电压残留会产生非线性放大的交换误差。

    Existing mitigation methods require many parameters

    已有策略包括有限/无限冲激响应滤波器和预失真，但需要调节大量参数。具体表述为：*"These strategies include the application of finite and infinite impulse response filters on control signals or mitigating the distortion effects with pre-distortions."* 限制为：*"these methods necessitate the tuning of numerous parameters to achieve high fidelities."* 参数多会导致调试慢和漂移敏感：*"a high number of tunable parameters leads to long tuning times and less stable outcomes due to parameter drift over time."*

    Net-zero pulses suppress residual offsets and low-frequency distortions

    net-zero Ansatz 通过正负脉冲片段抵消，使时间积分为零，用低参数结构缓解 RC 时间常数、bias-tee 滤波、残余偏置、长稳定时间和低频畸变。关键描述为：*"The net-zero pulse Ansatz provides pulses with a net-zero time integral, where positive and negative pulse segments cancel each other out."* 其作用为：*"mitigate effects of RC time constants and bias-tee filtering by ensuring that residual offsets, long settling times, and low frequency distortions cancel out."*

    Superconducting-qubit precedent motivates spin-qubit adaptation

    net-zero 设计已在超导量子比特中实现高保真门。原文为：*"In the field of superconducting qubits, it has been successfully utilized to yield high-fidelity gates."* 该研究将这一思想迁移并改造到 exchange-only spin qubit，面对的是交换相互作用的指数电压响应而非超导频率调谐环境。

    Quasi-zero pulses are introduced on Intel Tunnel Falls

    实验平台是 Intel Tunnel Falls六点器件，运行方式是 exchange-only qubit。核心设计为：*"We generalize the traditional net-zero pulse framework into a class of robust 'quasi-zero' pulses that feature a net-positive but significantly reduced time integral."* “net-positive but reduced”构成区别于 net-zero 的关键创新。

    Tradeoffs are mapped with hardware testing and Boulder Opal simulation

    通过开放环硬件测试与 Boulder Opal 数值仿真，研究脉冲时长、门保真度和校准复杂度之间的基础权衡。证据为：*"Combining open-loop hardware testing with numeric simulations via the Boulder Opal software package, we map out the fundamental trade-offs governing pulse duration, gate fidelity, and calibration complexity."*

    Blind randomized benchmarking validates operational performance

    最终使用blind randomized benchmarking验证优化 quasi-zero 门在操作层面的保真度与时长。关键表述为：*"using blind randomized benchmarking, we demonstrate that these optimized quasi-zero gates achieve operational fidelities and gate durations comparable to deeply optimized, multi-parameter pre-distortion filters."* 其核心优势是：*"fundamentally minimizing the number of parameters requiring active experimental calibration."*

    ---

    II Net-Zero pulses

    Linear-dynamical distortions are modeled by a step response

    研究起点是控制信号中的脉冲畸变；在线性动态假设下，畸变可由系统对阶跃电压的响应描述。原文为：*"Under the assumption that these distortions are linear-dynamical in nature, they can be described by the system’s response to a voltage signal with the shape of a step function."* 这把复杂硬件链路压缩为可测量的响应函数。

    Measured step response uses multi-exponential relaxation

    器件中的响应 (vᵣₑₛ) 通过预实验测量，并拟合为

    [

    vᵣₑₛ(t)=αłeft(1-sumᵢ cᵢ e⁻t/τᵢi̊ght).

    ]

    原文为：*"this response (vᵣₑₛ) was measured in preliminary experiments and fitted to the functional form"*。其中 (α) 是阶跃幅度，(cᵢ) 与 (τᵢ) 是拟合参数：*"where (α) denotes the amplitude of the step function in time (t). The fitting parameters are the magnitudes (cᵢ) (and the timescales (τᵢ))."*

    Distortion amplitudes and timescales span large ranges

    拟合参数的量级为 (cᵢ₌₀.03) 到 (0.1)，时间尺度为 4 ns 到 1 ms。原文为：*"which assume values between 0.03 and 0.1 (4 ns and 1 ms)."* 该跨度覆盖单脉冲内瞬态与跨门序列记忆效应。

    Nanosecond distortions are intra-pulse; microsecond distortions create memory

    短时间尺度畸变在单个脉冲内完全出现并衰减，长时间尺度畸变会依赖之前执行的脉冲或量子门。原文为：*"Short timescales on the order of nanoseconds describe distortions that fully arise and decay within a single pulse, while long timescales of microseconds introduce memory effects depending on the previously executed pulses or quantum gates."* 这解释了为什么随机序列中的历史依赖会破坏门一致性。

    Exchange-only qubits use symmetric rectangular base-band pulses

    所研究的 exchange-only qubit 通过对耦合量子点对的 barrier gates 施加对称矩形基带脉冲控制。原文为：*"The considered exchange-only qubits are controlled with symmetric rectangular base-band pulses controlling barrier gates in pairs of coupled quantum dots."* barrier gate 控制的是量子点间的隧穿势垒与交换耦合。

    Atomic pulses concatenate positive and negative segments

    为控制时间积分，构造由正片段和负片段串接的原子脉冲。原文为：*"To control the time integral of our control pulses, we construct control signals by concatenating atomic pulses with positive and negative segments."* 该设计允许在不引入复杂滤波参数的情况下改变低频响应。

    Amplitude ratio γ defines rectangular, net-zero, and quasi-zero pulses

    图 1 中，正负段的持续时间和幅度可通过幅度比 (γ) 缩放。定义为：*"Both the positive and negative segments can be scaled in duration and amplitude by changing the amplitude ratio (γ)."*

    具体分类为：*"A rectangular exchange pulse would correspond to an amplitude ratio of (γ=0), while a net-zero pulse would correspond to (γ=tₚₒₛ/tₙₑg). Quasi-zero pulses correspond to other values of (0<γ<tₚₒₛ/tₙₑg)."* 后续假设 (tₚₒₛ=tₙₑg)，因此 net-zero 对应 (γ=1)，quasi-zero 对应 (0<γ<1)。

    Temporal spacers reduce bleed-through from short-time distortions

    每个片段之后加入 temporal spacer，用于控制短时间畸变导致的脉冲串扰。原文为：*"After each segment, we include a temporal spacer to control for short-time distortions that could lead to bleed-through effects."* 这里的 bleed-through 指前一片段残留响应污染后一片段或后续原子脉冲。

    Exchange-only dynamics follow a two-axis effective Hamiltonian

    量子比特演化由有效哈密顿量

    [

    H=J_z(v_z)fracσ_z2+Jₙ₍ᵥₙ₎fracσₙ2

    ]

    描述。原文为：*"The evolution of an exchange-only qubit is described by the effective Hamiltonian"*。其中 (Jᵢ) 是由电压 (vᵢ) 驱动的交换相互作用：*"where (Jᵢ) denotes the exchange interaction driven by voltage (vᵢ) for (iinz,n)."*

    The N-axis is tilted by 120° relative to Z

    (σ_z) 是 Pauli Z 算符，(σₙ) 生成相对 Z 轴倾斜 120° 的旋转。原文为：*"(σ_z) is the Pauli Z operator and (σₙ) generates a rotation around an axis that is tilted by 120° with respect to the Z-axis."* 这说明单量子比特通用控制可通过两个非共线交换旋转轴实现。

    Exchange grows exponentially with barrier voltage

    交换相互作用与 barrier gate 电压关系近似为

    [

    Jᵢ₍ᵥᵢ₎propto evᵢ/v₀.

    ]

    原文为：*"The exponential relation between the exchange interaction and the barrier gate voltage is well-approximated over a large range of values by the function (Jᵢ₍ᵥᵢ₎propto evᵢ/v₀)."* 指数关系使正电压段强烈驱动交换，而负电压段交换被压低。

    Negative pulse segments behave approximately as idle evolution

    由于指数关系，负片段的交换作用被强烈抑制，近似为空闲行为，因此预期不会显著改变量子态。原文为：*"This relation strongly suppresses the exchange interaction at negative segments leading to an idling behavior and we therefore expect the negative pulse segments not to affect the evolution of the qubit’s state."* 这是使用负脉冲抵消畸变而不执行反向量子门的关键条件。

    Experimental perturbation sequence probes long-time distortions

    实验通过沿 N 轴施加近似 (π) 旋转并重复 (Nₚ) 次检测畸变。图 2 描述为：*"The qubit is initialized, (Nₚ) repetitions of (N(ψ)) pulses are applied and the qubit is read out."* 每个 (N(ψ)) 脉冲被调谐为绕 n 轴旋转角 (ψ)：*"Each (N(ψ)) pulse is tuned to rotate the qubit an angle (ψ) around the n-axis."*

    Reference positive pulses show repetition-dependent over-rotation

    纯正方波参考脉冲 ((γ=0)) 会因长时间扰动在较大重复次数下产生系统性过旋转。原文预测为：*"For purely positive square pulses as a reference pulse ((γ=0)), we expect the long-time perturbations to cause systematic over-rotations at higher repetition numbers."* 实验现象为：*"These time-dependent over-rotations are visible as a curvature in the Rabi fringes."*

    Net-zero pulses eliminate visible fringe shifts

    采用 net-zero 脉冲后，Rabi fringe 的系统性位移消失。关键证据为：*"we observe that these systematic shifts of the fringe pattern vanish when employing net-zero pulses."* 这被解释为线性动态长时间畸变被抵消的证据：*"This is a clear indication that the long-time distortions are partially caused by a linear-dynamical effect like charge accumulation, for example."*

    Boulder Opal simulations use explicit distortion parameters

    仿真基于 Eq. 2 的有效哈密顿量，并使用由 Eq. 1 阶跃响应提取的 transfer function。参数为 (α=1)，(c=(0.1,0.03,0.03,0.03))，(τ=(4,50,200,1000))。原文为：*"The simulation is based on the effective Hamiltonian from Eq. 2 and uses a transfer function extracted from the step response in Eq. 1 with (α=1), (c=(0.1,,0.03,,0.03,,0.03)) and (τ=(4,,50,,200,,1000))."* 单位在文本中对应 ns 量级仿真时间常数。

    Strict net-zero pulses over-correct distortions

    仿真显示 (γ=1) 的严格 net-zero 原子脉冲会使中心 fringe 曲率反向弯曲，表现为过补偿。图 3 描述为：*"We observe that the net-zero pulse bends the curvature of the central fringe and over-corrects the curvature on the considered time-scale."* 这说明“零积分”不是在所有实验时间尺度上的最优设计。

    Segment ordering likely causes over-correction bias

    过补偿被归因于负片段和正片段顺序的偏置，因为正片段总是先于负片段。原文为：*"We assume that this effect is caused by a bias due to the order of negative and positive segments, where the positive segments always precede the negative segments."* 因此严格面积抵消不能完全等价于动态响应抵消。

    Quasi-zero γ is optimized by straightening central fringe alignment

    最优 (γ) 通过让中心 fringe 峰值尽量对齐直线获得。图 3 方法为：*"The optimal amplitude relation (γ) of a quasi-zero pulse is found by maximizing the alignment of the teal dots along the central fringe to a straight line."* 理想情况是无时间依赖的过旋转或欠旋转：*"An ideal alignment would provide a pulse amplitude that does not show any time-dependent over or under-rotations."*

    Typical optimal γ is around 70%

    对于测得阶跃响应的典型配置，最优幅度比约为 (γapprox70%)。原文为：*"For typical configurations with the measured step response, an amplitude ratio around (γapprox70%) seems to be ideal."* 此时负曲率和正曲率在目标时间尺度上最大程度抵消：*"the negative and positive curvatures cancel each other to the largest possible extent on the considered timescales."*

    ---

    III Quasi-Zero Gate Set Performance

    Single-qubit gate sets substitute atomic pulses for square segments

    单量子比特门集沿用 Ref. [9]，但把标准方波片段替换为图 1 的原子脉冲，并优化 (γ)。原文为：*"We realize the single-qubit gate set described in Ref. [9] by substituting our atomic pulse described in Fig. 1 for the standard square pulse segment and optimizing the amplitude ratio (γ)."* 这说明 quasi-zero 是门集级替换，而非单门特例。

    Blind randomized benchmarking measures gate-set quality

    门集质量通过blind randomized benchmarking评估。原文为：*"We assess the quality of the resulting gate sets with blind randomized benchmarking."* 表 1 给出单量子比特 randomized benchmarking fidelity 和 leakage，但未报告置信区间、样本量或 P 值。

    Pre-distortion combinations are also evaluated after tuning free parameters

    quasi-zero 脉冲还与预失真滤波组合测试，并在所有自由预失真参数调谐后测量性能。原文为：*"We also consider combinations of pre-distortions with our atomic pulses. In this case, we measure the performance after tuning all free pre-distortion parameters."* 这允许比较“低参数 quasi-zero”与“多参数滤波”及二者混合策略。

    Table 1 systematically varies filter type, segment durations, γ, fidelity, and leakage

    表 1 包含 8 组设置：参考脉冲 #1–2 和 quasi-zero 脉冲 #3–8。原文说明为：*"We benchmark reference (#1-2) and quasi-zero (#3-8) pulses combined with a selection of pre-distortions and variations in the individual pulse segment durations."* 参数包括 pre-distortion 类型、滤波参数数目、(tₚₒₛ)、(tzₑᵣₒ)、(tₙₑg)、(tₛₚₐcₑ)、(tₜₒₜₐₗ)、(γ)、fidelity、leakage。

    Segment durations affect distortion dynamics and leakage susceptibility

    片段时长显著影响畸变动力学，例如更长的 spacer 可部分抵消原子脉冲之间的 bleed-through。原文为：*"These segment durations can have a strong influence on the distortion dynamics, for example when long spacer times (tₛₚₐcₑ) partially cancel bleed-through between atomic pulses."* 同时，总门时间影响超精细噪声导致的泄漏：*"The resulting total gate times affect the susceptibility to leakage caused by hyperfine noise."*

    Filter variants target short and long distortion timescales

    #6–8 组滤波方法覆盖短时间和长时间尺度的预失真。原文为：*"The different filter methods (#6-8) cover filter choices selectively filtering pre-distortions on short and long timescales."* #6 使用 30 ns 滤波，#7 使用 752 ns，#8 使用 1 µs / 1000 ns 长时间尺度滤波。

    Unfiltered positive reference pulse reaches only 99.66% fidelity

    #1 作为无预失真的纯参考脉冲，(γ=0)，总时长 30 ns，滤波参数 0，保真度 99.66%，leakage 0.01%。原文为：*"Its fidelity is limited by the distortions to 99.66%."* 该设置用于量化脉冲畸变的损害：*"The detrimental effect of the pulse distortions is captured by using pulse setting #1 as our reference pulse without any pre-distortions."*

    Full filtering reaches 99.96% but requires 12 parameters

    #2 是全滤波参考，(γ=0)，总时长 30 ns，滤波参数 12，保真度 99.96%，leakage 0.01%。原文为：*"The target performance is established by the full filtering approach ... where the fidelity is substantially increased up to 99.96% at the expense of introducing 12 tunable parameters."* 它代表畸变被强烈抑制时的上限参考：*"This pulse provides a reference point for the fidelity when pulse distortions are strongly suppressed."*

    Quasi-zero setting #3 reaches 99.93% with no tuning parameters
