    #3 为无预失真 quasi-zero，滤波参数 0，(tₚₒₛ=10) ns，(tzₑᵣₒ=0) ns，(tₙₑg=10) ns，(tₛₚₐcₑ=10) ns，总时长 30 ns，(γ=0.25)，保真度 99.93%，leakage 0.01%。原文为：*"In setting #3, we consider a quasi-zero pulse that reaches a fidelity of 99.93% coming close to the performance of the fully filtered setting #2 of the same total duration of 30 ns, but without any required tuning parameters."*

    Longer spacing improves fidelity to 99.94% at 40 ns

    #4 将 negative segment 后 spacing 增至 20 ns，总时长 40 ns，(γ=0.5)，无滤波参数，保真度 99.94%，leakage 0.01%。原文为：*"The fidelity can be further increased by increasing the spacing time after the negative segment to 20 ns bringing the total pulse duration to 40 ns while achieving a fidelity of 99.94% as in setting #4."*

    Longer drive segments reduce fidelity to 99.91%

    #5 将驱动片段增至 20 ns，总时长 60 ns，(γ=0.4)，无滤波参数，保真度 99.91%，leakage 0.02%。原文为：*"Also increasing the driving segments to 20 ns as in setting #5 reduced the fidelity to 99.91%."* 这显示“更慢更长”并非单调更优。

    Pulse-duration tradeoff reflects hyperfine noise versus charge noise

    长脉冲更受磁噪声影响，短而强的脉冲需要更高驱动电压，又因交换的指数电压依赖而更受电荷噪声影响。原文为：*"This demonstrates the tradeoff between longer pulse durations and higher driving amplitudes."* 机制为：*"Long pulses are affected more strongly by magnetic noise, while the exponential relation between the exchange interaction and the driving voltage increases the susceptibility to charge noise at higher driving amplitudes."*

    Short-timescale filtering degrades quasi-zero performance

    #6 在 quasi-zero 上加入 30 ns 短时间尺度滤波，滤波参数 4，(tₜₒₜₐₗ=40) ns，(γ=0.525)，保真度 99.90%，leakage 0.01%。原文为：*"Adding a filter on a short time scale of 30 ns, as in setting #6, reduced the fidelity to 99.90% indicating that the quasi-zero pulses are already sufficient to reduce distortions on short timescales."* 这表明短时滤波可能与 quasi-zero 内建补偿重复甚至冲突。

    Long-timescale filtering plus quasi-zero reaches 99.95% with only 2 parameters

    #7 使用 752 ns 长时间尺度预失真，滤波参数 2，总时长 40 ns，(γ=0.55)，保真度 99.95%，leakage 0.01%。#8 使用 1 µs / 1000 ns 长时间尺度预失真，滤波参数 2，总时长 40 ns，(γ=0.55)，保真度 99.95%，leakage 0.01%。原文为：*"In settings #7 and #8, we observe that a combination of net-zero pulses with long-time pre-distortions on the timescales of 752 ns or 1000 ns achieved a fidelity of 99.95% coming close to the performance of the fully corrected pulse within measurement accuracy, while requiring only 2 tuning parameters."*

    Optimized γ does not fully cancel large-timescale errors

    长时间预失真仍能进一步提升保真度，说明仅优化 (γ) 尚未完全抵消所有长时间尺度误差。原文为：*"This high fidelity shows that the optimization of the amplitude ratio (γ) leads to pulses that do not fully cancel out errors on larger timescales."* 因此 quasi-zero 是低复杂度强基线，而非严格替代所有传递函数补偿。

    Overall performance matches best references with fewer parameters

    整体结论是 quasi-zero 脉冲可达到与最佳参考脉冲相近的保真度和时长，同时显著减少需优化参数。原文为：*"Overall, we observe that quasi-zero pulses can reach similar fidelities and durations as the best reference pulses, but with fewer parameters that need to be optimized."* 数值上，#3 的 99.93% / 30 ns / 0 参数接近 #2 的 99.96% / 30 ns / 12 参数；#7–8 的 99.95% / 40 ns / 2 参数接近全滤波性能。

    ---

    IV Conclusion

    Quasi-zero pulses provide low-complexity mitigation of linear-dynamical distortions

    quasi-zero 控制脉冲被确认为缓解 exchange-coupled spin qubit 中线性动态脉冲畸变的低复杂度框架。原文为：*"quasi-zero control pulses provide a highly effective, low-complexity framework for mitigating linear-dynamical pulse distortions in exchange-coupled spin qubits."* 其价值在于无需完整传递函数标定即可大幅降低畸变影响。

    Negative segment tuning avoids net-zero overcompensation

    通过系统调节负脉冲片段的幅度和时长，可绕过严格 net-zero 设计固有的系统性过补偿，同时保留畸变抵消收益。原文为：*"By systematically tuning the amplitude and duration of negative pulse segments, we bypassed the systematic overcompensation penalties inherent to strict net-zero designs while retaining their robust distortion-canceling benefits."*

    High-fidelity gate sets are validated in simulation and hardware

    高保真单量子比特门集通过 Boulder Opal 仿真和 Intel Tunnel Falls 硬件直接实现验证。原文为：*"This approach yields high-fidelity single-qubit gate sets validated via both Boulder Opal simulations and direct hardware implementation on Intel’s Tunnel Falls processor."* 这提供了从模型到工业器件的闭环证据链。

    Benchmarking maps the tradeoff among duration, tuning parameters, and fidelity

    系统 benchmark 映射了门时长、所需调参量和实际保真度之间的可行权衡。原文为：*"With a systematic benchmarking of these gate sets, we mapped out the possible trade-offs between pulse duration, required tuning parameters and achieved gate fidelity."* 表 1 的 8 组设置构成这一权衡图谱的核心实验数据。

    Optimal tradeoff is governed by hyperfine noise and charge noise

    最优点由两类噪声竞争决定：更长脉冲受hyperfine noise影响更强，更短更高幅度脉冲因交换指数电压依赖放大charge noise。原文为：*"The optimal tradeoff is dictated by the interplay between hyperfine noise, which degrades performance at longer pulse durations, and charge noise, which is amplified at higher and therefore shorter pulse durations."*

    Pre-distortion plus quasi-zero offers near-full correction with fewer parameters

    quasi-zero 与预失真结合后可达到接近全校正脉冲集的保真度，但调参量显著减少。原文为：*"These combinations offer similar fidelities to the fully corrected pulse sets but with much fewer tunable parameters."* 实验量化为 #7–8 的 99.95%、2 个参数，对比 #2 的 99.96%、12 个参数。

    Quasi-zero pulses can accelerate spin-qubit tune-up

    quasi-zero 被定位为缓解电荷积累的简单鲁棒方案，可相较全预失真调谐加速自旋量子比特 tune-up。原文为：*"The proposed quasi-zero pulses therefore offer a simple and robust solution to mitigate charge accumulation that can accelerate the tune up process for spin qubits compared to a fully tuned pre-distortions approach."*

    Negative pulse charge configurations require further study

    未来性能提升需要详细分析负电压脉冲值下的电荷构型，包括量子点形变、位移及其对其他量子点对杂散耦合的影响。原文为：*"Further improvements of the presented gate-set performance could be based on a detailed analysis of the charge configuration at negative pulse values."* 具体方向为：*"This could include an investigation of the introduced deformation and displacement of the quantum dots and the influence on spurious coupling between other quantum dot pairs."*

    Crosstalk and noise susceptibility remain open issues

    杂散串扰及其对电荷噪声、超精细噪声敏感性的影响需要进一步分析。原文为：*"We suggest an analysis of spurious crosstalk and how this affects the susceptibility to charge and hyperfine noise."* 这也是从单量子比特扩展到多量子比特阵列时必须解决的问题。

    Extension to two-qubit gates is a natural next step

    工作可扩展到双量子比特门。原文为：*"The work can then be extended to two-qubit gates."* 由于交换相互作用也是多数自旋体系双量子比特门的核心，quasi-zero 对两比特门的影响可能更关键。

    Hardware setup comparisons can separate reflection, capacitance, and charge accumulation

    比较不同脉冲发生器和低温系统有助于区分信号反射、导体电容和电荷积累对畸变的贡献。原文为：*"A comparison of pulse generators and fridge setups would provide insights regarding how strong, unwanted signal reflections and the conductor capacitance affect the pulse distortions compared to charge accumulation."*

    Cryo-electronics may make quasi-zero pulses especially valuable

    低温电子学中更短传输线应减少脉冲畸变，但相比室温任意波形发生器，其滤波能力可能严重受限，因此 quasi-zero 更有吸引力。原文为：*"Especially interesting is the comparison to cryo-electronics, where shorter transmission lines should lead to fewer pulse distortions while also the filtering capabilities will be severely restricted compared to an arbitrary waveform generator at room temperature making quasi-zero pulses even more attractive to mediate charge accumulation."*

    Large-scale automated calibration is the central application

    控制脉冲简化为大规模商业量子处理器的自动化交换校准铺路。原文为：*"The control-pulse simplifications demonstrated here pave the way for easily automated, large-scale calibration of exchange interactions in commercial quantum processors."* 这与摘要中的低参数优势一致。

    Transferability extends beyond exchange-only qubits

    结论预期可迁移到其他依赖交换驱动的量子比特类型，包括 singlet-triplet qubit 的单量子比特门和 Loss-DiVincenzo qubit 的双量子比特门。原文为：*"We expect our findings to be transferable to other qubit types that rely on driving the exchange interaction to realize single qubit gates for the singlet-triplet qubit or two qubit gates for the Loss-DiVincenzo qubit."*

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持 (Understanding & Nuance)

    1. 术语解析

    #### Quasi-zero pulses

    quasi-zero 字面是“准零”，但语境中不是“接近无脉冲”，而是时间积分接近但不等于零的控制脉冲。严格 net-zero 要求正负面积完全抵消；quasi-zero 保留净正面积，使主交换旋转仍可有效执行，同时用较小负片段抵消低频畸变。关键微妙点在于：它不是弱化版 net-zero，而是针对真实动态响应中过补偿问题的重新最优化。

    #### Net-positive but reduced time integrals

    该表达指脉冲的电压-时间面积仍为正，但相比普通全正矩形脉冲显著减少。net-positive 保证仍有有效交换驱动；reduced 保证低频残留、电荷积累、RC 尾迹等效应被压低。它避免了“完全零面积”在顺序非对称系统中造成的反向过补偿。

    #### Linear-dynamical distortions

    该术语指输出波形可视为输入波形经过线性时不变或近似线性动态系统后的结果，例如指数响应尾迹、RC 滤波、bias-tee 高通/低通效应。重点不是“误差幅度小”，而是“畸变可由传递函数或阶跃响应描述”。在这种假设下，卷积补偿和 net-zero 面积抵消才有理论基础。

    #### Blind randomized benchmarking

    randomized benchmarking 用随机 Clifford 序列估计平均门错误率；blind 强调实验评价不依赖操作者对具体优化条件或序列结果的主观调节，降低人为调参偏差。该方法输出的是门集层面的操作保真度，而不是单个脉冲的理想仿真保真度。

    #### Bleed-through effects

    bleed-through 指一个脉冲片段的残余响应“渗漏”到后续片段或后续原子脉冲中。短时间常数畸变尤其容易造成这种效应。spacer 的作用不是执行量子门，而是给残余响应衰减留出时间，降低片段间污染。

    ---

    2. 疑难查证

    #### 为什么严格 net-zero 反而会过补偿？

    直觉上，正负面积完全相等应当最能抵消低频畸变；但真实脉冲不是静态面积问题，而是带时间顺序的动态响应问题。正片段总是先到，负片段后到。系统的指数响应具有记忆，后到的负片段不是简单抵消先前正片段的“同时镜像”，而是在不同状态和不同响应阶段叠加。因此零积分可能在观测时间窗口内产生过度负向残留，使 Rabi fringe 曲率反向。quasi-zero 通过降低负幅度，把“面积完全抵消”改成“动态曲率最小化”。

    #### 为什么负电压片段不会执行反向旋转？

    交换相互作用近似满足 (J(v)propto ev/v₀)。正电压会指数增强交换，负电压会指数压低交换。交换耦合通常为正且不会简单变成等幅负耦合，因此负电压片段主要让系统接近 idle，而不是实施反向交换门。负片段的主要功能是电路/电荷层面的畸变抵消，而非量子态层面的反向演化。

    #### 为什么更长脉冲不一定更好？

    延长脉冲可降低所需驱动幅度，从而减少电荷噪声放大；但更长的门暴露在磁噪声和超精细噪声下的时间更久，泄漏和退相干风险增加。相反，缩短脉冲需要更高电压，交换指数响应使电荷噪声敏感性增强。最优门时长位于这两种误差源之间，而不是单调偏向更快或更慢。

    #### 为什么 quasi-zero 仍可与长时间尺度滤波互补？

    quasi-zero 主要通过脉冲面积和局部结构降低畸变，对短时间和中等时间尺度尤其有效；但微秒量级记忆效应可能跨越多个门，单个原子脉冲的局部设计无法完全消除。长时间尺度预失真用少量参数补偿慢尾迹，因此与 quasi-zero 组合能以 2 个参数达到 99.95%，接近 12 参数全滤波的 99.96%。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联 (Synthesis & Novelty)

    1. 创新性判断

    #### 从 strict net-zero 到 optimized quasi-zero

    过去 2–5 年内，相关工作主要集中在两类路径：一类是超导量子比特中的 net-zero 或快速条件相位门设计；另一类是自旋量子比特中的控制脉冲预失真、滤波和传递函数校准。该研究的新颖性在于明确指出：严格 net-zero 在 exchange-only spin qubit 的实际动态响应中会过补偿，最优解不是零面积，而是净正但减小的 quasi-zero 面积。

    #### 把低参数鲁棒脉冲用于工业化 exchange-only 平台

    quasi-zero 不是纯理论构型，而是在 Intel Tunnel Falls 六点器件上通过 blind randomized benchmarking 验证。结果显示：

    • 全滤波：99.96%，12 个参数，30 ns；
    • quasi-zero 无滤波：99.93%，0 个滤波参数，30 ns；
    • quasi-zero + 长时滤波：99.95%，2 个参数，40 ns。

    这种“几乎保持保真度、显著减少调参量”的组合，直接解决大规模量子处理器中校准复杂度随器件规模增长的问题。

    #### 用 fringe curvature 作为动态畸变诊断与 γ 优化指标

    通过重复 (N(ψ)) 脉冲并观察 Rabi fringe 中心曲率，动态畸变被转化为可视化、可优化的几何指标。最优 (γ) 通过中心峰值沿直线对齐获得，而非通过完整重建 transfer function。这使 quasi-zero 具备自动化调参潜力。

    #### 明确量化“时长—保真度—参数数目”三方权衡

    相关工作往往只优化保真度或滤波效果；这里把保真度、门时长和调参复杂度放在同一个实验矩阵中比较。核心结论不是“quasi-zero 最高保真”，而是“在接近最高保真的同时显著降低校准维度”。这一点对商业量子处理器比单点保真度提升更具系统价值。

    #### 解决前人未充分解决的问题

    前人预失真方法可以补偿畸变，但需要详细 transfer function 和大量参数；net-zero 方法可以低参数抵消低频畸变，但严格零面积在 exchange-only qubit 中会过补偿。quasi-zero 同时解决两者缺陷：

    • 不需要完整传递函数标定；
    • 避免 strict net-zero 的动态过补偿；
    • 保留短门时长和高保真；
    • 降低自动化校准复杂度；
    • 可与少量长时滤波参数互补。
    阅读原文 ↗
    原文链接页内定位
  16. 16
    合成反铁磁体中斯格明子坍缩成核#
    Skyrmions in Synthetic Antiferromagnets: Collapse and Nucleation#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 物理 / 凝聚态📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 M. N. Potkina🔥 AI 78

    💡 亮点：最小能量路径刻画斯格明子可靠性。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题合成反铁磁体中，已写入的双层束缚 skyrmion 对如何热塌缩、未写入的反铁磁参考态如何反向成核；核心是区分“保持稳定性”和“写入难度”两种能垒，并判断逐层塌缩/逐层写入是否是能量景观本身的特征。
    创新方法用简化双层 SAF 晶格自旋模型结合最小能量路径/爬山图像 NEB，直接追踪 skyrmion 对到均匀反铁磁态的能量山脊；Aha 点是把塌缩能垒分解为“局域主鞍点能量 Eₛₚ”与“受钉扎边界惩罚的 skyrmion 对最低能量 Eₚₐᵢᵣ”，发现尺寸效应主要来自初态能量被边界抬升，而不是鞍点升高。
    工作流程输入双层铁磁晶格、界面 DMI、层内交换、反铁磁 RKKY 层间耦合、外磁场和下层 bias field；固定岛边界为反铁磁态，分别弛豫 skyrmion 对、单层 skyrmion 和均匀 AFM 态；用 MEP/NEB 连接 skyrmion 对与 AFM 态，定位主鞍点、低鞍点和可能的上层单 skyrmion 中间态；计算塌缩能垒 ΔE_coll=Eₛₚ−Eₚₐᵢᵣ 与反向成核能垒 ΔEₙᵤcl=Eₛₚ−E_AFM；输出尺寸 S、磁场 B 下的能量路径、稳定区域图和逐层塌缩/成核机制。
    关键结果主鞍点能量几乎锁定在 23–24 J，随岛尺寸 S=100 到 500 变化很弱；skyrmion 对最低能量随尺寸显著降低，使塌缩能垒从 S=100 的近零值升至 S=500 的约 4.7–6.0 J。塌缩通常不是双层同步消失，而是下层 skyrmion 先塌缩，经过上层单 skyrmion 中间态，再由第二个较低鞍点完成塌缩。反向成核能垒约 23–24 J，远高于塌缩能垒；若先辅助产生单层 seed，完成双层 skyrmion 对的能垒约 11 J，但 seed 自身衰减能垒仅 0.022–0.282 J。
    应用价值说明 SAF skyrmion 存储位具有“易保持受限、难自发写入”的能量非对称性：直接热成核 skyrmion 对极低效，器件应采用电流、激光、电压或局域注入先制造单层 skyrmion seed，再利用层间反铁磁耦合完成逐层写入；同时提示增大有效岛尺寸或减弱边界惩罚可提高已写入态的热稳定性。

    第一部分：核心概览（Overview）

    该研究以简化双层 SAF 晶格模型和最小能量路径（MEP）计算，系统刻画了合成反铁磁体中束缚 skyrmion 对的热塌缩与反向成核能垒。核心贡献在于揭示：钉扎边界下主鞍点能量随岛尺寸变化很弱，而 skyrmion 对最低能量强烈受边界惩罚控制；塌缩常呈逐层顺序机制；反向成核能垒远高于塌缩能垒，支持辅助式逐层写入而非自发热成核。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Skyrmions in Synthetic Antiferromagnets: Collapse and Nucleation》（None，）

    背景

    合成反铁磁体（SAFs）中的 skyrmion 兼具低 stray field、弱 skyrmion Hall 效应和层分辨可探测性，适合高密度存储。但存储可行性取决于两个问题：已写入 skyrmion 对能否长期保持，以及未写入反铁磁参考态能否高效写入 skyrmion 对。

    方法

    采用双层 ferromagnetic lattice spin model，包含层内交换、界面 DMI、反铁磁 RKKY 层间耦合、外磁场 Zeeman 项、固定 bias field。通过 constrained MEP / climbing-image NEB 计算从 skyrmion 对到均匀反铁磁态的塌缩路径，并反向解释成核路径。

    结果

    主鞍点能量约稳定在 23–24 J，而 skyrmion 对能量随尺寸从 S=100 到 S=500 显著降低；塌缩能垒从几乎为零增长至约 6 J。大尺寸岛中塌缩通常先发生在下层，随后经过上层单 skyrmion 中间态，再完成最终塌缩。

    讨论

    塌缩能垒的尺寸依赖主要来自钉扎边界对 skyrmion 对最低能量的抬升，而非鞍点显著移动。反向成核能垒约 23–24 J，远高于已写入态塌缩能垒，说明热自发写入极低效。

    局限

    模型未显式包含垂直各向异性、长程偶极/退磁场、Hessian 谱、动力学和熵前因子，且未搜索 edge-assisted annihilation、edge escape、random/spiral 路径。因此数值寿命和真实器件能垒不能直接一一对应。

    结论

    SAF skyrmion 对的保持与写入具有显著非对称性：保持受较低 interior-collapse barrier 限制，写入需克服高得多的 reverse barrier。最合理的器件策略是先辅助产生或注入单层 skyrmion，再由层间交换完成 skyrmion 对写入。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析（Section-by-Section Condensing）

    Abstract

    • Reliability problem for SAF skyrmion bits

    合成反铁磁 skyrmion 对被定位为 nanoscale bits，但可用性不只取决于能否存在，还取决于写入后能否可靠存活、能否可控创建。摘要直接界定问题：*"Magnetic skyrmions in synthetic antiferromagnets are promising nanoscale bits, but their usefulness depends on how reliably a written pair survives and can be created."* 这里将retention与writability并列为核心物理问题。

    • Reduced lattice model and MEP strategy

    计算对象是反铁磁束缚 skyrmion 对的塌缩路径与从钉扎反铁磁参考态反向成核路径，方法是 reduced lattice model + minimum energy paths：*"Using a reduced lattice model, we compute minimum energy paths for collapse of an antiferromagnetically bound skyrmion pair and for reverse nucleation from a pinned antiferromagnetic reference state."*

    • Boundary-size asymmetry between saddle and skyrmion-pair minimum

    钉扎边界下，主鞍点能量对 pinned-island size 不敏感，但 skyrmion-pair minimum 带有强烈尺寸依赖边界惩罚：*"With antiferromagnetically pinned boundaries, the main saddle energy changes only weakly with pinned-island size, whereas the skyrmion-pair minimum carries a strong size-dependent boundary penalty."* 这预示塌缩能垒的尺寸效应主要不是鞍点变高，而是初态能量被边界抬升或降低。

    • Layer-sequential collapse and single-layer intermediate

    大尺寸 pinned islands 中塌缩常不是两层同时发生，而是逐层完成，并可经过单层 skyrmion 中间态：*"For large pinned islands, collapse is layer-sequential and can pass through a single-layer skyrmion intermediate whenever this state satisfies the relaxation criterion."*

    • Strong collapse–nucleation asymmetry

    反向成核能垒远高于塌缩能垒，形成明显非对称性，并指向 assisted layer-sequential writing：*"The much larger reverse barrier for nucleation shows a strong asymmetry with collapse in the same pinned-boundary model and is consistent with assisted layer-sequential writing."*

    ---

    1 Introduction

    • Skyrmions as racetrack information carriers

    磁 skyrmion是局域手性自旋纹理，可被自旋极化电流驱动，因此被视为 racetrack memory 和 logic devices 的信息载体：*"Magnetic skyrmions are localized chiral spin textures that can be moved by spin-polarized currents and are therefore considered as information carriers for racetrack-type memory and logic devices."*

    • Miniaturization creates density–stability tension

    高密度存储需要小尺寸 skyrmion，但纳米尺度 skyrmion 在 ultrathin ferromagnetic films 中塌缩激活能垒可能较低；大尺寸 dipolar-stabilized skyrmion 又不利于高密度，因为 stray fields 增大尺寸并引发长程相互作用：*"miniaturization creates a direct tension between bit density and thermal stability"*；*"Nanometer-scale skyrmions in ultrathin ferromagnetic films can have low activation barriers against collapse"*；*"stray fields increase their size and mediate unwanted long-range interactions between neighboring bits."*

    • Compensated systems reduce dipolar and Hall-effect problems

    反铁磁与补偿 ferrimagnet能降低净磁矩、dipolar fields，并因 gyrotropic response 抵消而抑制 skyrmion Hall effect：*"In compensated materials the net magnetization and dipolar fields are small, and the cancellation of the gyrotropic response suppresses the skyrmion Hall effect."* 这使 compensated systems 对高密度、低串扰器件有天然优势。

    • SAFs solve detectability and controllability problems of intrinsic antiferromagnets

    本征 antiferromagnets 中单个拓扑纹理难以检测和操控，SAFs 通过两层 ferromagnetic layers + nonmagnetic spacer + antiferromagnetic RKKY coupling 提供可调、可探测平台：*"A practical difficulty in intrinsic antiferromagnets is detecting and controllably manipulating individual topological textures."*；*"two ferromagnetic layers are separated by a nonmagnetic spacer that mediates antiferromagnetic Ruderman–Kittel–Kasuya–Yosida (RKKY) coupling."*

    • SAF skyrmion platform already has experimental support

    相关实验已实现 room-temperature SAF skyrmion bubbles、约十纳米 antiferromagnetically coupled skyrmions、zero-field skyrmions、局域成核、快速电流驱动运动。关键证据包括：*"room-temperature formation and current-induced motion of synthetic antiferromagnetic skyrmion bubbles with negligible skyrmion Hall deflection"*；*"room-temperature stabilization of antiferromagnetically coupled skyrmions of about ten nanometers in Pt/Co/Ru-based SAFs"*；*"current-induced motion in compensated SAFs with velocities up to hundreds of meters per second."*

    • Writing is harder than motion control

    skyrmion 器件中，运动控制已有多个方案，但写入更具挑战：*"The writing problem is more challenging than controlling motion."* 现有 assisted writing 包括 local current injection、ultrafast laser excitation、voltage-controlled magnetic anisotropy、thermal assistance、defect/notch 降低成核能垒、hybrid ferromagnet/SAF sequential transfer。

    • Central question: dynamical convenience or energy-landscape feature

    核心科学问题不是“逐层写入能不能动态实现”，而是“逐层路线是否本身就是 pinned SAF island 的能量景观特征”：*"The question here is whether a layer-by-layer route is only a convenient dynamical protocol, or also a feature of the energy landscape of a pinned SAF island."*

    • MEP and HTST frame rare thermal transitions

    热稳定性由 local minima 间的 rare transitions 决定，MEP 与 harmonic transition state theory 可定位 saddle points 与 activation barriers：*"The thermal stability of skyrmions is determined by rare transitions between local minima of the magnetic energy."*；*"Minimum energy path (MEP) calculations and harmonic transition state theory (HTST) provide a microscopic way to find the relevant saddle points and activation barriers."*

    • Previous SAF work established non-simultaneous collapse but not pinned-island trends

    前人已发现 interlayer exchange 可改变 collapse barrier 与 collapse mechanism，并导致非同步逐层塌缩：*"previous calculations have shown that interlayer exchange can change both the collapse barrier and the collapse mechanism"*；*"interlayer coupling can produce non-simultaneous, layer-resolved collapse."* 新增内容集中在 pinned islands、尺寸依赖分解、collapse–reverse nucleation 联系、single-skyrmion intermediate 稳定图：*"The new elements addressed here are the behavior of this mechanism in pinned islands, the lateral-size dependence of the interior-collapse barrier separated into saddle and pair-minimum contributions, the connection between collapse and the reverse layer-sequential nucleation path on the same MEP, and the stability map of the independently relaxed upper-layer single-skyrmion intermediate."*

    • Retention and writability are distinct questions

    skyrmion memory bit 需要区分两个问题：已写入 skyrmion pair 的 barrier-limited retention，以及从 unwritten reference state 创建 pair 的 writability。原文明确分离：*"The first is barrier-limited retention: what collapse barrier protects an already written skyrmion pair against thermally activated decay?"*；*"The second is writability: if the pinned collinear antiferromagnetic state is the unwritten reference state, what route can create the skyrmion pair without relying on exponentially rare spontaneous nucleation?"*

    • Reduced model parameterized from Legrand-type SAF stack

    计算采用 reduced lattice model，保留与 collapse path 直接相关的相互作用，并从 Legrand-type SAF stack 的长度和能量尺度参数化：*"Here we calculate MEPs for collapse and nucleation of bound skyrmion pairs in pinned SAF islands using a reduced lattice model parameterized, for the retained interaction terms, from the length and energy scales of the Legrand-type SAF stack."*

    • Physical stack motivation and bias-field origin

    实验参数来源包含 Co/Pt、RKKY spacer、DMI 以及额外 [Pt(0.45 nm)/Co(0.6 nm)]₄ bias layers。关键结构描述为：*"The experimental stack used for this parameterization consists of two magnetic layers separated by a nonmagnetic metal layer."*；*"The magnetic layers are Co films interfaced with the heavy metal Pt, which induces Dzyaloshinskii–Moriya antisymmetric exchange"*；*"additional [Pt(0.45 nm)/Co(0.6 nm)]4 magnetic layers with strong perpendicular uniaxial anisotropy were introduced into the system."*

    • Model deliberately omits anisotropy, magnetostatics, prefactors

    模型是 energy-landscape model，不是完整 micromagnetic description；不显式包含 perpendicular anisotropy、magnetostatic/dipolar fields、dynamical prefactors：*"It is a reduced energy-landscape model rather than a full micromagnetic description of the experimental multilayer: perpendicular anisotropy, magnetostatic/dipolar fields, and dynamical prefactors are not included explicitly."* 因此只能识别 retained interactions 内的机制与趋势。

    • Pinned island interpreted as interior-collapse estimator

    pinned island 的作用不是模拟自由边界器件，而是估计无限或足够大 collinear SAF 区域中的 interior collapse saddle：*"the pinned island has a limited role: it lets us estimate the saddle point for an interior collapse event in an infinite or sufficiently large collinear SAF region, provided the saddle is localized away from the artificial boundary."*

    • Barrier definition combines localized saddle and boundary-dependent pair minimum

    计算 barrier 是 pinned-boundary MEP-channel barrier，其中 Eₛₚ 是局域 interior saddle 估计，Eₚₐᵢᵣ 带有 boundary penalty：*"The reported barriers combine a localized interior-saddle estimate with a boundary-dependent estimate of the skyrmion-pair minimum."*；*"“barrier” below means the calculated pinned-boundary MEP-channel barrier unless explicitly stated otherwise."*

    • Three main conclusions already declared

    第一，主鞍点能量随 pinned-island size 弱变，pair minimum 强变；第二，塌缩非同步，下层先塌缩并可能经过上层单 skyrmion；第三，反向成核能垒远大于塌缩能垒，支持逐层辅助写入。原文概括为：*"Within this reduced model, the MEPs lead to three main conclusions."*；*"the calculated interior saddle energy varies only weakly with pinned-island size, while the energy of the skyrmion-pair minimum changes strongly."*；*"the collapse is generally not simultaneous in the two SAF layers."*；*"the reverse nucleation barrier from the pinned collinear antiferromagnetic reference state is much larger than the collapse barrier of an already written pair."*

    ---

    2 Model and method

    • Two-layer SAF lattice spin model

    系统由两个 ferromagnetic layers 表示，每个晶格点携带单位自旋向量 Sᵢ⁽l)，层标号 l=1,2：*"We use a lattice spin model representing two ferromagnetic layers of an SAF separated by a nonmagnetic spacer."*；*"Each lattice site carries a unit vector Sᵢ⁽l), where l=1,2 labels the two magnetic layers."*

    • Interaction terms retained in Hamiltonian

    Hamiltonian 保留层内 ferromagnetic exchange、DMI、反铁磁 RKKY interlayer exchange、applied field、lower-layer fixed bias field：*"The intralayer interactions include ferromagnetic exchange and Dzyaloshinskii–Moriya interaction (DMI)."*；*"The two layers are coupled antiferromagnetically through an RKKY-type interlayer exchange."*；*"a third, uniformly magnetized bias layer is not treated dynamically; its effect is included as a fixed effective bias field acting on the lower SAF layer."*

    • Hamiltonian structure and layer asymmetry

    能量式包含

    [

    E= -sumₗ₌₁²sumłₐₙgₗₑ ᵢ,ⱼåₙgₗₑ[Jmathbf Sᵢ⁽l⁾ḑotmathbf Sⱼ⁽l⁾+mathbf Dᵢⱼḑot(mathbf Sᵢ⁽l⁾×mathbf Sⱼ⁽l⁾)]

    -J₁₂sumᵢmathbf Sᵢ⁽¹⁾ḑotmathbf Sᵢ⁽²⁾

    -μsumᵢ[(mathbf B_b+mathbf B)ḑotmathbf Sᵢ⁽¹⁾+mathbf Bḑotmathbf Sᵢ⁽²⁾].

    ]

    层 1 受 B_b+B，层 2 只受 B：*"the net field entering the Zeeman term is B_b+B in layer 1 and B in layer 2."*

    • DMI convention fixes chirality

    DMI 向量为 Dᵢⱼ = D(eᵢⱼ × e_z), D>0；+x 与 +y 方向键分别为 (0,−D,0) 与 (D,0,0)：*"For a nearest-neighbor bond directed from site i to site j ... the interfacial DMI vector is Dᵢⱼ₌D(eᵢⱼ×e_z), D>0."*；*"bonds along +eₓ and +e_y have Dᵢⱼ₌₍₀,-D,0) and (D,0,0), respectively."*

    • Omitted physical terms constrain interpretation

    模型不含单独 perpendicular anisotropy 和 long-range dipole-dipole interaction：*"The omitted terms include a separate perpendicular anisotropy ... and the long-range dipole-dipole interaction."* 因而稳定窗口、半径、路径、能垒、寿命均是 model-level quantities：*"the absolute stability windows, skyrmion radii, collapse paths, activation barriers, and lifetimes are model-level quantities rather than one-to-one predictions for the full multilayer."*

    • Discrete–micromagnetic mapping controlled by dimensionless ratios

    参数映射使用

    J=2d𝒜，|Dᵢⱼ|/J=a𝒟/(2𝒜)，|J₁₂|/J=a²𝒥_RKKY/(2d𝒜)，μB_b/J=a²MₛB_b/(2𝒜)。原文强调：*"The mapping from discrete parameters to micromagnetic ones is controlled by dimensionless ratios."* RKKY ratio 随厚度 1/d 缩放：*"Because the RKKY coupling is interfacial, its ratio to J scales as 1/d."*

    • Numerical parameters from Legrand-type stack

    采用 a=0.2505 nm, d=1.47 nm, 𝒜=10×10⁻¹² J/m, 𝒟=0.5×10⁻³ J/m², 𝒥_RKKY=0.23×10⁻³ J m⁻², Mₛ₌₁.2×10⁶ A/m, B_b=50 mT。对应离散参数为 J=183.5 meV, D/J=6.3×10⁻³, |J₁₂|/J=5×10⁻⁴, μ=12 μ_B：*"which gives the following set of discrete-model parameters: J=183.5 meV, D/J=6.3·10−3, |J12|/J=5·10−4, μ=12μB."*

    • Pinned-island sizes and fields

    MEP 使用 S=100, 300, 500，外场 B=−25, 0, 10, 20, 30 mT；因 a=0.2505 nm，对应 lateral lengths 约 25, 75, 125 nm：*"The MEP barrier calculations use S=100, 300, and 500, with applied fields B=-25,0,10,20,30 mT."*；*"these three sizes correspond to lateral lengths of approximately 25, 75, and 125 nm."*

    • Single-layer intermediate stability grid

    上层单 skyrmion 稳定图额外使用 S=100,200,300,400,500 与 B=−20,−10,0,10,20,30 mT：*"The stability diagram of the upper-layer intermediate ... is obtained from an additional grid of independent relaxations with S=100,200,300,400,500 and B=-20,-10,0,10,20,30 mT."*

    • Antiferromagnetically pinned boundary condition

    最外层晶格轮廓固定为反铁磁态，内部自旋自由弛豫：*"The boundary spins are pinned in the antiferromagnetic state and kept fixed throughout the calculation."*；*"The pinned sites form the outermost lattice contour of the island; all interior spins are free to relax."* 该条件聚焦 interior collapse，排除 open-edge deformation、skyrmion escape、edge-assisted annihilation：*"open-edge deformation, skyrmion escape, and edge-assisted annihilation paths are outside this boundary-value problem."*

    • Pinned boundary raises skyrmion-pair energy

    固定边界限制纹理弛豫，使 skyrmion-pair energy 成为允许边界弛豫时的 upper-bound estimate：*"Since pinning restricts the variational space, the relaxed skyrmion-pair energy obtained in this way is an upper-bound estimate for the corresponding pair state when boundary relaxation is allowed."* 因此 ΔE_coll=Eₛₚ−Eₚₐᵢᵣ 倾向于低估 interior-channel barrier：*"Because Eₚₐᵢᵣ is raised by the boundary constraint, ΔE_coll=Eₛₚ−Eₚₐᵢᵣ tends to underestimate the interior-channel barrier."*

    • Endpoint and intermediate relaxations use stringent gradient tolerance

    均匀 AFM 态、skyrmion 对、上层单 skyrmion 初态分别用 nonlinear conjugate gradient 弛豫，最大 tangent-space energy gradient 小于 10⁻⁹ J：*"These single-configuration relaxations are performed by nonlinear conjugate gradient minimization on the fixed-length spin manifold until the maximum tangent-space energy gradient is below 10−9 in units of the exchange energy J."*

    • Field orientation selects lower-layer-first collapse

    对给定场方向，优化路径首先失去下层 skyrmion，因此中间态若存在，是上层 skyrmion；下层单 skyrmion 不构成报告 MEP 上的独立中间态：*"For the field orientation used here, the optimized collapse paths first lose the lower-layer skyrmion (l=1), so the stationary intermediate, when it exists, is the upper-layer skyrmion."*；*"The lower-layer-only configuration is not a separate intermediate on the reported MEPs."*

    • MEP algorithm: constrained fixed-length spin path

    MEP 连接 skyrmion pair 与 homogeneous state，路径由 unit spheres product 上的 spin configurations/images 表示，端点固定：*"MEPs connecting the skyrmion pair and the homogeneous state are obtained with a constrained MEP algorithm for fixed-length magnetic moments."*；*"The path is represented by a sequence of spin configurations, or images, on the product of unit spheres."*

    • Image counts scale with island size

    最终优化链包含：S=100：20 images；S=300：23–37 images；S=500：27–37 images，均包括两个固定端点：*"The final optimized chains used in the figures contain 20, 23–37, and 27–37 images for S=100, 300, and 500, respectively, including the two fixed endpoint images."*

    • Climbing and descending image treatment

    能量极大处 images 作为 climbing images，切向分量反转以收敛到 saddle point；能量极小处 images 作为 descending images：*"Images at energy maxima are treated as climbing images; for these images the tangential component is reversed so that the image converges to the saddle point on the MEP."*；*"Images at energy minima along the path are treated as descending images."*

    • Path distance is configuration-space Euclidean distance

    两个 images 的距离定义为 embedding spin-vector space 中所有自由自旋差的平方和开方，固定边界不贡献：*"The distance between two images ... is the Euclidean distance in the embedding spin-vector space"*；*"fixed boundary spins make no contribution because they are identical in all images."*

    • Convergence and saddle validation

    最终 endpoint、saddle、intermediate minima 的最大 tangent-space gradient 均低于 10⁻⁹ J；saddle energies 与 single-layer minimum 存在性对 image 数和迭代数收敛：*"For the stationary configurations used as endpoints, saddle points, and intermediate minima, the maximum tangent-space energy gradient after the final relaxation is below 10−9 in units of the exchange energy J."*；*"The number of images and relaxation iterations were increased until the saddle energies and the presence or absence of the single-layer minimum no longer changed."*

    • Single-skyrmion intermediate acceptance criterion

    上层单 skyrmion 被认为 locally stable 需同时满足：path image 是 strict discrete minimum、独立 CG 弛豫至 gradient < 10⁻⁹ J、与相邻 saddle 分离；最终接受中间态相对相邻 images 最小能量降低 8×10⁻⁴ J，低于 5×10⁻⁴ J 的浅特征视为数值路径分辨率：*"The upper-layer single-skyrmion state is counted as locally stable only when the corresponding path image is a strict discrete minimum..."*；*"the smallest energy decrease relative to the neighboring images is 8×10−4J; shallower features below 5×10−4J are treated as numerical path resolution."*

    • No Hessian spectra and no HTST prefactors

    稳定性分类基于 nonlinear relaxation 与 discrete MEP structure，而非 positive-definite Hessian test；HTST prefactors 不计算：*"No Hessian spectra were evaluated in the present work."*；*"the stability classification is based on nonlinear relaxation and discrete MEP structure rather than on a positive-definite Hessian test."*；*"quantitative HTST prefactors are outside the scope of the calculation."*

    • Collapse and nucleation barriers defined on same MEP

    塌缩能垒为

    [

    Δ Ecₒₗₗ=maxₚₐₜₕE-Eₚₐᵢᵣ,

    ]

    反向成核能垒为

    [

    Δ Eₙᵤcₗ=maxₚₐₜₕE-EAFM.

    ]

    原文定义：*"The collapse barrier of an already written skyrmion pair is ΔEcoll=maxpathE−Epair."*；*"The reverse barrier from the pinned collinear antiferromagnetic reference state is ΔEnucl=maxpathE−EAFM."*

    • Static equilibrium reverse path is not assisted writing dynamics

    collapse/nucleation 指静态能量景观上的热激活转变，无 nonconservative driving force；current、voltage、laser、geometry-assisted writing 不必沿反向静态 MEP：*"the terms “collapse” and “nucleation” refer to thermally activated transitions on the static energy landscape ... with no nonconservative driving force."*；*"Current-, voltage-, laser-, or geometry-assisted writing is a nonequilibrium process and need not follow the reverse static MEP."*

    • Only one interior channel explored

    优化 MEP 定义一个 pinned-boundary interior collapse/nucleation channel，未搜索 random、spiral、edge-twisted、edge-escape 等竞争低能垒路径：*"The optimized MEPs reported below define one interior collapse/nucleation channel for this boundary-value problem; random, spiral, edge-twisted, and edge-escape routes were not searched for competing lower barriers."*

    ---

    3 Results

    3.1 Layer-by-layer collapse mechanism

    • Representative case: B=30 mT, S=500

    代表性 MEP 使用 B=30 mT, S=500，显示 skyrmion-pair collapse 的逐层过程：*"Figure 1 shows representative configurations along the MEP for B=30 mT and S=500."*

    • Initial pair has opposite core magnetizations

    初态是两层 core magnetization 相反的 bound skyrmion pair：*"The initial state is a bound skyrmion pair with opposite core magnetizations in the two layers."* 这对应 SAF 中两层反铁磁耦合纹理。

    • Layer-dependent fields create different skyrmion sizes

    下层受 B_b+B=80 mT，且方向与 skyrmion core magnetization 相反；上层只受 B=30 mT，且与中心磁化方向平行，因此两层 skyrmion 尺寸不同：*"the lower layer is subject to a net field of magnitude Bb+B=80 mT, opposite to the direction of magnetization at the skyrmion core, while the upper layer is subject only to the applied field of magnitude B=30 mT, parallel to the magnetization at the center."*

    • Applied field has opposite size effects in two layers

    增大 applied field 会减小下层 skyrmion 尺寸、增大上层 skyrmion 尺寸；当 B=−B_b/2 时两层半径相同：*"Increasing the applied field decreases the skyrmion size in the lower layer but increases it in the upper layer."*；*"When the applied field is set to B=−Bb/2, the skyrmion radius in both layers is the same."*

    • Collapse is sequential, not simultaneous

    下层 skyrmion 先经高鞍点塌缩，上层仍局域；随后路径弛豫到上层单 skyrmion local minimum；第二个低鞍点对应剩余上层 skyrmion 的塌缩：*"The collapse is not simultaneous."*；*"First, the skyrmion in the lower layer collapses through the higher saddle point, while the skyrmion in the upper layer remains localized."*；*"The second, lower saddle point corresponds to the collapse of this remaining skyrmion."*

    • Topological charge changes layer by layer

    初始 SAF pair 每层各有一个 skyrmion charge，符号相反；第一鞍点下层 charge 变为零，上层仍非零；第二鞍点上层 charge 也消失，最终两层为零拓扑电荷：*"Equivalently, the layer-resolved topological charge changes sequentially."*；*"At the first saddle the lower-layer charge changes to zero, while the upper-layer charge remains nonzero."*；*"the final pinned collinear state has zero topological charge in both layers."*

    • MEP profile consistently shows pair → main saddle → single-layer segment → lower saddle → AFM

    全部 MEP 都呈现同一能量轮廓：从相对 pinned collinear reference 为正能量的 skyrmion-pair minimum 出发，爬升到 main saddle，下降到 upper-layer skyrmion 能量范围，再跨过 lower saddle，最终到 homogeneous state：*"The same structure is seen in the full set of MEPs in Fig. 2."*；*"It then climbs to the main saddle point, drops to the energy range of the upper-layer skyrmion, crosses a lower saddle point, and finally reaches the homogeneous state."*

    • MEP horizontal coordinate is not real-space coordinate

    横轴是 full spin configuration space 的 accumulated Euclidean distance，大岛更大，不可解释为实空间位置：*"The position along the horizontal axis is the accumulated Euclidean distance in the full spin configuration space; it is therefore larger for larger pinned islands and should not be interpreted as a real-space coordinate."*

    • Reverse path nucleates upper layer first

    反向过程沿同一 MEP 反向运行：从 pinned collinear state 出发，先成核 upper-layer skyrmion，再成核 lower-layer partner；若单层态是 local minimum，则是真正中间态：*"The reverse process follows the same MEP in the opposite direction."*；*"Starting from the pinned collinear reference state, the upper-layer skyrmion is nucleated first, and only then is the lower-layer partner nucleated."*；*"When this single-layer state is a local minimum, it is a genuine intermediate on the path."*

    ---

    3.2 Interior collapse barrier and role of confinement

    • Energy branches separated: pair minimum and main saddle

    Figure 3 比较 skyrmion-pair minimum E₀、main saddle Eₛₚ 和 resulting collapse barriers：*"Figure 3 shows the energy of the skyrmion-pair minimum E0 and the energy of the main saddle point Esp, together with the resulting collapse barriers for this MEP channel."*

    • Skyrmion pair is metastable but above AFM reference

    所有显示参数下 skyrmion pair 是 local minimum，但能量高于 pinned collinear reference state：*"The skyrmion pair is a local minimum in all cases shown, although its energy lies above the pinned collinear reference state."*

    • Main saddle energy weakly depends on size

    主鞍点能量随 S 变化较弱，并保持在 23–24 J 附近窄区间：*"The main saddle energy varies comparatively weakly with S and remains in a narrow interval near 23–24J."*

    • Skyrmion-pair energy strongly depends on pinned-island size

    与鞍点不同，skyrmion pair 绝对能量强烈依赖 pinned-island size，并应理解为包含 fixed collinear edge boundary penalty 的 upper-bound estimate：*"the absolute energy of the skyrmion pair depends strongly on pinned-island size and should be read as an upper-bound estimate that includes the boundary penalty imposed by the fixed collinear edge."*

    • S=100: almost no thermal protection

    对 S=100，E₀≈24 J，几乎与 saddle point 简并，塌缩能垒接近零；表 1 中能垒为 0.036 J（B=−25 mT）, 0.028 J（0 mT）, 0.024 J（10 mT）, 0.020 J（20 mT）, 0.017 J（30 mT）。原文总结：*"For S=100, E0 is close to 24J and is nearly degenerate with the saddle point, leading to an almost vanishing collapse barrier."*

    • S=300: barrier around 3.1–3.4 J

    对 S=300，E₀≈20 J，塌缩能垒约 3.1–3.4 J；表 1 可见 B=−25 mT 时 E₀/J=20.508, Eₛₚ,1/J=23.681, ΔE_coll/J=3.173；B=0 mT 时 E₀/J=20.360, Eₛₚ,1/J=23.524, ΔE_coll/J=3.164。原文概括：*"For S=300, E0 lies near 20J and the barrier is about 3.1–3.4J."*

    • S=500: barrier rises to about 4.7–6.0 J

    对 S=500，E₀ 从 B=−25 mT 时约 19 J 降至 B=30 mT 时约 17 J，而 saddle energy 仍约 23 J，因此 barrier 从约 4.7 J 增至 6.0 J：*"For S=500, E0 decreases from about 19J at B=−25 mT to about 17J at B=30 mT, while the saddle energy remains near 23J."*；*"the barrier of this channel increases from about 4.7J to about 6.0J."*

    • Barrier size dependence mainly comes from E₀, not Eₛₚ

    最核心结论是 ΔE_coll=Eₛₚ−E₀ 的尺寸依赖主要由 skyrmion-pair minimum 变化控制，而非 saddle energy 变化：*"the pinned-boundary energy barrier for collapse ΔEcoll=Esp−E0 is controlled mainly by the skyrmion-pair energy rather than by a variation of saddle energy."*

    • Applied field is secondary compared with confinement

    增大 B 通过降低 skyrmion-pair energy 提高 barrier，但在探索区间内，field effect 小于 S=100 到 S=500 的 lateral-size effect：*"Increasing B also raises the barrier by lowering the skyrmion-pair energy, but over the explored interval its effect is moderate compared with the change of lateral size from S=100 to S=500."*

    • Smallest island is a limiting case

    S=100 中 pair 虽可作为局域构型弛豫存在，但 saddle point 能量太接近，几乎无热塌缩保护：*"The smallest pinned island is an important limiting case: the relaxed pair exists as a local configuration, but the saddle point is so close in energy that the pair has essentially no barrier protection against thermal collapse."*

    • Open finite island requires different calculation

    若是开放有限岛，需要重新计算边界弛豫和可能 edge-assisted paths：*"For an open finite island, the corresponding barrier would have to be recalculated with boundary relaxation and possible edge-assisted paths."*

    • Field-induced barrier increase appears only for sufficiently large S

    对 S=100，field-induced barrier increase 几乎不存在；对 S≳300 才明显：*"The field-induced increase of the barrier is almost absent for S=100 and becomes noticeable only for S≳300."* 因而 applied field 是 secondary tuning parameter：*"an applied field acts as a secondary tuning parameter compared with lateral confinement."*

    • Arrhenius interpretation of reduced barriers

    HTST 寿命形式为

    [

    τsimeqτ₀ exp(Δ Ecₒₗₗ/k_BT).

    ]

    原文给出：*"In HTST, the lifetime of a metastable state has the Arrhenius form τ≃τ0 exp(ΔEcoll/kBT)."*

    • Energy-scale conversion: 3J, 5J, 6J

    使用 J=183.5 meV，代表性能垒 3 J, 5 J, 6 J 分别约为 0.55 eV, 0.92 eV, 1.10 eV；在 T=300 K, kBT≈25.9 meV 下分别为 21, 35, 43 kBT：*"Representative reduced barriers of 3J, 5J, and 6J therefore correspond to approximately 0.55, 0.92, and 1.10 eV, or about 21, 35, and 43 in units of kBT at T=300 K."*

    • Absolute lifetime still cannot be inferred directly

    真实寿命还需 Hessian 与 dynamical prefactors、omitted anisotropy/magnetostatics、edge-assisted path 检查：*"an absolute lifetime would also require the Hessian and dynamical prefactors, the omitted anisotropy and magnetostatic contributions, and a check for competing edge-assisted paths."*

    • Retention criterion stated as scale condition

    给定目标保持时间 τᵣₑₜ，形式条件为

    [

    Δ Ecₒₗₗ(S,B)gtrsim k_BTłn(τᵣₑₜ/τ₀₎.

    ]

    原文说明：*"For a given material and operating temperature, this gives the formal Arrhenius scale condition: ΔEcoll(S,B)≳kBT ln(τret/τ0)."*

    ---

    3.3 Reverse barrier and assisted writing

    • Reverse nucleation barrier has much larger energy scale

    反向成核能垒相对于 pinned collinear AFM reference state 测量，几乎整个参数范围为 23–24 J，显著高于已写入 skyrmion pair 的塌缩能垒：*"The reverse transition has a very different energy scale."*；*"It is approximately 23–24J over the whole parameter range, much larger than the collapse barrier of an existing skyrmion pair."*

    • Positive applied field weakly lowers reverse barrier for large islands

    对较大 pinned islands，正 applied field 增大时 reverse barrier 略微下降，但相对 23–24 J 的绝对值变化很小：*"The barrier decreases slightly with increasing positive applied field for the larger pinned islands, but the change is small compared with the absolute value of the barrier."*

    • Upper-layer single-skyrmion stability diagram is discrete, not interpolated

    Figure 4(b) 显示上层 l=2 单 skyrmion intermediate 关于 B 和 S 的稳定图；每个色块对应一个计算网格点，不做插值：*"Each colored cell represents one calculated grid point; no interpolation between grid points is used."*

    • Bound pair stable throughout displayed region

    束缚 skyrmion pair 在显示区域均满足 relaxation-based local-stability criterion：*"The bound skyrmion pair satisfies the relaxation-based local-stability criterion throughout the displayed region."*

    • Dark cells identify genuine two-stage paths

    深色 cells 表示上层单 skyrmion 也满足局域稳定判据：独立 nonlinear conjugate-gradient relaxation 后仍存在，MEP 包含 strict intermediate minimum，且相邻 images 能量深度超过 5×10⁻⁴ J：*"The darker cells mark parameters where the upper-layer single-skyrmion state also satisfies this criterion: the state remains after independent nonlinear conjugate-gradient relaxation, the optimized MEP contains a strict intermediate minimum, and the minimum is deeper than 5×10−4J relative to the neighboring images."*

    • Two-stage path has small seed-decay barrier but large completion barrier

    在这些 two-stage 参数中，单层 seed 衰减回 AFM 的 barrier Eₛₚ,2−E₁ₛₖ₌₀.022–0.282 J，远小于从 intermediate 完成 pair 的 barrier ΔE_comp≈11 J：*"the seed-decay barrier Esp,2−E1sk remains small, 0.022–0.282J, compared with barrier for completing the pair ΔEcomp≈11J."* 这意味着单层 seed 若仅靠热稳定性并不牢固，但一旦被辅助产生或维持，完成 SAF pair 需要跨越的第二步能垒远低于从 AFM 直接反向成核的 23–24 J 主能垒。

    • Table 1 defines saddle and completion metrics

    数值表中 Eₛₚ,1 是主高鞍点，Eₛₚ,2 是低鞍点，ΔE_comp=Eₛₚ,1−E₁ₛₖ 是从 intermediate 完成 pair 的能垒，Eₛₚ,2−E₁ₛₖ 是 intermediate 的竞争衰减能垒：*"Here Esp,1 is the main, higher saddle point, Esp,2 is the lower saddle, and ΔEcomp=Esp,1−E1sk is the barrier for completing the pair from intermediate minimum."*；*"The competing decay barrier of the intermediate is Esp,2−E1sk."*

    • Available Table 1 values confirm near-constant reverse barrier for S=100 and S=300

    表 1 显示 S=100, L=25.1 nm 时，ΔEₙᵤcl/J 随 B 从 −25 到 30 mT 分别为 24.013, 23.998, 23.988, 23.976, 23.962；同一尺寸的 ΔE_coll/J 仅 0.036 到 0.017。S=300, L=75.2 nm 时，B=−25 mT 有 ΔEₙᵤcl/J=23.681, ΔE_coll/J=3.173；B=0 mT 有 ΔEₙᵤcl/J=23.524, ΔE_coll/J=3.164。这些数值吻合：*"Table 1: Numerical summary of the calculated MEPs."*；*"Energy columns are in units of J relative to the pinned collinear reference state."*

    • Missing accepted intermediate marked by dash

    表 1 中 dash 表示最终 discrete path 上没有被接受的上层单 skyrmion minimum：*"A dash means that no accepted upper-layer single-skyrmion minimum is present on the final discrete path."* 例如 S=100 全部列出的 field 点均无 accepted upper-layer intermediate，这与小岛中路径 effectively single-stage 一致。

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持（Understanding & Nuance）

    1. 术语解析

    • Synthetic antiferromagnet（SAF）

    指由两个或多个 ferromagnetic layers 通过 nonmagnetic spacer 产生 antiferromagnetic RKKY coupling 的人工反铁磁结构。与 intrinsic antiferromagnet 不同，SAF 的每层仍是铁磁层，因此更易通过 layer-sensitive probes 探测与操控。语境中的关键优势是：低净磁矩、低 stray field、弱 skyrmion Hall effect，同时保持层可访问性。

    • Minimum energy path（MEP）

    指连接两个 local minima 的最低能量过渡路径，用于识别 saddle point 与 activation barrier。这里 MEP 不是真实动力学轨迹，而是静态能量景观中的最可能热激活路径。反向 nucleation path 与 collapse path 是同一条 MEP 的相反方向，但真实 current/laser-assisted writing 不必沿这条路径。

    • Pinned-boundary interior-collapse channel

    指边界自旋被固定为反铁磁参考态，只允许内部自旋弛豫的塌缩通道。这个设定模拟“嵌入无限 collinear AFM 背景中的内部塌缩事件”，而不是自由边界纳米岛。其微妙点在于：鞍点较局域，可能较可靠；skyrmion pair minimum 受边界惩罚明显，导致计算能垒带有边界依赖。

    • Layer-sequential collapse / nucleation

    指 SAF 双层 skyrmion 对不是同步消失或生成，而是一层先发生拓扑变化，另一层随后发生。该工作中塌缩方向是下层先消失，上层形成单 skyrmion intermediate；反向成核则是上层先出现，再生成下层 partner。

    • Relaxation-based local-stability criterion

    指不通过 Hessian 正定性判断稳定性，而是通过非线性共轭梯度弛豫后是否保持 stationary configuration、是否是 MEP 上 strict discrete minimum、是否与相邻 saddle 分离来判定 metastability。它比“肉眼看到能量小凹陷”严格，但弱于完整 HTST/Hessian 稳定性分析。

    2. 疑难查证

    • 为什么反向成核能垒远大于塌缩能垒？

    能垒定义的参考态不同。塌缩能垒是

    [

    Δ Ecₒₗₗ=Eₛₚ-Eₚₐᵢᵣ,

    ]

    反向成核能垒是

    [

    Δ Eₙᵤcₗ=Eₛₚ-EAFM.

    ]

    在 pinned-boundary 计算中，Eₚₐᵢᵣ > E_AFM，因此同一个主鞍点相对于 AFM reference 看起来很高，相对于 skyrmion pair minimum 看起来低得多。物理含义是：已写入的 skyrmion pair 是 metastable higher-energy state，容易热塌缩；从低能 AFM reference 自发涨落到 skyrmion pair 则需要爬到同一高鞍点，概率指数级小。

    • 为什么尺寸效应主要来自 skyrmion-pair minimum 而不是 saddle？

    主鞍点是局域塌缩事件，发生在岛内部；只要离边界足够远，边界对其能量影响小。skyrmion pair minimum 是较扩展纹理，尤其在小岛中占据较大面积，固定反铁磁边界会强行约束远场自旋弛豫，显著抬高其能量。于是 S=100 中 pair minimum 被抬到接近 saddle，能垒几乎消失；S=500 中 pair 可较充分弛豫，Eₚₐᵢᵣ 降低，Eₛₚ 仍近似不变，能垒变大。

    • 为什么逐层写入是合理策略？

    从 AFM 直接热成核 pair 需要约 23–24 J。但如果外部手段先在上层产生一个 skyrmion seed，路径可从 intermediate 出发，完成 pair 的能垒约 11 J，显著低于直接成核主能垒。尽管 seed 自身 decay barrier 很小（0.022–0.282 J），非平衡驱动可以持续提供或稳定 seed，使 interlayer exchange 帮助第二层成核。

    • 为什么没有 Hessian 仍可讨论 saddle 和 metastability？

    climbing-image NEB 可把路径最高点优化到 MEP 上的 stationary point；局部稳定性则通过独立弛豫和 discrete minimum 判据确认。但严格 HTST 需要 saddle 与 minimum 的 Hessian eigenvalues 来计算 prefactor 与确认所有稳定/不稳定方向。因此这里的“saddle”和“local minimum”是 MEP/relaxation 层面的操作性定义，不等价于完整谱分析。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联（Synthesis & Novelty）

    1. 创新性判断

    • 把 SAF skyrmion 的 retention 与 writability 明确分离

    近几年 SAF skyrmion 研究集中于稳定化、运动、Hall-effect suppression、实验成核和材料参数调控。该研究把“已写入 pair 的热保持”和“从 AFM reference 写入 pair”拆成两个能垒问题，揭示两者在同一 MEP 上却具有强烈非对称性。

    • 首次在 pinned-island 框架下分解尺寸依赖来源

    关键新意不是简单报告“尺寸越大能垒越高”，而是把 collapse barrier 写成 Eₛₚ−Eₚₐᵢᵣ 并指出：Eₛₚ 约 23–24 J，随 S 弱变；Eₚₐᵢᵣ 随 S 强变。这种分解避免误把能垒上升理解为 saddle 被抬高，实际主要来自 skyrmion-pair minimum 的 boundary penalty 减弱。

    • 将逐层塌缩与反向逐层成核放到同一条 MEP 上统一解释

    前人已显示 interlayer exchange 可导致非同步 collapse；这里进一步说明反向路径自然对应 upper-layer-first nucleation，再由 lower-layer partner 完成 pair。由此把动态 assisted writing 方案与静态能量景观联系起来。

    • 给出单层 skyrmion intermediate 的稳定区域图

    不是假定单层 intermediate 总存在，而是用 independent relaxations 与 MEP discrete minimum 判据构建 S–B stability map。这解决了一个关键细节：逐层路径何时是真正 two-stage，何时只是 effectively single-stage。

    • 为 assisted layer-sequential writing 提供能量景观依据

    反向直接成核约 23–24 J，completion barrier 约 11 J，seed-decay barrier 仅 0.022–0.282 J。这组能量关系说明：单纯热成核低效，但外部辅助先制造上层 seed 后，层间交换辅助完成 pair 更可行。这为 current/laser/voltage/local-injection 写入机制提供了明确的 saddle-level 解释。

    • 明确限定 reduced model 的适用边界

    模型不声称给出真实 multilayer 的一一对应寿命，而是把 anisotropy、magnetostatics、prefactors、edge routes 排除在外，专注 retained interactions 内的机制。这种限定提高了结论的可审查性：可信的是机制趋势和能量景观结构，非直接器件寿命预测。

    阅读原文 ↗
    原文链接页内定位
  17. 17
    多亚晶格钙钛矿反铁磁反常熔化#
    Inverse Melting of 3D Antiferromagnetic Order in Multi-sublattice Magnetic Perovskites#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 物理 / 凝聚态📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 Bangye Qin, Dmitry D. Khalyavin, Ran Liu, Kazunari Yamaura, Alexei A. Belik, Roger D. Johnson🔥 AI 75

    💡 亮点：升温可诱导三维反铁磁有序。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题常规反铁磁体通常是“低温3D有序、升温无序”，但 NaRMn₂Ti₄O₁₂（R=Dy, Sm）是否会出现相反路径：最低温时3D C-type反铁磁长程序被磁堆垛层错熔化成2D相关无序态，升温后反而恢复清晰3D长程反铁磁有序？
    创新方法用中子粉末衍射峰形作为“磁层错显微镜”，结合 Rietveld 精修与 200×200×2000 大超胞磁散射模拟，把 Dy 的非对称 100 宽峰解释为 c轴 Ising-like 磁堆垛层错，把 Sm 的宽赝非公度卫星峰解释为面内 canting 层错；Aha 点是：低温无序不是缺陷噪声，而是稀土–Mn f–d交换、A位Na/R随机分布和稀土单离子各向异性共同触发的 order-by-heating 机制。
    工作流程合成柱状有序四重钙钛矿 NaDyMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 与 NaSmMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ → 在 1.5–20 K 进行 ISIS WISH 中子粉末衍射 → 精修核结构、TiO₂杂质相和 k=(0,0,0) C-type Mn反铁磁结构 → 追踪 Tₙ 与 T* 附近磁峰从尖锐到展宽/卫星峰的变化 → 构建含 Mn–R 层的超胞并设置层错概率 p、canting角和最小畴尺寸 → 输出温度依赖的3D有序分量、2D层错无序分量和逆熔化相变图像。
    关键结果两种材料在 Tₙ≈10–12 K 以下先形成 k=(0,0,0) 的3D C-type Mn²⁺反铁磁长程序，但在更低温 T*≈5–6 K 以下发生逆熔化。Dy 样品 1.5 K 的 100 磁峰强烈非对称展宽，核峰仍尖锐，模拟得到 Ising-like 磁层错概率最高约25%，说明 c轴磁相关被破坏为2D层状相关。Sm 样品保留尖锐公度 C-type峰，同时出现 k=(0,0,0.385) 的宽赝非公度卫星峰，15°面内自旋倾斜与约57%层错概率可重现实验峰形。
    应用价值该研究建立了一种不同于自旋玻璃、拓扑相或几何阻挫重入相的磁相变范式：通过混合阳离子无序、多磁子晶格竞争交换和稀土各向异性，可以设计“低温无序、升温有序”的反铁磁材料；为调控钙钛矿磁有序维度、层错相关长度和温度驱动磁功能提供材料设计路线。

    第一部分：核心概览 (Overview)

    该研究在柱状有序四重钙钛矿 NaRMn₂Ti₄O₁₂（R = Dy, Sm） 中发现反常磁相变：低温基态不是常规 3D 长程反铁磁有序，而是由密集磁堆垛层错导致的 2D 相关无序态；升温后反而形成清晰的 3D C-type 反铁磁长程序，再于 Tₙ ≈ 10–12 K 转入顺磁态。该结果把 inverse melting / order-by-heating 扩展到多磁子晶格钙钛矿反铁磁体，突出 A 位化学无序、稀土–Mn f–d 相互作用、单离子各向异性 的耦合机制。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Inverse Melting of 3D Antiferromagnetic Order in Multi-sublattice Magnetic Perovskites》（None，）

    背景

    常规反铁磁体通常在低温形成 3D 长程有序基态，升温后有序被热涨落破坏并进入顺磁态。Inverse melting 则表现为冷却时有序相失稳、低温重新出现更无序状态。该现象在合金、超导涡旋物质、聚合物、超分子体系中已有报道，但在 关联磁性材料 中罕见。

    方法

    采用 中子粉末衍射（NPD） 研究 NaDyMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 与 NaSmMn₂Ti₄O₁₂。样品质量分别约 1.88 g 与 2.20 g，装入 3 mm 钒罐，在 1.5–20 K 测量；使用 ISIS WISH 飞行时间衍射仪，Rietveld 精修采用 FullProf，探测器 bank 平均 2θ = 58° 与 154°。

    结果

    两种材料在 Tₙ 以下 出现 k = (0,0,0) 的 C-type Mn²⁺ 反铁磁有序；但在更低温 T* ≈ 5–6 K 以下发生反常失稳。Dy 样品在 1.5 K 出现 100 磁峰强烈非对称展宽，对应 Ising-like 层错与 2D 磁相关；Sm 样品保留尖锐 C-type 峰，同时出现 k = (0,0,0.385) 的宽赝非公度卫星峰，对应面内自旋分量的层错调制。

    讨论

    无序基态并非仪器或结构因素导致，因为核峰保持尖锐。稀土离子不直接贡献清晰衍射强度，但通过 f–d exchange 改变 Mn 层间耦合。Dy³⁺ 的强 Ising 各向异性 诱发 Ising-like 堆垛层错；Sm³⁺ 的 easy-plane 各向异性 降低层错成核能垒，使层错概率更高。

    局限

    数据以粉末平均 NPD 为主，Sm 体系中的宽峰在 Rietveld 中难以区分 赝非公度层错态 与 短程相关非公度相；稀土随机分布导致稀土磁矩本身不易由衍射直接解析。补充材料中的均场与模拟支撑机制，但缺少单晶动量空间分辨、非弹性谱、局域探针等进一步验证。

    结论

    NaDyMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 与 NaSmMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 展现 3D 反铁磁长程序的逆熔化：低温无序、升温有序、再升温顺磁。该机制由 多磁子晶格、A 位内禀化学无序、竞争交换相互作用、稀土单离子各向异性 共同控制，构成区别于自旋玻璃、拓扑效应、几何阻挫重入相的磁相变范式。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析 (Section-by-Section Condensing)

    Title: Inverse Melting of 3D Antiferromagnetic Order in Multi-sublattice Magnetic Perovskites

    • Core phenomenon

    标题直接界定核心物理对象为 3D antiferromagnetic order 的 inverse melting，材料平台为 multi-sublattice magnetic perovskites。研究重点不是普通 Néel 转变，而是 三维反铁磁长程序在低温反而熔化为更无序磁态。标题中的 *"Inverse Melting of 3D Antiferromagnetic Order"* 明确指向反常热力学路径：升温形成有序、降温破坏有序。

    • Material class

    multi-sublattice magnetic perovskites 指含多个磁性子晶格的钙钛矿体系，本研究具体落在 columnar-ordered quadruple perovskites NaRMn₂Ti₄O₁₂，其中 Mn 子晶格、稀土 R 子晶格、Na/R 随机 A 位共同构成复杂磁耦合网络。标题中的 *"Multi-sublattice Magnetic Perovskites"* 强调该现象不是孤立单子晶格磁体行为，而依赖多子晶格耦合。

    ---

    Abstract

    • Conventional antiferromagnetic paradigm is inverted

    常规反铁磁体的升温路径是 3D 长程有序基态 → 临界区低维相关 → 顺磁无序态；该研究展示完全相反的关键中间过程：低温基态缺乏长程有序，升温后先形成 3D 长程序。摘要开头给出对照：*"In conventional antiferromagnets a long-range ordered 3D ground state transitions to a disordered paramagnetic state on warming, often via lower dimensional spin correlations within the critical regime."* 随后的核心反转为 *"Here we demonstrate a striking departure from this paradigm."*

    • Ground state contains only 2D spin correlations

    NaRR Mn₂Ti₄O₁₂（RR = Dy, Sm） 的磁基态不是 3D 有序，而是只有 2D spin correlations。关键证据来自中子粉末衍射分析：*"Through analysis of neutron powder diffraction data, we show that the magnetic ground state of columnar-ordered quadruple perovskites, Na R R Mn2Ti4O12 (R R = Dy, Sm), lacks long-range order, hosting only 2D spin correlations."* 这里的 lacks long-range order 是判断基态无序的核心表述。

    • Heating creates 3D long-range antiferromagnetic order

    升温不是破坏有序，而是在进入顺磁态前先诱导 3D long-range ordered antiferromagnetic structure。摘要中直接表述：*"On warming, this disordered state transitions into a 3D long-range ordered antiferromagnetic structure prior to the phase transition to the paramagnetic state."* 这一点构成 order-by-heating 的实验证据链。

    • Mechanism couples chemical disorder and competing exchange

    反常相变机制来自 A-site chemical disorder 与 rare earth–Mn sub-lattice competing exchange interactions 的耦合。摘要中的机制句为：*"Our results establish an unconventional order-by-heating mechanism in which intrinsic A-site chemical disorder is coupled to competing exchange interactions between the rare earth and Mn sub-lattices, leading to a novel type of magnetic phase transition."* 这里的 intrinsic 表明无序不是外加缺陷，而是晶体化学本身的一部分。

    ---

    Main text

    • Inverse melting is thermodynamically allowed but rare in correlated magnets

    Inverse melting 指有序相在冷却时失稳，低温重新出现更无序相。该现象需要特殊自由能结构，例如淬火无序、随机场或竞争相互作用，使有序相本身携带有效熵。原文定义为：*"Inverse melting refers to the unusual phenomenon by which an ordered phase becomes destabilized upon cooling and a more disordered state re-emerges at lower temperature."* 热力学条件为：*"Such behavior is thermodynamically allowed when the free-energy landscape is reshaped by quenched disorder, random-field effects, or competing interactions, such that entropy is effectively carried by the ordered phase itself."*

    已报道体系包括 chemically disordered alloys、metallic systems、type-II superconductors vortex matter、polymeric materials、supramolecular assemblies、electronic liquid crystals，但在磁性关联材料中稀少：*"it remains relatively rare in correlated magnetic materials."*

    • Prior magnetic re-entrance differs from the present mechanism

    近年 pyrochlore antiferromagnets 中已有场–温相图重入现象，钙钛矿中也出现过 reentrant spin-glasses 和 multi-q magnetic states，但当前目标是另一类重入磁行为：内禀化学无序和竞争磁相互作用导致 3D 反铁磁有序逆熔化。原文对比为：*"Recent studies of geometric frustration in pyrochlore antiferromagnets have demonstrated multiple instances of re-entrance in their field–temperature phase diagrams, while perovskites have been shown to host reentrant spin-glasses and multi-q magnetic states."* 新目标为：*"a distinct form of re-entrant magnetic behaviour, in which intrinsic chemical disorder and competing magnetic interactions can lead to inverse melting of 3D antiferromagnetic order into a disordered ground state."*

    • Columnar quadruple perovskites provide a multi-sublattice platform

    AA′₃B₄O₁₂ 与柱状变体 A₂A′A″B₄O₁₂ 具有耦合结构畸变和多个磁性子晶格，天然产生竞争交换与复杂磁结构。原文概括为：*"Quadruple perovskites AA′3B4O12 and their columnar variants A2A′A′′B4O12 are known to host coupled structural distortions and multiple magnetic sublattices, giving rise to competing exchange interactions and complex magnetostructural phenomena."*

    结构上，A 位三阳离子排序由四方 a⁺a⁺c⁻ 八面体倾斜稳定：*"A2A′A′′B4O12 perovskites have a unique triple-cation A-site ordering, stabilised by a tetragonal a+a+c− octahedral tilt pattern."*

    • NaRMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ contains intrinsic A-site randomness and two Mn coordinations

    NaRMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 中 A = Na₀.₅R₀.₅, A′ = Mn, A″ = Mn, B = Ti。A 位 Na/R 随机占位，Mn 同时处于 square-planar MnO₄ 与 tetrahedral MnO₄ 环境。原文给出化学占位：*"such as in Na R R Mn2Ti4O12, where A = Na0.5R0.5, A′ = Mn, A′′ = Mn, and B = Ti."*

    晶体结构具有沿 c 轴 延伸的 AO₁₂ 柱，以及交错的 A′O₄ square-planar 与 A″O₄ tetrahedral 柱：*"10 coordinate AO12 cages form two columns per unit cell that run parallel to the c-axis"*；*"staggered columns of alternating square-planar A′O4 and tetrahedral A′′O4 units are arranged between the AO12 columns in a checkerboard pattern when viewed down c."*

    • Earlier work established C-type Mn order and unexplained low-temperature anomaly

    既有研究显示 NaRMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 在 Tₙ ≈ 8–13 K 以下形成 Mn²⁺ C-type antiferromagnetic order，传播矢量 k = (0,0,0)；部分 R，尤其 Dy、Sm、Eu，在 T* ≈ 6 K 还有第二热力学异常。原文数值为：*"develop C-type antiferromagnetic order of the A′A′′ Mn2+ magnetic sublattice with k = (0,0,0) immediately below TN ∼ 8–13 K"*；低温异常为：*"a second, lower–temperature thermodynamic anomaly indicative of a low temperature phase transition at T∗ ∼ 6 K appears only for selected R (notably Dy, Sm, and Eu)."*

    Dy 成员已知 Tₙ = 12 K、T* = 6 K，C-type 磁矩沿 c 轴，但低温磁峰变宽、基态无序尚未解释：*"Neutron powder diffraction experiments performed on the Dy member established C-type magnetic order with moments ∥ c below TN = 12 K, and showed a marked broadening of magnetic Bragg peaks on further cooling below T∗ = 6 K, indicative of a disordered ground state that is yet to be understood."*

    Sm 成员有 Tₙ = 10.5 K、T* = 5 K，但磁结构演化未知：*"the Sm member was found to exhibit two thermodynamic anomalies at TN = 10.5 K and T∗ = 5 K, but little is known about the evolution of the magnetic structure."*

    • Experimental design uses neutron powder diffraction over 1.5–20 K

    多晶样品按高压方案合成；NPD 在 ISIS WISH 上完成。Dy 样品约 1.88 g，Sm 样品约 2.20 g，装入 3 mm diameter vanadium cans，温区 1.5–20 K。原文实验细节为：*"For the R = Dy and Sm compositions, approximately 1.88 g and 2.20 g of sample, respectively, was loaded into cylindrical 3 mm diameter vanadium cans and measured between 1.5 and 20 K."*

    精修采用 FullProf，数据来自平均 2θ = 58° 和 154° 探测器 bank：*"Rietveld refinements of the nuclear and magnetic structures were performed using the fullprof suite against data collected in detector banks centred at average 2θ values of 58° and 154°."*

    • Nuclear structures refine well, with minor impurity and disorder

    NaDyMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 与 NaSmMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 的 P4₂/nmc 晶体结构在 20 K 与 14 K 数据下均获得优良拟合，结构参数与文献一致。原文为：*"Refinement of the NaDyMn2Ti4O12 and NaSmMn2Ti4O12 P42/nmc crystal structures against neutron powder diffraction data measured at 20 and 14 K, respectively, gave an excellent fit."*

    两个样品均有 TiO₂ impurity phase 2–3 wt%：*"A number of weak reflections could be modeled by a minor TiO2 impurity phase (2–3 wt%) present in both samples."*

    两类结构无序被纳入模型：R/Na 随机占 A 位，square-planar Mn 随机偏离配位平面上下两侧。原文为：*"The refined structural models encompassed two disordered elements; 1) the R/Na ions randomly occupy the A-site, and 2) the square-planar coordinated Mn cation is randomly displaced above or below the coordination plane."*

    Sm 样品还存在少量 Sm 占 Mn2 位，但 Sm:Na 比偏离 1:1 可能是中子吸收与 Sm 散射长度不确定造成的精修伪影：*"in NaSmMn2Ti4O12 a small occupation of Sm at the Mn2 site was found"*；*"This is likely an artefact in the neutron data refinement due to strong absorption compounded by the fact that the Sm scattering length is not well known."*

    • Both compounds form intermediate C-type antiferromagnetic order below TN

    在 Tₙ 以下，空间群禁戒位置出现新 Bragg 强度，可用 k = (0,0,0) 指数化，表示长程反铁磁序出现。原文为：*"Upon cooling both materials below TN, new Bragg intensities emerge ... at space group forbidden positions that index with propagation k = (0,0,0), signaling the onset of long-range antiferromagnetic order."*

    磁结构为 C-type：ab 面内 Mn²⁺ 层反铁磁耦合，沿 c 轴铁磁堆垛；Mn²⁺ 同时位于 square-planar 与 tetrahedral 位点。原文为：*"The magnetic diffraction intensities could be well accounted for by a C-type magnetic structure that incorporates Mn2+ moments on both the square-planar and tetrahedral sites."* 结构特征为：*"antiferromagnetically coupled Mn2+ layers in the ab plane are stacked ferromagnetically along c."*

    (100) 磁峰出现且 (001) 缺失唯一确定有序矩沿 tetragonal c axis：*"the appearance of magnetic intensity at (100), together with the absence of (001), uniquely determines the ordered moment direction along the tetragonal c axis."*

    • Dy ground state shows asymmetric broadening and loss of c-axis correlations

    在 T* ≈ 6 K 以下，NaDyMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 的 100 磁峰强烈非对称展宽；核峰保持尖锐，排除仪器或结构起源。原文为：*"below T∗ ∼ 6 K the 100 peak from NaDyMn2Ti4O12 develops a severe asymmetric broadening on cooling into the ground state"*；排除项为：*"Nuclear reflections remain sharp, excluding instrumental or structural origins."*

    展宽表明 c 轴磁相关长度随温度降低而减小，C-type 反铁磁长程序在最低温失稳为层错化层状态。原文解释为：*"The broad, asymmetric peak reflects a temperature-dependent reduction in the magnetic correlations along the c axis, indicating that the antiferromagnetic C-type order becomes destabilized into a faulted layered state at the lowest temperatures."*

    对 4 K、2 K、1.5 K 数据继续精修 C-type 模型，仅能拟合大部分谱形，不能解释展宽磁强度：*"we refined the above magnetic structure model against data measured at 4, 2 and 1.5 K"*；*"showing excellent agreement throughout most of the pattern, but failing to account for the broadened magnetic intensity, as expected."*

    • Sm ground state retains commensurate order but adds broad pseudo-incommensurate scattering

    NaSmMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 在 T* 以下仍保留尖锐分辨率受限的 C-type 反铁磁峰，同时出现宽的非公度卫星磁强度。原文为：*"On cooling below T∗, the sharp resolution–limited antiferromagnetic intensities persist, while additional broad magnetic intensities at incommensurate satellite positions emerge."*

    这些卫星峰可由 k = (0,0,0.385) 指数化：*"These incommensurate intensities index with wavevector k = (0,0,0.385)."*

    1.5 K 精修采用 C-type moments ∥ c 加 incommensurate helix moments ⟂ c 的锥形结构模型：*"A magnetic structure model including the C–type magnetic structure with moments ∥ c, augmented by an incommensurate helix with moments ⟂ c (a conical structure), was refined against NPD data measured at 1.5 K."*

    非公度分量使用严重展宽峰形函数，指向后续解释的 pseudo-incommensurate modulation：*"A severely broadened peak profile function was used for the incommensurate component, which points towards a pseudo-incommensurate modulation of the C-type magnetic structure discussed later."*

    • Both compounds share inverse melting but differ by rare-earth ion

    两种材料具有相同四方晶体框架和无序基态，且无序基态均由中间 3D C-type antiferromagnetic structure 的逆熔化到达。原文总结为：*"both NaSmMn2Ti4O12 and NaDyMn2Ti4O12 share the same tetragonal crystallographic framework and a disordered ground state, reached by inverse melting of an intermediate 3D ordered C–type antiferromagnetic structure."*

    差异来自稀土离子选择：*"the exact nature of the disordered ground state differs between these two materials, indicating that the choice of rare-earth ion is key."*

    非磁性或弱 f–d 参照 NaYMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 具有常规序参量行为，凸显 f–d interactions 的必要性：*"in NaYMn2Ti4O12 the C-type Mn ordered moment exhibits a conventional order-parameter behavior at all temperatures below TN, highlighting the essential role of f–d interactions in this material system."*

    • Large-supercell simulations model magnetic stacking faults

    为理解基态磁散射，使用最小磁结构模型模拟 100 附近的弹性粉末平均中子散射。超胞尺寸为 200 × 200 × 2000，每个晶胞含两个沿 c 轴堆垛的 Mn–R layers。原文为：*"We construct a 200 × 200 × 2000 crystallographic supercell, in which each unit cell consists of two Mn–R layers stacked along the crystallographic c axis."*

    每层 Mn²⁺ 子晶格含两个不等价位点：square-planar S-Mn 与 tetrahedral T-Mn；二者相差 [0.5, 0.5, 0] 平移并反铁磁对齐。原文为：*"Within each layer, the Mn2+ sublattice comprises two crystallographically inequivalent sites associated with square-planar (S-Mn) and tetrahedral (T-Mn) coordinations."* 以及 *"These two Mn sublattices are displaced by a [0.5,0.5,0] translation and are antiferromagnetically aligned."*

    无序通过层依赖的磁矩分量翻转引入，发生概率为 p，导致沿 c 轴的铁磁堆垛出现层错，但每个层内部仍相干：*"Magnetic disorder is then introduced as a layer-dependent flip in magnetic moment components that occurs with probability, p."*；*"the ferromagnetic stacking sequence along c incurs faults, while each individual layer remains internally coherent."*

    • Dy is captured by an Ising-like stacking-fault model

    Dy 模拟中所有磁矩约束为沿 c 轴平行/反平行，并施加最小 2-layer domain size。原文为：*"For NaDyMn2Ti4O12, all magnetic moments were constrained to be aligned (anti)parallel to the c-axis, and a minimum 2-layer domain size was imposed."*

    Ising-like 堆垛层错模型很好重现实验，层错概率在基态最大为 25%，升温接近 T* 时降为 0：*"This Ising-like magnetic stacking fault model well reproduces the experimental data, with the probability of a fault being maximal (25%) in the ground state and decreasing to zero on warming as T∗ is approached."*

    模拟得到的 100 integrated intensity 平方根按 6 K 精修有序矩标定，总磁矩随温度单调演化，而低温无序态在 T* 以下出现：*"The square root of the simulated 100 integrated intensity is plotted in Fig. 4a, having been scaled to the refined ordered moment at 6 K."*；*"The thermal evolution of the total moment is monotonic, as expected of a conventional order parameter, while the onset of a disordered ground state below T∗ is clearly seen."*

    • Sm is captured by in-plane canting faults and pseudo-incommensurability

    Sm 基态采用 Mn spin canting 模型，层错只发生在 in-plane component，而沿 c 轴平行/反平行分量保持长程相关。原文为：*"instead of Ising-like faults we introduce a model of Mn spin canting with stacking faults occurring in the in-plane component only."* 以及 *"well correlated order of the Mn moment components (anti)parallel to c is maintained."*

    1.5 K 时拟合良好需要 15° canting angle，基态层错概率接近 57%：*"good agreement with the data is achieved for a canting angle of 15° at 1.5 K, with a fault probability approaching 57% in the ground state."*

    该状态不是常规长程非公度相，而是最小畴大小约束下的 pseudo-incommensurate non-stochastic faulting pattern，大 p 值时强度偏离公度位置。原文区别为：*"Unlike a conventional incommensurate phase, which is characterized by a well-defined incommensurate propagation vector and long-range phase coherence, the present case is characterized by a pseudo-incommensurate non-stochastic faulting pattern due to the minimum domain size."*

    Rietveld 层面该情景与短程相关非公度相难以区分：*"in Rietveld refinement, this scenario is indistinguishable from a poorly correlated incommensurate phase with characteristically broad diffraction peaks."*

    • Rare-earth moments influence Mn order indirectly through f–d exchange

    稀土磁矩不直接贡献中子衍射强度，因为 R 与 Na 在晶体结构中随机分布；其作用通过 T* 以下 Mn 磁结构层错表现出来。原文为：*"the rare-earth magnetic moments do not contribute to the neutron diffraction intensities (R and Na are randomly distributed throughout the crystal structure), but their effects are witnessed through faults in the Mn magnetic structure that develop below T∗."*

    T* 对应 f–d exchange energy 的特征温度：*"a temperature characteristic of the f-d exchange energy."*

    • Dy³⁺ Ising anisotropy causes Ising-like magnetic stacking faults

    Dy³⁺ 通常具有强 Ising anisotropy 的 Kramers 双重态。Mn 子晶格长程有序后产生有限交换场，劈裂 Dy³⁺ Kramers 双重态，并随冷却增强，相当于“打开”局域 Dy Ising 磁矩。原文为：*"Dy3+ ions typically adopt a ground state Kramers doublet with strong Ising anisotropy."*；*"the onset of long-range magnetic order of the Mn sublattice splits the Dy3+ Kramers doublet via a finite exchange field that grows on cooling, effectively ‘switching-on’ large local, Dy3+ Ising moments distributed throughout the crystal."*

    Dy-rich 区域中竞争 Dy–Dy 相互作用产生强交换场，破坏理想 C-type Mn 结构的层间铁磁对齐，形成 Ising-like 堆垛层错：*"in Dy-rich regions, competing Dy–Dy interactions generate a sufficiently strong exchange field to destabilize the ideal interlayer ferromagnetic alignment of the C-type Mn magnetic structure, leading to Ising-like magnetic stacking faults."*

    • Sm³⁺ easy-plane anisotropy lowers the fault nucleation barrier

    Sm 基态同样由 f–d interactions 触发，但各向异性为 easy plane，不同于 Dy 的 Ising 极限。原文为：*"the disordered magnetic ground state in NaSmMn2Ti4O12 can occurs due to f-d interactions, but in the presence of easy plane magnetic anisotropy of Sm3+, as opposed to Ising anisotropy of Dy3+."*

    补充材料均场计算显示，层错能量代价随自旋偏离 Ising 极限的 canting angle 增大而单调降低：*"Mean-field calculations given in the Supplemental Material show that the energetic cost of a fault decreases monotonically as the spin canting angle increases away from the Ising limit."*

    非 Ising 各向异性降低层错成核能垒，解释 Sm 中更高的 57% 层错概率：*"non-Ising anisotropy permits a lower energetic barrier for fault nucleation, providing a natural mechanism for the increased probability of faulting observed in the Sm-based compound."*

    • Final conclusion establishes order-by-heating in mixed-cation perovskites

    NaRMn₂Ti₄O₁₂（R = Dy, Sm） 的核心结论是多磁子晶格与内禀化学无序相互作用导致 3D long range antiferromagnetic order 的逆熔化，并可由稀土单离子各向异性调谐。原文总结为：*"columnar-ordered quadruple perovskites Na R R Mn2Ti4O12 (R = Dy, Sm) host a remarkable inverse melting of 3D long range antiferromagnetic order due to the interplay between multiple magnetic sublattices and intrinsic chemical disorder, tunable by choice of rare-earth single-ion anisotropy."*

    该发现区别于拓扑效应或自旋玻璃，改变了对共线反铁磁体磁相变的理解：*"This discovery marks a paradigm shift in our understanding of magnetic phase transitions in collinear antiferromagnets that is distinct from effects of topology or spin glass behaviour."*

    order-by-heating 机制可能广泛适用于混合阳离子钙钛矿型材料：*"The order-by-heating mechanism, through which low dimensional correlations transition into long-range 3D order on heating, is expected to be relevant across a wide range of mixed-cation perovskite-type materials, where multiple magnetic sublattices and competing interactions coexist."*

[2025]。正文概括为：*"Inverse melting has been observed in a limited number of systems, including chemically disordered alloys and metallic systems, vortex matter in type-II superconductors, polymeric materials, supramolecular assemblies, and electronic liquid crystals."*

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持 (Understanding & Nuance)

    1. 术语解析

    • Inverse melting

    字面是“逆熔化”，但在凝聚态语境中并不限于固液相变，而是指 低温更无序、高温反而更有序 的反常相序。关键微妙点在于“melting”描述的是 有序度降低，不是材料真的熔化。原文定义：*"an ordered phase becomes destabilized upon cooling and a more disordered state re-emerges at lower temperature."*

    • Order-by-heating

    与常见 order-by-disorder 接近但不完全相同。这里不是量子/热涨落从简并态中选择有序态，而是 升温使低维/层错无序态恢复 3D 长程有序。语境中的含义是：低温 f–d 交换和稀土各向异性诱导层错；升温削弱这些局域交换场后，Mn 子晶格恢复 C-type 有序。

    • Resolution-limited

    指峰宽受仪器分辨率限制，样品本征相关长度足够长，无法从峰宽看出有限相关长度。Sm 在 T* 以上和中间相中的 C-type 磁峰为 resolution-limited，意味着 3D 长程有序。相反，宽峰表示短程相关或层错相关。

    • Pseudo-incommensurate

    “赝非公度”并不等于真正非公度长程螺旋相。真正非公度相应具有明确传播矢量与长程相位相干；这里的宽峰可被 k = (0,0,0.385) 指数化，但模拟认为来源于非随机层错和最小畴大小导致的强度偏移。核心区别是 缺少 long-range phase coherence。

    • Stacking fault

    在这里不是晶体结构层错，而是 磁堆垛层错：每个 ab 层内部仍保持相干 C-type 排列，但沿 c 轴的层间铁磁堆垛序列发生翻转或面内分量错位。Dy 中层错发生在 Ising-like c 轴分量；Sm 中主要发生在面内 canting 分量。

    2. 疑难查证

    • 为什么低温反而更无序？

    普通直觉认为降温会降低热涨落，因此磁有序更稳定。但该体系低温时会“打开”稀土磁性自由度：Mn 子晶格先在 Tₙ 附近形成 C-type 有序，Mn 的交换场进一步劈裂 Dy³⁺ 或 Sm³⁺ 的低能态，使稀土局域磁矩逐渐增强。由于 Na/R 在 A 位随机分布，稀土磁矩不是周期排列，而是在空间中随机出现；这些局域稀土矩通过 f–d exchange 给 Mn 层施加随机且各向异性的交换场。温度越低，稀土矩越有效，局域竞争越强，Mn 层间理想铁磁堆垛越容易被破坏。因此，低温不是简单“更安静”，而是激活了一个无序的竞争耦合网络。

    • 为什么 Dy 与 Sm 的无序态不同？

    Dy³⁺ 具有强 Ising anisotropy，局域交换场倾向于把 Mn 磁矩沿 c 轴翻转，导致类似 Ising 变量的层错；所以 Dy 的 100 峰表现为强烈非对称展宽，对应 c 轴相关长度降低。Sm³⁺ 更偏 easy-plane anisotropy，允许 Mn 自旋产生面内 canting；层错主要作用于面内分量，同时 c 轴 C-type 分量仍保持尖锐长程峰。因此 Sm 同时出现尖锐公度峰和宽的赝非公度卫星峰。

    • 为什么说不是自旋玻璃？

    自旋玻璃通常表现为随机冻结、无明确长程有序，并常需要 AC 磁化率频率依赖、历史效应等证据。这里的中间温区具有清晰 resolution-limited C-type Bragg peaks，低温无序也不是完全随机，而是有层内相干、层间层错的低维相关态。机制来自 多子晶格 f–d exchange + A 位化学无序 + 单离子各向异性，不是传统自旋玻璃的随机冻结范式。

    • 为什么粉末衍射仍能区分 2D 层错与 3D 有序？

    3D 长程有序给出尖锐 Bragg 峰；沿某一方向相关长度降低会导致特定磁峰展宽、非对称化，粉末平均后仍保留特征峰形。Dy 的 100 峰展宽而核峰尖锐，说明不是晶格结构或仪器问题。Sm 的附加宽卫星峰说明存在短程调制或层错调制分量。大超胞粉末平均模拟进一步把这些峰形与层错概率 p = 25%（Dy 基态）、p ≈ 57%（Sm 基态） 联系起来。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联 (Synthesis & Novelty)

    1. 创新性判断

    • 把 inverse melting 明确推进到 3D 共线反铁磁长程序

    过去 2–5 年内，inverse melting 与重入行为更多出现在 超导涡旋物质、电子液晶、几何阻挫磁体、重入自旋玻璃、多-q 磁态 等场景。该研究的独特性在于：被逆熔化的对象是一个相对常规、可由 k = (0,0,0) 描述的 C-type collinear antiferromagnetic order，不是拓扑相、玻璃冻结或外场诱导相图中的重入区。

    • 解决了 NaDyMn₂Ti₄O₁₂ 低温磁峰展宽的未解问题

    既有研究已发现 Dy 样品在 T* = 6 K 以下磁 Bragg 峰显著展宽，但基态性质未明。该研究把展宽解释为 2D-correlated Ising-like magnetic state 与 dense magnetic stacking faults，并通过 200 × 200 × 2000 超胞模拟和 25% 基态层错概率 给出定量峰形解释。

    • 首次给出 Sm 成员低温磁结构演化图像

    Sm 样品此前仅知有 Tₙ = 10.5 K 与 T* = 5 K 两个热异常，磁结构演化信息不足。该研究发现 Sm 在低温保留公度 C-type 分量，同时发展 k = (0,0,0.385) 的宽赝非公度分量，并用 15° canting angle 与 p ≈ 57% 层错概率解释其峰形。

    • 建立“稀土单离子各向异性可调控无序基态类型”的机制

    Dy 与 Sm 的比较显示，同一结构框架和同类 Mn C-type 中间相可因稀土离子不同而进入不同无序基态。Dy³⁺ 的 Ising anisotropy 诱导 c 轴 Ising-like 层错；Sm³⁺ 的 easy-plane anisotropy 允许面内 canting 层错并降低层错成核能垒。这一机制比单纯“化学无序导致展宽”更具体，连接了 f–d exchange energy、Kramers doublet splitting、local exchange fields、fault nucleation barrier。

    • 提出混合阳离子钙钛矿中的普适 order-by-heating 路线

    该发现提示：含 A 位随机占位、多磁子晶格、竞争交换、稀土各向异性 的钙钛矿材料，可能普遍存在低温低维相关态升温转化为 3D 长程序的相变。相对于过去集中在几何阻挫或外场相图重入的研究，该工作给出一种基于 内禀化学无序 + 多子晶格交换竞争 的材料设计原则。
